et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	and if there is pain outside, as we have said in the case of liver abscess.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work there is fear or the patient dies now, or a fistula develops which cannot be healed.
de la mice	Of the mouse.
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the illness of a mouse according to what we have said in the section on treatments and it does not improve, then there are three methods of cautery which are all beneficial.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	Of which one method is to make three or four cauteries in a line following the length of the arm, according to the shape of the liver abscess cautery that we mentioned earlier;
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	And do not rush your hand with every cautery, let the patient rest often on their back.
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	And another method of cautery is to heat the cauterizing iron with two handles, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder.
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	Lift the heart which is on the right side of the chest, where the patient's wound faces left, and let the elevation by which you lift the heart be according to its length along the body, and the cautery should be made according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	After inserting the two heated handles until they pierce through to the other side of the heart, then pull out the cautery iron forcefully, and thus there will be four of them.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you see fit, cauterize with a three-nered cautery.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when it has removed putrefaction over a long time, and this is better than other treatments mentioned before.
de ydropisie	From dropsy
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterization is not suitable for dropsy, except in the case of the method known as 'ascites'.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you treat it according to the methods we have mentioned in divisions, and your treatment does not benefit, then it is necessary for you to make four cauterizations around the lump, one on the stomach, one on the liver, one on the spleen, two behind the back on the spine, and one towards the breast.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cauterizations be close to the base of the heart.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	Afterwards, leave the cautery open to drain pus over a long time, and do not neglect the treatment of the patient after the cauterization.
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and healing would hasten, and the two intentions would be combined with God's help.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The form of the cautery for the belly is the clavicle, which we have shown before.
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	And that for the back should be olive-shaped, according to what was previously mentioned here.
de l’enfleure des piez	The swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in someone who is dropsical, and they are full of yellow water, it is necessary that you cauterize on the back of the foot between the little finger and ring finger.
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	And lift your hand with the cautery without turning it.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, lest you burst the yellow water; let the cautery be according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	Afterwards, make two cauterizations on each leg at the tip of the small toe.
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	And let the long cauterizations be one below the knee in front and the other behind, in the middle of the leg.
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	And leave the caustic applications for a long time without treatment, until it heals.
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	After treating other ailments that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	From the residence
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When an abdominal ailment arises from cold and moisture, such that the retaining and digestive faculties which are in the stomach and intestine become weakened, and cannot be cured by ordinary remedies;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	And if you see the patient in great suffering and with strong constitution, then make a large cauterization on the stomach according to what has been discussed previously regarding gastric cautery, using the circular cautery iron.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	And four small cauterizations around the navel with each one slightly larger than the previous one, and two on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you observe abundant moisture and the patient suffering, perform a cautery on the wrist, one cautery above each elbow, and two small cauteries on the stomach near the large one, for the treatment is beneficial when there is good assistance.
de la cure des emorroydes	For the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When hemorrhoids are present in the fundament, whether one or more, and they are ancient, consisting of large cold, moist, corrupted humors, and are treated as we have described above, but to no avail, then perform cauterizations.
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	Above the spine of the back, where it is entirely outside [of its normal position], first perform one cautery and then another in a triangular pattern.
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	And if you believe their stomach is cooled and the meat not cooked, and one sees their face swell, then on the face perform a large cautery over the stomach as described before, another on the liver, and yet another on the spleen with each cautery being performed in turn.
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	Leave the cautery open for an extended period of time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After treatment, let the wound heal completely.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	Of fleshiness which is named 'thelul'
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you treat a wound with a hot iron, heat up the cauterizing tool like a razor, and then place it fully ignited on top of the wounded area.
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	And leave your hand there until the cauterizing tool reaches the edge of the wound, causing blood to flow out.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	Do this twice, and if there is a lot of flesh, cauterize each part as we have said.
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	After the treatment with beneficial ointments, let it heal until it is completely cured.
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	And if you use a larger cauterizing tool on the wound, it will provide greater relief.
de plaie mal curee	of poorly treated wound
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure suturing nor incision, which we shall relate in its place, such a sickness comes that can only be healed through cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When any person develops a fistula and it is filled with pus and putrefied moisture, you should first try a subtle treatment, and make sure that you know all about the treatment's effect.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	Afterwards, heat up the cauterizing tool resembling a razor, and push it into the fistula according to how much has entered, and repeat the cauterization as many times as needed until all corrupted flesh is burned away once or twice or three times depending on how severe the injury is.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	And beware of burning the nerves which are sensitive, and of large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	If the fistula goes into the body of the bladder and the intestine, avoid these places, and do not make incisions there as it is dangerous.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	After treatment, examine the wound until it is healed, and if the wound has been dry for a long time, with all matter removed, then know that the wound is completely healed.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	And if matter remains unremoved, understand that the wound is open, and bone at its base has decayed.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	And as for one of these which we will say in its place.
de la maladie des reins	Of kidney disease
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain from cold arises in the loins, and due to severe flatulence, and it does not affect a woman's disposition, then you must perform cauterisation on the loins, one side and the other, with the clavicle cautery as we previously mentioned;
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if we cauterise in the middle, there will be three cauterisations in a row, which will provide greater relief.
de la vessie	from the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is soft and weak from cold and moisture, causing the patient to retain urine, then cauterise outside on the bladder, where the hairs of the forearm begin, both right and left, with each cauterisation as long as a thumb's width.
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and make one cauterisation outside the back, or two if necessary.
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	And let the clavicle cauterization be done according to the form mentioned above.
de la marris	from the uterus
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the wife is cold and moist, and does not allow conception, and her flowers are corrupted and their endings delayed;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, she experiences great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	then it is necessary that we do three cauterizations around the navel, as we have said for bladder cauterization, and two on the outside of the back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	And let the clavicle cauterization be done, as we have said.
de la hainche	For the hip
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the viscous moisture descends into the hip socket, causing it to dislocate from its place, and the sign is that one thigh appears longer than the other when measured together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	And the location of the wound is found on the outside of the hip, so you must cauterize the patient over the box of the hip with a circular cautery, and bleed in front of the joint around the box as it turns, such that the bone is within the circle.
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and let these cauteries be like those with which one has cauterized the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if these cauteries are not present, make three olive-sized cauteries, and let the cautery be as perfect as all hearts.
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat until it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	Of the pain in the hip
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes to the bone of the hip, which is due to cold and moisture, and the patient has been treated as we have said in the previous section but it does not help, and the illness is chronic:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	Thus it is necessary for you to purge the patient of gross humours with fetid pills or other good similar pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After performing the cautery;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	And the manner of cauterisation is according to two methods:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	That is to say, caustic medicine together, and cautery by fire.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Cauterisation by fire is according to many methods, of which one is as follows:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	You should perform the cautery on the hip's bone with three triangular cauteries according to this form, making sure it is deep and large, leaving a space equal to a thumb's width between each cautery, and ensuring that they are olive-shaped.
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	Sometimes a cauterization is performed in the middle of the hip, for which there are four methods according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see fit, use the circular cautery, as we have previously mentioned, in the case of hip dislocation;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	But make sure that the circles cover the entire hip, and all the flesh around the heart is burned.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is how it is done for sciatica, when the pain is in the hip and does not reach down to the thigh or leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it reaches the thigh and leg, make two cauterizations where the patient indicates that the pain is felt, and four cauterizations above the ankle, slightly more to the left side.
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	And let the cauterization be with a knife, burning through the thickness of the flesh.
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And if the patient feels that the pain extends down to their toes or close to them, cauterize where they feel the pain with three or four points using the cautery called "point".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if necessary, do more of it.
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the patient believes that the pain is below the knee and towards the thigh, use the knife-like or circular cautery on them, and be very careful with all your cauterizations so as not to leave it there long enough for you to burn their nerves and large arteries, and do not cause greater harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who were cauterized on the ankle of the foot, and they left it for so long that the entire leg became swollen, as did the foot, and was perforated and completely ruined.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After an abdominal operation from which he died.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pain is in two parts together, cauterize one and then the other, according to this method.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	The wise ones said about the hip cauterization that it is like this: make a piece of iron, and at its head let it be as big as an inch-wide button or slightly less, and have it perforated from end to end with holes spaced out by an inch.
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and they are hinged on two sides, and also like knots, and there is one iron loop well made;
et c’est li forme:	and this is the shape:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	and it is heated until it becomes completely red and emit sparks, and then place it on the sore hip joint, turning it onto the healthy side;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and cauterize once with one cautery application and leave it for three days;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then apply an ointment of butter, leaving the wound open for a long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	after the treatment with ointments until it is healed.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasim says we rarely use this cautery due to the fear of its appearance, and if we did observe it more often.
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and yet it is one of the good cauterizations, which can be tolerated by some patients, depending on where it is applied.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The cauterization of medicine that burns is such that you make an instrument with crossbars into which the edge of the door descends, and it should be made of brass or iron on one side, and on the other let there be two handles, and between each a space equal to the thickness of a thumb;
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and let them be open above and below, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	Afterwards place the box of the hip on the patient lying on their healthy side, and press your hand firmly onto the box of the hip;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After immersion between the two circles of hot water that has been heated by one fire pot, leave for an hour, and let the patient bear its heat and burning.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For it is found to have a bite like fire there also;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the bite is over, lift your hand with the instrument and raise the hip of cool water, and leave it like this for three days, and apply butter until that which is black from the scald is removed.
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and let it rest for three days so it dries out;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this would be the final aid after the treatment of ointments until it is healed.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain extends to the thigh or down to the leg, make for him an instrument that holds it fast according to what you have done at the hip equally;
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and this is the method of the hot splint, and I have written it in the treatise on medical correction.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkali and quicklime, equal amounts of each, grind them together, then put in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	where there is a small opening through which the point of a lancet can enter;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and place above this another vessel well-weighted, and put on an alkali and heat it with gentle steam until there are two inches of water above the powders when you have properly grasped it in your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and leave it thus until water and moisture descends into the weighted vessel, then take all this water, and pour it onto heat and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then there will be great pain, administered by many works of medicine and cauterizations of other members.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it makes the same work like fire, and has other medicines with which one cauterizes well the hip thus as theses and honey of anacardium and hot soap; all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a cure where a man was healed from the pain in his hip and sciatic vein, and he praises it greatly, saying that no other treatment was required, and that he was cured immediately upon completing this cure, and then he bathed as he instructs below.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And it says in this manner that you take some fresh and dry green litharge (lead oxide), and grind it very well with one pound of grease, and put it on the hip and on the thigh and on the leg where the pain is located, and bind it there.
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and leave it for three hours; by the quantity that the patient no longer feels the burn.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	Then have him enter the bath so that his body is slightly moistened, and then let him into bed, and the pain will disappear completely and he will be cured.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And know that no one should use such medicinal cauterization without prior bodily evacuation.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dioscorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with goat's dung, it helps greatly;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and the cautery should be done in such a way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take linen and smear it with old oil, and place it on the depression between the big toe and the one next to it, which is called 'foscile'.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	After, take dry goat's dung and ignite it until it becomes charcoal, then place it on the wool, leaving it there until it is extinguished.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	Repeat this process again, and do not cease until you feel it has reached the hip and the pain has ceased.
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	This method of cautery is called "goat's dung cautery".
de la dolor dou dos	Of the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether due to falling or impact or excessive bleeding, or from any similar matter of cold spreading material; for none of these situations is cauterization beneficial except in the case that it arises from an influx of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	The patient should then be purged with foul-smelling pills or similar to empty their bowels, followed by three straight lines of ink on their back where the pain is felt, and in each line, apply five cauteries or more depending on the strength and endurance of the patient.
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	And perform the cauterization according to the method called "pricking.
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	And if you see fit, make three or four clavicle cauterizations in the middle of the bone following this method:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	Often this illness afflicts young children, and the signs of its onset are narrow shoulders when they lift their arms, and fear.
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	And you find at the last vertebra of the spine, an appearance different from those above it.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this one and wish to treat it, cauterize it with the full-circle cautery in this manner.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	Ensure that the cautery touches each part of the vertebra evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you wish to treat it, cauterize around the vertebra with two or three lines of pricking points, and let these be close together.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	Afterwards treat the area until it is dry according to what we have said, and ensure you do not apply cautery over any swelling that is on a nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	From the pain of joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When joint pain arises from moisture that has spread to every part of the body, and when pain occurs in the feet, which doctors call "gout," and when it is caused by coldness and cannot be cured with medicine, it must be treated with cautery in this way:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make a row of cauterizations around the ankle joint, and let the cauterizations be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is a need to treat the front of the foot, make a cauterization on what they call the "point.
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	If the pains extend up to the knees and other joints, which happens often, make three or four cauterizations on each knee, in all places, with every cauterization olive-shaped.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you need more, make even more, but do not hold your hand too close other than so that the heart of the cauterization iron is hot.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pain extends down to the knees and back, apply the cautery as we described in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, make two lines of punctures around the wrist.
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	And if there is no remaining pain in the fingers, make punctures on each joint and also upon the hair of the hand.
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pains reach the arms or shoulders, cauterize each part, and provide good care to the patient and have them take medicine.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you provide good care and remove phlegm, the patient will recover with God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the fracture of the cheekbone
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When a rupture occurs in the groin, and the testicles descend to the thighs, if it is recent, then when you see it being cured, ensure he does not eat that day.
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	And have him use things to loosen the belly, so that the feces descend from his stomach.
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	Afterwards, make him sit on his back between your hands, and instruct him to hold his breath until the testicles are retracted, then pull them with your fingers, and cut above the rupture over the bone of the pubic region, and continue cutting in a sign similar to half a circle across his body.
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Then heat the cautery which takes this form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	So long as they are white and shed no scent.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then reposition the balls to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	And the minister should hold his hand so that it does not return backwards;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	And spread the patient's legs well, place a cushion and a rolled cloth underneath them, and another on their lower back to hold the hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	Then place the cautery on the sign with all your might, and hold it straight while holding it until you reach the bone; if you do not reach it the first time, repeat it again until you get to the bone;
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	And be careful that the eye does not jump when you do the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	Que tu non li brusques.
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Et qu'en cela, le patient ne meurt pas, ni n'ait d'autres maux.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	Know that if you do not reach the bone with the cautery, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	Il convient que les cautères pour enfants soient subtils selon leur taille, et pour les grands de même en proportion.
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	Après trois jours, traite l'endroit du cautère au beurre jusqu'à ce que la brûlure disparaisse.
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	Après les soins initiaux, applique d'autres onguents jusqu'à ce que la plaie guérisse, et le patient doit rester alité quarante jours jusqu'à ce que la blessure soit complètement cicatrisée.
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	Il convient que son alimentation soit satisfaisante et prolongée afin qu'il puisse sortir de son lit sans trop s'affaiblir lorsqu'il sera prêt à aller dans une autre chambre.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after forty days, when he wishes to rise up, provide him with a well-made bandage, and wear it for another forty days.
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	And he should have good rest, not overexert himself, avoid excessive drinking or eating, and refrain from shouting loudly.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	When he follows this instruction, he will be entirely healed.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will now say the treatment for amputation within its chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	Of abdominal rupture.
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When sores appear in other body parts and are known to be infected, if they do not grow larger, apply a caustic [substance] as a cautery according to its quantity, and let the third part of the heart be burnt.
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	After the treatment, proceed with care as we have mentioned before.
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and some of the ancients have said it should be cauterized with the three-angled cautery according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	But first mark the place of incision and make a line across the width above the rupture, and another below it, then hold your hand in the middle to secure the iron tool throughout its use.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first set of cauterizations should be lighter and less severe.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of old pain in any limb
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes to any limb, whether from falling or injury, and this pain persists for a long time, and medical treatment is ineffective, then it must be cauterized with the cautery called 'point', and the cautery should be applied according to the length of the limb, its smallness, weakness, strength, and location of torsion, as well as the intensity of the pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	if it is burned by the first cautery, that's good;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	and if it does not bleed from the first one, start another cautery on top of that one, for such a custom is that it should change to the member that is nearest, which means you must perform cauteries until the patient bleeds.
de meselerie	of the mastectomy
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The months are aided sometimes by cauterization with great relief, especially illnesses that come from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	When you see it being cauterized, pay attention if the patient is at an early stage of illness, and if they are cured according to what we have said in the division, and there is no descent or remaining [symptoms], but you doubt that corruption may spread throughout the entire body, then do five cauteries on their head.
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	I place one [hand] under my head, and the other towards the forehead at the end of my hair.
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	And two above the two temples, and one behind on the nape.
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	And leave your hand there until the cauterization reaches down to the bone, and [leave it] so that scabs form such that vapors from thick fluids can escape.
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	And cauterize [the wound] on the muscle according to its depth.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the injury is spread across multiple places.
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	And if it clearly becomes worse, then you must treat [the injury] with these cauterizations that we have mentioned for the head, and one cautery at the nape of the neck, two cauteries on the spine in the back, six cauteries on the spinal column, one large one on the lower back and another beside it, and two on each shoulder.
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	et II sur les côtes, et II sur les tendons du pied, et I sur chaque joint des mains et des pieds, et sur les creux des mains;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	et prends garde aux nerfs qui sont au-dessus du talon en marchant, pour ne pas les brûler ;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	et une fois fais un cautère sur l'os du poignet, et un autre sur l'os de l'estomac, et un autre sur le foie.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	Et saches qu'autant tu en fais de cautères, autant tu apportes de l'aide, et il y a un bienfait ;
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	Et saches que les malades ne ressentent pas la douleur du cautère comme un corps sain la sentirait, car leur corps est déjà corrompu ;
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cautery be large or small depending on the limbs and joints, according to what you find appropriate for each type of iron tool.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After the operation, dress the wound with flour paste mixed with honey and other remedies until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When swelling occurs in any limb and is treated with medications, oils, and plasters, but it does not heal, then make cauterizations on the limb according to its size.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and let the cauterization be slightly deeper into the thickness of the heart.
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	then treat it with ointments until it is healed.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And sometimes one makes a cauterization on the hand and foot and back, at the exit of the nerve that moves the limb, in this way removing the swelling.
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	but in any case, do not attempt this if you are not knowledgeable about the limbs and the exits of nerves that move the body.
de albaras	For skin disease.
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the illness known as 'albaras' has subsided, and medical remedies are of no use, then cauterize it with a perfect cautery, according to the depth of the heart's species, until the whiteness is removed, and its color changes.
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	Then treat it with a cure made of flour from vetch and lentils, with rosehip oil and plantain leaves, along with partridge blood and pigeon blood, each in equal parts;
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	Mix everything together well, bind it with a cloth, and apply it to the affected area until it is healed.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of cancer by cauterization.
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When cancer appears at its beginning, and you want to stop it from spreading, cauterize it with a circular-shaped cautery, all around the edge of the cancerous area.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	Additionally, the wise ones say that one should also apply cautery to the center of the cancerous growth;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	and yet it does not seem good to me, for I fear that it will become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have already seen this happen once before;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and a more effective approach is to cauterize around it with the circular cautery, as we have mentioned extensively on cauterization techniques.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	Of swelling that cannot die.
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When someone has an illness called "adubelati", and their death is delayed either due to the excess waste it produces or due to the patient's condition when they are decrepit (meaning very old) with little blood, or because of the season;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you want to hasten their death:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	then cauterize around it with many small cauteries, being careful not to overheat.
aprés le laisse ensi.	After leaving it like this.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For she will hasten to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it piercing through at all the cauterization points, heat the cauterization tool that is shaped like this:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	Place your hand in the middle of this disease called "adubelati" until the cauterization tool has pierced the heart, and let the cauterization be such that the patient feels it externally in a way that slows the course of the rot.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment, wait until it is perfectly healed.
li cure dou feu par fer	The fire cure with iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	There is another kind of illness called "corrodens", which is nothing other than the wasting away of limbs, for it consumes the limbs just as fire consumes dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this illness in a place that can endure the fire cautery, then heat up both small and large cauterizing claws according to what is suitable for the area where the disease is located;
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	After that, cauterize thoroughly from all sides until you eradicate all the decay, leaving no trace of it behind, so that everything which is corrupted is removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then leave it for three days, and apply to the cauterized areas a soft paste made with oil until the scalds from the fire are removed, along with all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	Afterwards treat it with ointments that generate flesh.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see no healthy scab forming after three days, it is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if not, restart the cauterization on whatever remains in the corrupted areas.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this illness was sometimes treated with wet compresses instead of fire cauterization;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	But nevertheless, the fire cautery is of greater help, and I have already mentioned the treatment of a fever in this section.
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	Take it when you need it.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of the swellings that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Often it happens that on the feet, due to some external injury, a disease arises which we call "claws", and this is a faulty growth that wounds the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And there are two ways of performing cautery for this disease.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	That is to say, fire cautery and hot water cautery.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Fire cautery is when you heat a red-hot iron like the feather of an owl, and it should be made of good iron with the right measurements so that it can grip the nail from all sides, and have fine edges.
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	After that, place it very hot on the nail, and turn your hand all around the nail until it reaches its base.
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	Leave it like this for three days until it starts to discharge pus.
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Then make an ointment of wild mallows crushed with salt, and leave the ointment on overnight; the nail will come out and be uprooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound with ointment until it is healed.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are converted by force in the body, and often occur on hands and feet, then you must apply a hot water cautery to them.
et est en teil maniere:	and it is done this way:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	Take a copper or iron rod, or a goose feather quill, and place it on the nail and wart, that is, for warts;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	Place the rod on it so that it touches all around, then add a drop of hot water, and hold your hand firmly, pressing your hand in such a way that the edge of the rod comes to the root of the nail, allowing the hot water to penetrate deep into the root.
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and let the patient endure the biting of hot water for an hour.
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	then leave them be, and they will uproot themselves at their roots entirely.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Thus do one after another until you eradicate all those that are in the body, then treat them with ointments that generate flesh.
li cure dou trembler	The doctor of shaking.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When some tremble with coldness of nerves, or from quartan fever or another, you must make four cauterizations or four on their spine, one between each vertebra.
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and one cauterization on the foot, and one on the stomach with an olive-oil cautery.
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	let them tremble, and hasten their recovery from the cold illness.
des pustules puans	Pustules that stink.
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	At times when the body breaks out in baths or stinking pustules, this comes from gross corrupted matter.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	at first, when they appear, one must cauterize each head of the pimple.
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	A subtle cautery with myrtle wood, of which the tip is taken by fire, or with a long root of aristoloche, or with the lenticular cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And sometimes they cauterize them at the beginning when they appear, according to this method, and it prevents their growth from then on, but breaks the excess which causes them, and heals them.
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	But it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	There are often great bleedings from the artery which is cut at the wound that appears on the outside, or in the incision of an abscess, or in the cauterization of a limb, and similar things.
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	It is a very serious thing to stop (the bleeding).
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And nonetheless, when this happens to someone, hasten to place your index finger on the wound's injury, and press firmly until the blood stops flowing beneath your finger, with no more drops emerging.
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	Then apply to the fire several small and large olive oil cauteries until they are all red.
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	Afterward, take either the large or small one depending on the wound and the location of the artery, and place the cautery on that vein where you hold your finger, keeping the cautery there until the bleeding stops.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if sparks fly when you lift your finger from the wound, and the cauteries are extinguished, quickly take another one of the cauteries that are on fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not cease doing one after another until the blood is staunched.
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and make sure you do not burn the nerve nearby, and that no other harm comes to the patient.
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and know that when blood escapes from the artery, it cannot be properly stanched especially if the artery is large, unless through one of the four methods we have mentioned:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	either by cauterization, or by extracting it if it is not treated, or by strongly binding with thread, or by applying medications that have the power to stanch blood.
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and bind it tightly so.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever introduces bandaging with tight linen strips or applying hot compresses, or other similar methods, will not benefit much from it.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if this happens to someone and they have no mirror or medicine available, one must put their index finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and stretch it well until it is stanched over the wound and over the vein.
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	And do not move the arm, but often wet it with cold water, very cold so that the blood is frozen and thickened and reduced in volume.
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And make incisions beforehand on those who need cauterization and medicine.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here begins the second book on treating hernias.
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have told you in the first chapter about all ailments requiring fire cauterization or burning medicines, and their effects, causes, instruments, and forms of cauterization.
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	And I have placed this chapter about the head down to the feet; I will go through this same path in this chapter so that what is sought may be found more easily.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And so as I begin this work, my dear son, you must learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the previous one on cauterization, and thus it requires even greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	For there is doubt and fear, and death comes to many.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I warn you not to attempt folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For people come for treatment in many different ways.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	If such patients die quickly upon seeing their condition and the severity of their illness, they perish due to despair.
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	And this we ought to fear.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	Of these there are those who give you their meaning, and say:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	Wait, I am healed";
et li maladie est despitouse.	But the illness is deceitful.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	It is not right to agree with those who come to you in this manner, but place greater emphasis on your honour than on your greed, and do not act foolishly but wisely regarding what you are sure of and can achieve.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	And make use of prognosis and diagnosis in treating your patients, for their salvation depends on it.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	And this will help you gain a good reputation, glory, and a memory of praise.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Very dear son, may our Lord give you good understanding and righteousness, and may he will to inspire you with the holy inspiration of his hand, Amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Or I have ordered this chapter in a way that divides it into sections, according to how it is presented before the chapter on cauterization, which I explained to you from head to toe, so that you can find more easily what you need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	Water-filled head.
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	Know that this illness often comes to children during birth, when the midwife grips the child's head too tightly.
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	And sometimes it happens due to an unknown cause that is not known.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this illness occur in anyone but children, and death came swiftly to all that I witnessed.
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	And for this reason, it seems best to abandon the work of such treatments.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw a child whose shoulder was full of water, and his head grew larger each day until he could no longer bear it.
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and the moisture increased so much that he died, and this fluid had gathered beneath the bone above the shoulder-blade, between the heart and the bone.
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the treatment is such if the moisture is between the heart and bone, and the abscesses are small, that you should make a wide incision in the head.
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and it should be as long as two fingers, so that the moisture drains out.
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and observe here the shape of the spatula.
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is deeper, and the abscess larger, make two incisions in the form of a cross, according to this shape:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is beneath the bone, and you see that the sutures of the head are open on all sides, and water spurts out when you press it with your hand inside, but it does not respond to you:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	So you must divide the head into three incisions, like this.
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision extract all moisture quickly.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	Then bind the incisions with cloth strips and powders, apply wine and oil, and leave it like this for five days.
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	Then untie the bindings, treat the wound with tenting and ointments, keep the head bound evenly, and feed the patient dry meat without moisture until the limb is strengthened and healed.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another method of incision is to observe where the abscess seems largest, and where fluid has gathered.
car aucune fois est elle devant;	because sometimes it appears there first.
aucune fois derrier;	sometimes at the back.
aucune fois en destre;	Some times to the right side;
et aucune fois en senestre.	and some times to the left side.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Cut therefore the place where the abscess appears, and drain the pus, and make an incision according to your ability;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and take care not to cut the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and if the vein starts to bleed, so that the patient dies due to loss of blood and evacuation of moisture.
de reume	Of rheumatism
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When someone has a disease called "cataract" in the eyes or throat, and the illness is chronic, and medical treatment is ineffective, then the final remedy is cauterization along with the cutting of two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is necessary, therefore, when you cut the veins, that the patient should turn his head backwards;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	Afterwards, rub the place with a rough cloth until the arteries are visible, then stretch the patient's neck back with all your strength.
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	Then look where the vein beats, and the eyes of both are after the ears, and they are almost closed.
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then mark the eyes of anchovy, then cut both with a sharp spatulate knife in two parts, so that the incision reaches down to the bone, and it should be done across the width of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see it, push the spatula under the artery and cover it above, cutting as deep as necessary across it.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut open, blood spouts upwards continuously outwards.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not open to the touch, you must measure the space of three fingers, then mark and cut until reaching the bone.
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	And the amount of blood to be let out is six ounces, and perhaps a little more or less, depending on how much the patient can endure, and the fullness of the artery.
puis regarde la plaie:	Look at the wound next.
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	If it remains over the bone without a splint, cut to prevent hot abscesses from forming; open up the wound and bind it closed, then treat it with ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	Of migraine
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When ancient migraine comes with acute catarrh due to moisture of tears and warmth in the temples, along with old and persistent madness and similar things, and it is treated with various medical cures but nothing helps, then we extract the arteries from the temples and cauterize them, as we have described.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the method of arrow extraction is as follows: have the patient grasp their own hair at the temples and feel for the artery that pulses there, as it is quite prominent due to its beating, although in some men who are very cold this may not be apparent;
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	If it is retracted, have the patient constrict their neck with some cloth, then rub the area with a coarse cloth and bathe it in hot water until the artery becomes clearly visible.
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the spatula which is shaped like this:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then scrape the skin lightly until you reach the artery, then draw it upwards with pincers, and carefully remove the membranes that are beneath on each side.
et se li artere est subtilz, si la torne a la pointe de l’uncine, puis la cope de celle partie selonc la quantiteit des II chiés.	and if the artery is thin, turn it to the point of the lancet, then cut that part according to the size of two fingers.
Car s’elle n’est copee, si ne saut mie li sans dou tout en tout.	For if it is not cut, the blood cannot flow out completely everywhere.
Et trai dou sanc des VI c/, jusc’a III;	and draw out blood from six cupfuls down to three.
et se li artere est grans, si covient que tu la lies en II leus d’un fil double fort de soie, que porriture n’i veigne devant le soudement de la plaie, et veigne decorremens de sanc;	and if the artery is large, you must tie it in two places with a strong double thread of silk, so that nothing may come before the healing of the wound and blood may flow freely.
puis cope la superfluiteit qui est entre les II liiens en celle houre meisme, et puis, se tu vues, si lou cauterize dou cautere cutellaire jusc’a l’os tant que li chiés soient copez;	Then remove the excess flesh that is between the two ligaments at the same time, and then, if you wish, cauterize it with a knife-like tool until the bone is exposed so that the head is cut.
et c’est li muedre oevre, se li malaides n’a fievre et il est de chaude complexion.	It is a delicate operation if the patient has no fever and has a warm constitution.
Car li cauteres est aide por finir les moistors:	For cauterization helps to dry up moisture.
por ceu est il de plus grant aide as moistors.	It is especially useful for dealing with moisture.
Ou il covient por l’estraction des arteres que om emplisse lou leu de viel coton et mette on sus tentes bien faites;	When extracting arteries, one must fill the space with old cotton and place well-made bandages over it;
et quant on les desliera, si soit curez de medicines seches que font naistre char, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when one removes the bandages, ensure that they are covered with dry medicinal substances that promote flesh growth and bandages until it is healed.
et se sans cort de l’artere tant dis com tu i oevres, si te haste dou coper par cautere, ou tu emple lou leu de vitriole et l’estrain a ta main que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if you see blood flowing from the artery as you work, hasten to cut with cautery, or apply to the place of injury vitriol and hold it in your hand until the bleeding ceases.
et se tu n’as ceu present, si met sor le leu ton doit tant que li sans soit congelez, et arose le leu d’aigue froide tant que li sans cesse, et soit estraint si com il covient;	And if you don't have that available, place your hand over the wound until the blood is coagulated, and pour cold water onto the area until the bleeding stops, holding it firmly as required.
et ceu qui est muedre et plus legier en l’estraction de l’artere est que tu cauterizes la voinne de cest cautere trenchant de II pars, mais li trenchant soient bien espés por warder plus longement lor chalor.	What is easier and lighter in the extraction of an artery is to cauterize the wound with this sharp cautery cut into two parts, but ensure that the cuts are deep enough to retain their heat for longer.
Car quant li estrumens est trop tenves, si tient moins sa chalor.	For when the instruments are too thin, they hold less heat.
Et doit avoir entre les II coutelz I doit de gros d’espaice, et puis quant tu as signiet d’enche les II leus, et tu mes lou fer ardant sus tant qu’il viegne jusc’a l’os, et cope la voinne en II leus;	There should be a thumb's width between the two knives, and once you have joined together the two ends, place the heated iron on top until it reaches the bone, then cut the wound into two parts.
et soient esloigniet entre les II chiés car il n’est mie soudez de cest cautere dou tout en tout;	and they are separated between the two joints for it is not fully healed from this cauterization.
et c’est li forme dou cautere:	and this is the shape of the cautery:
des larmes	tears
