Quant les larmes des eulz sont dessendans des voinnes que sont sus lou test dou chief de fuer, et il ne profite mie cure de medicine c’on i faice, et tu vois la faice dou malaide enrougir, et sent ou front ambulation si com de fremis;	When the tears from the eyes flow down the veins that are on top of the head, and no treatment with medicine helps, and you see the patient's face turn red, and they feel itching or tingling on their forehead;
et sui oil sont tenve et moiste si que li poil des papieres sont cheut, et sont eschaufees les papieres, et escorchies de l’ardor des larmes, si ait mestier de ceste cure.	and if their skin is tense and moist so that the hair of the eyelids falls out, and the eyelids are burned and peeled from the heat of the tears, then this treatment is necessary.
Et l’apelerent li ancien «cure contuse», et est que tu faices a rere au malaide qui a ceste maladie les poilz qu’il ait ou front, puis li fai III fendures ou front igalment selonc la longesce dou front;	And the ancients called it "contusive cure," and you must make the patient with this disease grow hair on their forehead, then make three incisions equally spaced on the forehead along its length.
et soit l’une des fendures ausi com II doi tout emmi lou front en avalant aval jusc’a neif, et les autres II as II costelz par desus les papieres, et te garde de l’incision des arteres que sont as II costez par desus les papieres;	and let one of the incisions be just like that two fingers across your forehead downwards to the nose, and others from these two to the ribs above the nipples, and take care not to cut into any arteries which are on either side above the nipples.
et aloigne ta main de la continuation des II mandibules, et soit chescune plaie la quantiteit de III dois au traver joins;	keep your hand away from the extension of the two jaws, and let each wound be the size of three fingers in width across.
et aies apparillie une piece d’esponge et mout de drapelz ses por essuer lou sanc, puis boute le spatumile agut de II pars de coi ci est li forme:	have ready a piece of sponge with plenty of fine linen to wipe away the blood, then insert the sharp-pointed probe which is divided into two parts; this is its shape:
des l’incision qui est dever la temple jusc’a la seconde incision;	from the first incision over the temple down to the second incision.
et escorche tout le keur qui est entre les II fendures a tot lou syfac qui est sus l’os, puis fai autreteil des la moiene incision jusc’a l’autre seconde, et puis estrai fuer cest spatumile.	scrape out all the brain which lies between these two incisions down to the bone itself; do likewise from the middle incision down to the other second one and then withdraw this probe.
si boute en la premiere fendure l’estrument qui est apelez «cultellaire», et est tresbien trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part est souef, ne mie trenchans, et c’est li forme:	If you insert into the first incision the instrument called 'scalpel', which is very sharp on one side and soft, not sharp, on the other, this is its form:
Et met le costeit taillant vers la char aerse au keur, et lou costeit souef vers l’os, et lou boute tant qu’il veigne a la moiene fendure.	And place the cutting edge towards the flesh near the heart, and the soft edge towards the bone, insert it until it reaches the middle incision.
Et cope toz les vasselz que dessendent dou chief as eulz tant que l’incision soit continue jusc’a ceu qui apert dou keur, et puis autreteil fai en la moiene fendure jusc’a l’autre defuer;	And cut all the vessels that descend from the head to the eyes until the incision is continuous up to what appears of the heart, and then make another similar incision up to the other side.
et puis estrai dou sanc igalment, et espresse lou leu por le sanc pris;	then extract the blood evenly, and press the area for the extracted blood.
puis met en chescune fendure une tente de viel coton, et met sus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile et en aisil, et garde que apostemes chaus n’i veigne;	after that, place in each incision a tent made of old cotton, and put on moist bandages with wine, oil, and egg white, taking care not to let any abscesses develop.
et au tier jor deslie lou liien, et i amenistre grant planteit d’aigue tede, puis lou cure d’oignement basilicon avec oile roset, et d’autres cures dont on cure plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	on the third day, remove the binding, and apply a great deal of warm water, then treat it with an ointment made from basilicon and rose oil, and other treatments used for wounds until it is healed.
dou reume des eulz	The realm of eyes
Quant a aucun vienent catarre agut acostumeement, et tu vois les eulz tenves et petis, et afoiblir la veue, et les papieres brulees;	When someone is afflicted with acute catarrh repeatedly, and you see their eyes turned and small, weakening the sight, and the eyelids burnt;
et li poil chieent, et ou chief en parfont a dolor ague, et li malaides esternue;	the hairs fall out, and in the head they produce sharp pain, and the patient sneezes;
adonques saiches par ces accidens que celles matieres et cil catharre ne vient fuer que de maintes voines, et li muedre cure que i est, si est ceste.	then you should know that these symptoms and this catarrh come from many blocked passages, and the best treatment is as follows:
Et est que tu comande au malaide a rere son front, puis fai une grant fendure emmi lou front, et une autre dou large I poc.	And so instruct the patient to clear their forehead, then make a wide incision in the middle of the forehead, and another from ear to ear.
Et comence des la fendure de la temple senestre a la temple destre, et soit li incision jusc’a l’os;	Begin with an incision from the left temple to the right temple, and let it reach the bone;
et esloigne ta main des ners des temples que muevent au mengier;	and keep your hand away from the nerves of the temples that control chewing;
et quant li os est descovers, si essue tout le sanc a une esponge, et puis desevre entre les II levres de la fendure et i met coton viel, et tentes de lin;	and when the bone is exposed, wipe away all the blood with a sponge, and then separate between the two lips of the incision and place old cotton and linen cloth there;
puis lie desus drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile, et te garde d’aposteme chaut;	Then place damp cloths soaked in wine and oil above it, and beware of hot abscesses.
quant il est ostez, si covient que tu frottes l’os tant que chars i comence a naistre, puis le cure de choses exiccatives, que font enjanrer char.	Once it is removed, you must rub the bone until flesh begins to grow, then treat it with drying agents that promote flesh growth.
En teil maniere:	In this way:
pren II parties de flor de froment, et de colofoine IIII parties, et en fai emplaustre;	Take two parts wheat flower, and four parts colophony, and make an ointment.
et l’aministre en ces plaies por enjanrer char per tout.	Apply it to these wounds to promote flesh growth everywhere.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	Of the stuffing of ears
Tout ceu que chiet ens oreilles est une des IIII choses:	Everything that falls into the ear is one of four things:
ou grains, ou beste, ou piere de mine ou semblans chose si com fer;	Or grains, or insects, or rock from underground or similar thing like iron;
ou semence, si com jaisses, feves, pois;	Where seed, such as beans, peas, and chickpeas;
ou chose defluans si com aigue et aisilz et semblans choses.	Or things flowing like water and fluids and similar things.
Quant il chiet en l’oreille piere ou autre maniere de chose que ne s’ajoste mie a l’oreille, ne ne croist en l’oreille, si met l’oreille au solel.	When a stone or other object that does not fit or grow in the ear falls into it, place the ear in the sun.
Se tu vois la piere, si distille aucun poc d’oile violet ou oile de sisament, puis i amenistre extraction;	If you see the stone, drip some purple oil or olive oil into it, then proceed with the extraction;
et lou fai esternuer de condisi, et li estoupe les narines quant li esternuemens vient, et met entor l’oreille pieces de drapelz ou laine;	Make him sneeze with powder, and plug his nostrils as the sneeze comes on, and put woollen cloths around his ears;
et estent l’oreille au desus.	And stretch out the ear upwards.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure;	Often it happens that there is bleeding during this treatment;
et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	And if there is no bleeding, proceed with the extraction using fine pincers, which are shaped like this:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin;	If she can endure pincers, it is good;
se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure;	if not, then administer the gentle onion knife for removal;
et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne;	and if she cannot bear this, then make a brass tube and insert the head of the tube into the ear canal with force, blocking what surrounds the tube with soft wax so that no air can enter alongside it.
puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit;	then treat her forcefully, for it often becomes necessary as we have said.
et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor;	and if she does not heal with such methods, then take bird lime and put an instrument that serves this purpose inside it, wrapping some cotton around.
puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	Then press the wound on the stone or whatever it is, and draw hard.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme;	And if it cannot be done with all these things that we have said, then hasten to open the ear rather than an abscess before heat and spasm come.
et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant;	the method of the incision is that you first empty the patient's head of blood, and extract according to the measure of its strength, then make the patient sit between your hands and turn their ear upwards, and cut a small incision in the root of the ear at the fat where it depends.
et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche;	and let the incision be like a moon, so that you reach the stone, then remove it according to your ability, and suck it quickly into your mouth.
et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat it until it is healed.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction;	And if there is an abscess that has formed and it swells, administer the procedure for its removal.
et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	And if it cannot be extracted, use the spatula, very thin according to this form:
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and make an incision of that grain.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces;	But do not attempt this if you think the abscess is moist due to ear moisture, until you have made many incisions.
puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	Then extract it with fine pincers and by sucking, as we have said, so that the extraction is eased.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	Therefore, in the case of water falling into the ear, the patient should first use sneezing as a remedy, and fill the ear with old cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And let them lie on that same ear where the water is.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If this should work, it is good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu;	If not, take many stones according to the length of your thumb, thin and light, and heat them a little in the fire.
et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille;	and place the patient with a hole in his ear, and let it protrude from one of his feet on the other side, and pierce another stone above the stone that is in the ear.
et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer;	and do not stop making stones from stone until the water comes out completely, and thus let it come out completely.
et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars;	and if you see this, take a reed and push one end into the ear, and ignite the other end with fire until the tip of the reed burns.
puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	then remake another with other reeds until the water comes out completely, as we have said about stones.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division;	In the extraction of the beast, if it has a small body like a flea and similar things, treat it as we have said in the section on division.
mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures;	but if she is of great body such that one can feel her, so arrange to extract pincers;
et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	and it is the lightest thing that can be removed from within the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil:	In the extraction of worms embedded in the ears, when you treat it as we have said in the section on distillations and its treatment does not help, then one must look at the ear in the sun:
s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	if no worms appear, so catch them with fine pincers, and if none show up, take a cane shaped like this one:
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	And it is narrow below and wide above.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine;	And insert the finest head into the ear according to the severity of the patient's suffering, then suck hard on all parts of the cane;
fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	Fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere;	And if they do not obey to come out, stuff cotton around the stem as I have said for stones.
et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations;	and if they do not come out as we have said, then administer the distillations that ancient doctors have tested for worm occlusion, and you will find it in the treatise on distillations.
et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	and distill your oils and medicines into the ear with all these instruments, of which the form is as you see here:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller;	And be it of silver or copper, narrow below to the small openings, and overhang above for distillation;
et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton;	and to compress the distillation into the instrument of well-made copper for this purpose, and if you wish take the razor and envelope around the point with cotton accordingly;
puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille;	Then I pour your oil or your juice, and whatever medicine you desire in the cane, and let the cane be placed into the ear.
puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille;	Then push in the razor with all the cotton, and press your hand firmly until the oil is completely drained from the ear.
et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille;	The patient should smell the oil within, and let it be that the distillation is slightly warm from the fire, unless you are to distill it into the ear.
et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	Be careful that it is not too cold, as the medicine would not be so effective.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	Of the stuffing of ears
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles;	No child is born without openings in their ears.
et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir;	And this same thing happens to men due to a wound or wax buildup within the ear, and these blockages sometimes become so deep in the ear that one cannot see them.
et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	and sometimes there is a protrusion of the hole, and one can see it clearly.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil;	Therefore, when it is not visible and there are several conditions for a rapid cure, you should place the patient's ear in the sun.
et regarde dedens:	and look inside.
se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	if you see the dark spot appear, operate with this small spatula as follows:
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille;	Make sure it is sharp and flat both in front and behind so as not to wound the ear;
se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	if the dark spot is in the earwax or the body of the ear, hold it with fine tweezers and extract it gently until all the wax is removed.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	And if the earwax is completely blocking the ear, take a thin and light scraper, heat it slightly over a flame, then insert it into the ear canal.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille;	If you detect an impaction that causes the patient earache, pierce gently, and be careful not to damage the nerves of the ear.
puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	Then place in the ear a tent according to the size of the hole, and moisten it with Egyptian ointment.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet;	Do this for as long as it takes until the wound is healed, on that day you take a tent and moisten it with rose water, then powder it with ground vitriol.
et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	And if you see the ear swollen, it is necessary that you treat the tent and remove another one moistened in a wax made of rose oil and beeswax, until the swelling is gone.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	And if bleeding occurs, immerse a sponge and small cloth in cold water, place it on the ear, and employ other treatments that stop the flow of blood as described in the section on distillations.
de la char des papieres	of the paper flesh
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines;	This eyelid remedy that comes in paper when they are moist and dry out, you must extend with tweezers and small pincers, then scrape with a spatule made from its roots.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	Then place ground vitriol on it quickly.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues;	And if it peels off, gently cauterize with a subtle lenticular cautery, and the cauterizer after incision is better.
et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines;	and they often return when any remains of their root stays behind.
et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	And when they are cauterized by fire, those roots are burned and do not return.
de la gresle	Of the hail
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz;	Many times there come to the eyes certain things that appear like hail in form and hardness, and for this reason this illness is called "glaucoma," and it is an accumulation of moisture thick upon the paper above and below.
li ovraiges est telz:	The works are such as these:
pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir;	Take note if the glaucoma moves from one side to another, for this is a minor thing to know;
fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	Make it therefore wide, then lightly scrape each side, take the pincers to it and scoop it out.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide;	If you cannot remove it without piercing the paper slightly, this does not harm the patient much;
et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	And if the wound is large, sew it together with stitches, and treat it until it is healed.
et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	If the wound is small, apply no pressure or force, for ointments will restore it quickly and promote flesh growth.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre;	If the blood is descending into the ear towards the upper part, then turn it upside down and catch the blood with some absorbent paper. Press and squeeze gently from both sides.
et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien;	And if the blood-soaked paper is far away due to an incision made, it does not matter.
et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	Once the blood is extracted, rinse the eye with salty water and treat it with an ointment that promotes flesh growth until the patient is healed.
de la graisse des eulz	from the fat around the eyes
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz;	Exinach is a grease that forms on the paper-like membranes above [the eyes], and this happens more often in children than adults, causing great discomfort to their eyes. They experience catarrh in the mornings, and cannot bear to look at the sunlight because tears rush to their eyes;
et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	And so they lie on their faces afterward, sleeping above [the dislocation], and the paper-like membranes beneath their eyebrows become moistened by a flower's appearance or covering of exinach that appears in the eye.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	And when you press the place with your fingers and feel the bone between them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain;	The procedure is carried out as follows: with the patient's head placed in your lap;
et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li;	You then take a linen cloth and prepare a tent-like structure in the shape of a circle according to the amount needed to contain the exinach from each part, placing it over [the patient];
et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle;	and press with your two hands from either side so that the extraneous matter is gathered within the circle;
puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne;	then make in the middle of the moisture with the sharp spatule a slit no wider than the wound made when opening a vein;
et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach;	and make the skin perfect until you reach the extraneous matter;
et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	and in many cases, extraneous matter comes out of the slit, resembling a piece of white fat.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars;	Extract it, therefore, all at once with a piece of lint cloth between your two hands outside the wound, and turn your hand to the right and left until it is dispersed.
et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	And make sure you do not insert it into the incision, lest you reach the entire spinal cord up to the eye and injure it.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere;	And if the bone does not appear at the beginning of the incision, then slightly enlarge the incision gently until it becomes visible.
puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	Then extract it as we have described, then wet some cloth in vinegar and water, and place it on the site, and bind with bandages.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	And for such men who grind salt and put it on to corrupt that moisture which has remained.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat [it] until it is healed.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it comes to the place of an abscess with heat, treat [it] with soothing emollients until it is healed.
des poilz des papieres	Of the hairs on papules.
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz;	When hairs grow on the eyelids contrary to nature and are not plucked out, they harm the eyes, causing various ailments such as habitual tearing and softening of the lids, ultimately leading to blindness.
et est li cure selonc IIII manieres:	and the treatment is performed according to four methods:
ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	by means of cauterization with fire, or by medicinal treatment depending on what has been presented in the chapter on cauterization, and it is done either through incision and stitching, or by canes, as I shall explain.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre;	You must place the patient's head on your lap, then turn their left eye toward your left hand;
s’elle est convertie, c’est boin;	if it turns [toward your hand], that is good;
se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus;	if not, insert a needle into the corner of it [the eye] along with some thread;
et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur;	and let this be near the edge of the eyelid where the hairs grow next to these hairs, and pull the thread above all the eyelid, and turn it back [toward you];
puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit;	Then make an incision under that part of the skin, beneath the hairs close by, cutting all the patella along its breadth, from the large hollow down to the small one.
puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	Then extract the thread and place beneath the skin a small tent made of cotton and linen, then make an incision in the skin shaped like an anchor, just as the myrtle leaf is, but it ought to be proportionate according to how much you wish to raise the skin that has been divided all over.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie;	And if the one who requires it needs to cut away a large quantity of skin according as the skin is softened;
puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit;	Then make an incision along the entire patella following the two lines you have marked, beginning at the large hollow and going down to the small one.
et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute;	and be one of the incisions near natural hairs with a thickness of a root, then insert the uncinus into one of the two angles of the heart, and then strip all of it.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce;	then join the two lips with a seam using a needle and any fine wool thread, wipe away the blood, remove excess threads above both eyebrows and any sticky substances if you wish to do this.
et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII;	and if not, have no care for it, then leave the seam and threads for three or four days.
puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor;	then treat the wound without a seam using drying and binding substances, for paper becomes loose during the healing of the wound and its reunion, but the seam is harmful (as the ancients said), and this work is free from fear.
et si a une autre maniere:	and if you do so in another way:
et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	and take a piece of paper that is shaped like the leaf of myrtle, as we have said, three ounces separated according to the form that is here:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	Then cut what is above with small scissors evenly according to the form which is here:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure;	And if you cannot hold the forceps, and the thing is not even, then take a needle with one thread, and place it in the middle of the shape;
et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment;	and place another thread by the large border, and the second thread by the small one, and join between your two fingers the threads evenly;
puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then raise your hand evenly, and lift all the skin that you have cut, as we have said, then join the two lips of the wound by stitching, and treat it until it is healed;
et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans;	And if an abscess arises at your incision site, soothe it with cautery and similar soothing ointments.
et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit:	And sometimes the hair on the paper turns white:
si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision;	Then it is necessary that you follow what we have said about incision;
mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	But the suture on one side or the other is more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme:	The treatment of ulcers follows this form:
et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est;	And it is that you turn the paper over and cut within according to what I have said, then make two ulcers per side, and also two subtle threads as long as the paper's width and the thickness of a spatula.
et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz;	et hold the two heads of two parts where you hold the tendons;
puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment;	then bring together one and the other carefully on that which is above the cornea of the eye, and remove the two chains from the two parts thus formed;
et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	and leave it thus for a few days, and the skin which has been stretched will die and turn black and rot until it falls off by itself.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	If it takes too long, cut it with some force, then treat until it is healed;
et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil;	and once the wound has healed, if the cornea is raised, and hairs will no longer prick there;
et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	and this is the form of the two chains which you will make according to this figure, and with these quantities in length and width:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil;	The works are such that you take a subtle needle, and insert into it soft and subtle silk thread;
puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc;	Then bring together the heads and tie each one subtly, and let the length of the threads be a palm's length.
puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil;	Then place in the wound another thin silk thread briefly, and tie the ends of the threads together.
puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain;	Then put the patient's head on your lap.
et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil;	And let it be near the sun so that the work is illuminated, for this is delicate and precise work, then insert the needle into the entire wound at the root of the adjacent hair, and pierce through to the other side until you extract it from above the natural hair.
puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors;	Then extract the hair up to the shaft, and push it into the shaft if there is one or two or three or more.
puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	Then extract your hand until the hairs come towards you fully into the paper with their natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil;	And if the shaft is treated and the hair does not come towards you with it, then treat the shaft from below along all of the thread that you have arranged there, until the shaft comes forward through the hole above and you see it by eye.
adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus;	Then treat the shaft and thread like this, close the eye, and leave it closed for two or three days until the hair dries in its place and flesh grows over.
et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	And if the hairs are small, accompany a long hair with natural horsehair, and raise it with that one or leave it alone until it is elongated, then pull it out.
de la porriture de l’oil	Of the decay of the eye
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres:	When this disease, which is called "aleacrati" or inflammation comes into the eye, it has two manners.
l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	One natural, and the other unnatural.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And it happens suddenly due to a wound, or from a surgeon's knife, or from cauterization, and through similar means.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee;	And the way to treat it is to open that suture, and separate its lips, and place linen threads inside, and bind it until it is healed.
et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	And you must not use anything that dries out or constricts in its treatment.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere;	For if you do this, the disease will return worse than before;
mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic;	but I use softening substances, like fenugreek;
et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	and the decoction of water or wine and flax seed are cooked, with melted diaklon ointment in any oil, wrap it in a cloth, and treat accordingly.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant;	And the key to your treatment is that you must be careful not to join it back together in its previous form;
et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	And these treatments we have mentioned are not strong enough to prevent this disease from returning in its previous form.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	of the flesh which comes to the eye
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This illness, which is dislocated and truly called 'axacrati', is natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans;	The complications arise from wounds, cuts, cauterization, and similar procedures;
et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char;	and the way of working is such that you take a needle with two threads on it, and insert it into the flesh, piercing from left armpit to right so that the thread comes out at both shoulders of the body;
puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	then lift up all the flesh above the needle, and cut with a wide spatula.
Et se li figure de la papiere revient selonc ceu qu’il covient, c’est boin;	and if the shape of the paper returns according to what is needed, it is good;
se ceu non, si pren I raseur et le met en la fendure, et torne la papiere, et fent II fendures ou costeit dedens la papiere;	if not, take a razor and place it in the gap, turn the paper, and make two cuts along its edge within the paper;
et soient li chiés des II fendures des II angles de l’incision que tu as copeit, et soit fais uns angles si que quant elles sont assemblees, que li figure soit ausi com li figure d’une lettre qui a non «I griesche»;	and let the edges of the two cuts be at the two corners of the incision you have made, and make these corners so that when they are assembled, the shape is like that of a letter called 'Greek';
puis oste celle char, selonc la quantiteit que ses costez est agus desoz, de ceu qui enseut la papiere, puis ajoste les II parties desevrees, et les cout d’un fil de lainne;	Then remove that flesh, according to the amount that its sides are extended below, from what follows the paper, then adjust the two separated parts, and sew them with a thread of wool.
puis lou cure de ceu que nos avons dit des medicines mollifians, et de tentes, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it with what we have said about softening medicines and bandages, until it is healed.
Et se li maladie vient de fendure ou de costure ou de cautere, si covient que tu fendes une fendure plainne desoz les poilz des papieres, et selonc ceu qui est ci devant;	And if the illness comes from a rupture or suture or cauterization, you must make an incision directly below the hairs of the papers, and according to what is written above;
puis desevre entre les II leivres d’une tente, si com j’ai dit;	Then separate between the two lips of a bandage, as I have said;
et doit on faire l’ovraige selonc la forme de la maladie, car elle est mout diverse en forme, et li saiges maistres appareille engien de tout som pooir coment il faice revenir la figure a sa forme natureil;	And one must perform the operation according to the form of the illness, as it is very diverse in shape, and wise surgeons devise instruments with all their power on how to restore the figure to its natural form;
et li malaides meisme, selonc ceu qu’il i covient d’ovraige et d’estrumens em plusors dispositions.	And the patient themselves, according to what they need for treatment and tools, it is necessary to have several arrangements.
dou soudement de la papiere	suddenly from the skin paper
Quant ceste soudure avient a mains homes en teil maniere que li papiere desus est sodee avec le blanc de l’oil, et ne puet movoir ne faire ses ovraiges naturez, si covient donques que tu i boutes la pointe d’un raseur desoz la papiere, et la lieve en haut;	When this welding occurs in young men, so that the iris is welded to the white part of the eye, and cannot move or perform its natural functions, it is necessary for you to insert the tip of a razor blade under the iris and lift it upwards.
et l’estent as pinceures, tant que tu copes ceu qui est aert au spatumile subtil, qui ne soit mie trop agus ne trop trenchans, si que li malaides ne puisse soffrir que li spatumile trop agus ne blecent l’oil;	And stretch it with pincers until you cut what is hard with the fine spatula, which should not be too sharp or cutting so that the patient can bear it and the sharp spatula does not hurt their eye.
et soit ton incision, dont tu escorche celle assemblee, legierement, si que li papiere reviegne selonc sa forme natureil;	And make your incision, from which you remove the assembly, lightly so that the iris returns to its natural shape.
et est sanee toute celle assemblee, et font aucune fois en l’oil aigue salee, et le leve d’aigue douce, et de coliere;	And the whole assembly is healed, and sometimes they use salted water on the eye, and raise it with warm water, and with collars.
puis met entre la papiere et l’oil une tente de lin, et met sus l’oil laine moillie en abun d’uef;	Then place between the eye and paper a tent of linen, and put on the eye wool moistened in egg white.
et aprés le tier jor use dou coliere et des choses soudans tant qu’il soit sanez.	After three days, use collars and hot compresses until it is healed.
de l’ungle de l’oil	of the fingernail of the eye
Saiches que li ungle est selonc II manieres:	Know that the nail grows in two ways:
elle est nervouse et semblans a I dur syfac, et une autre qui n’est mie nervouse, mais est semblans a blainche moistor congelee, que quant on la touche de fer et on la cuide panre as pinceures, si ne puet om;	One is nervous and resembles hard skin, and the other is not nervous but looks like white frozen moisture, which cannot be pierced by iron or scraped off with pincers when touched.
et l’une et l’autre semblance encomence devers le grant larmier, et croist poc et poc tant qu’ele cuevre toute la veue et toute la lumiere et le movement de l’oil.	And both these appearances begin towards the large tear duct, and grow little by little until they cover all of the view, all of the light, and all of the eye's movement.
Et li maniere de l’incision si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz;	And the manner of incision is such that the patient must place their head on a sound pillow, then open their eyes for you.
et lieve la papiere a ta main, puis coil l’ungle as pinceures de petite doubleure, et l’estent au desus;	hold the paper to your hand, then curl your nail into tiny pincers, and stretch it above [the incision].
puis pren une aguille, et i met I poil de cheval, ou de vaiche, ou de buef, et I fil fort;	then take a needle, and put into it either horse hair or cow hair or ox hair and strong thread;
et double la pointe de l’aguille un poc et la fiche emmi l’ungle, et la perce a tout l’aguille, et lie l’ungle d’un fil et l’estent au desus, et escorche a tout lou poil le costeit de l’ungle qui enseut la prunele et la soie au poil jusc’au chief, puis cope lou remanant en la racine dou larmier a tout lou spatumile subtil et as petites forces, et laisse la char natureil ou larmier, si que par l’incision ne veigne li cors des larmes acostumeement;	and bend the tip of the needle slightly and insert it into your nail with the hair-side facing the underside of the nail. Pierce all the way through the nail with the needle, tie off the needle from one side of the nail to the other with thread, stretch it above [the incision], pluck out every hair on either side of the nail that might touch the eyelid or lash and the surrounding area, then cut away what remains at the root of the tear duct with a very sharp knife and small forceps. Leave the natural flesh around the tear duct intact so that bodily fluids may still flow as usual through the incision;
et aucune fois s’estent li ungle a l’oncine soulement, et au fil, si com nos avons dit;	and sometimes they extend to the nail bed with just the file or needle as we have said.
puis l’escorche on a tout le spatumile souef de coi ci est li forme:	then scrape away all of the skin until you reach the patella, which is shaped like this:
Et garde que li spatumile ne touche la toile charnue et la rompe, et que li prunele ne soit percie;	And be careful not to touch or tear the fleshy membrane with the patella, and ensure that the cartilage is not pierced.
et aprés l’incision giete en l’oil un poc de seil broiet, et dou coliere fait de litargire, et le laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	After the incision, apply a pinch of ground silk into the eye and make a collar from litharge. Leave it on until the next day.
puis le cure de ceu qu’il i covient tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat him for whatever he needs until he is healed.
Et se li ungle n’est mie nervouse, et tu ne pues bouter l’aguille, et li uncines n’i puet entrer, maintes fois est curee ceste semblance d’ungle de medicines;	And if the nail is not nervous and you cannot insert the needle, and the file cannot enter, often this type of condition is treated with medicine.
et naissent sicom j’ai conteit en la division, et se tu la vues coper, si oevre l’oil dou malaide, et pren le spatumile legier poc agut selonc ceste forme:	and are born as I have described in the division, and if you see it cut, operate on the patient's eye, and take a light spatula with a sharp edge according to this form:
Et reis l’ungle desus subtilment, et se tu vois qu’elle amenuise point et li rasion i apresse, si distille de ta bouche en l’oil coliere fait de litargire et dou coliere rouge et seil broiet, et estoupe l’oil jusc’a l’autre jor;	And lift the eyelid gently, and if you see that it does not diminish and the reason for this is urgent, then pour into the eye a collar made of litharge and red lead powder, both ground with salt, and pack the eye until the next day;
puis rencomence l’autre ovraige selonc ceste meisme oevre, tant qu’elle soit toute ostee.	then resume the other procedure according to this same method until it is all removed.
Se aucune chose ne t’est contraire en l’oil, si com aposteme chaus, adonques la lait, et cure premier l’aposteme chaut tant qu’il soit sanez, puis rencomence l’ovraige si com devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If nothing opposes you in the eye, like a warm abscess, then lance it, and treat first the hot abscess until it is healed, then resume the work as before, until it is healed.
Et se li apparance de la chair dou larmier nuit en l’oil par grant nuisement, si la sospent a l’oncine, et en cope une partie et non mie tot, que cors de larmes n’i viegne;	And if the appearance of the flesh in the eyelid harms the eye severely, then suspend it with an unguis, and cut away a portion but not all, so that no corpus of tears comes out;
puis distille en l’oil coliere rouge qui est fais de litargire.	Then instill red collar ointment into the eye, which is made of litharge.
de la char qui naist sus la prunelle	Of the flesh that grows on the cornea.
Es eulz d’aucuns homes naist aucune fois char rouge, et cuevre la prunele et restraint sus les papieres et les torne au defuer, et semble une rose de balauste;	Some men's eyes are born with a red spot, which covers the pupil and extends onto the sclera, resembling a red rose petal.
et li ovraiges si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, puis li oevre les eulz, et coil toute celle char as uncines convenaubles a ceu, et la sostien a la force;	And the work is that the patient should place their head on your hand, then you open the eyes and turn all of this flesh with suitable hooks and hold it firmly.
puis cope la premiere char, et vai tout copant au raseur jusc’a la fin, et te garde que tu ne bleces l’oil a l’ovraige;	Then cut the first flesh, and continue cutting with a razor until you reach the end, being careful not to injure the eye in your work.
et soit li incision dou spatumile que nos avons dit en l’incision de l’ungle et as petites forces de coi on oste lou sebel, si com li forme aprés cest chapistre lou demostre;	And let the incision be made with the spatula we mentioned when cutting the nail and using small forceps to remove it, as illustrated in this chapter.
et quant li incision est acomplie et ostee toute li char, si emple l’oil de seil broiet ou tu i distille coliere rouge et semblans medicines corrosives, et met sus l’oil defuer coton avec abin d’uef, si qu’il soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut;	When the incision is complete and all the flesh is removed, apply ground linseed oil or distill red collarwort and similar corrosive medicines onto it. Place cotton wool mixed with egg white over the eye to ensure the hot abscess is secured.
et s’il i demore rien, et li sans chaus te sormonte, et tu doutes aposteme chaut, si laisse l’oil et cure l’aposteme de choses apaisant aposteme chaut;	If nothing remains, and hot blood rises to the surface, and you suspect a hot abscess, leave the eye alone and treat the abscess with soothing medications for hot abscesses.
puis revien a ton ovraige tant qu’il soit sanez, et ensi fai cant chars est ajostee en l’oil par ceste semblance.	Then return to your work once it is healed, and thus do likewise when flesh has adjusted in the eye through this process.
Mais toutevoie il covient que tu aliges la cure de chescun oil foible de la voie natureil;	However, it is necessary that you alleviate the treatment for each weak eye through natural methods;
et de la voie accident, en ovraige de fer;	and accidental injury with iron instruments;
et ne bouter mie ta main en aucun de ces ovraiges tant que tu voies que cist membres soit soffrans celui ovraige.	nor should you insert your hand into any of these procedures until you see that this limb is tolerant to the operation.
des voines des eulz	eyelid veins
Sebel sont voinnes rouges que sont covertes sus l’oil, et tolent a la veue son ovraige et afoiblissent l’oil toz jors.	Beneath the eyelids are red veins that cover the eye, obstructing its function and weakening vision over time.
Mestier est donques au premier que tu regardes se li oil, en coi sebel est, est fors, et n’i a autre maladie fuers que lou sebel;	It is necessary for you to first examine the eye in which the injury appears, whether it is sound or not and has no other disease except that of soundness.
adonques le coil en teil maniere:	then treat it as follows:
comande au malaide qu’il mette son chief en ton sain, puis sospent celles voines a tout l’oncine selonc sa sapience, et soit li oncines subtilz double selonc ceste forme:	instruct the patient to lay their head in your lap, and then bind those veins as much as is appropriate according to your knowledge; let the binding be twice as strong on these parts.
Et soient dui oncine par degrez en I cors selonc ceste forme:	And let there be two ounces by degrees in I body according to this form:
puis c’on coil as forces celles voinnes subtilment, et essue lou sanc houre aprés autre, tant que tu voies removoir celles voines fuers de l’oil;	then treat the areas around those veins with force, wiping away blood after an hour until you see a removal of the soundness from the eye.
et garde que tu ne blecier l’oil as pointes des spatumiles, et fai cest ovraige a houre de midi devant lou soleil, et soies mout fervans en ton ovraige si que tu ne copes fuer que celles voinnes;	And make sure you do not injure the eye with the points of spatules, and perform this work at noon in front of the sun, being very diligent in your task so that you only cut those veins.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si distille en l’oil coliere vert et rouge por corrumpre ceu qui est demorez dou sebel.	And when you have done this, then distill into the eye green and red collirio to corrupt that which remains of the humors.
Et se tu n’as pooir de coillir tout ceu en celle houre, si fai emplastre sus l’oil de choses apaisans la dolor des eulz, et le laisse aucuns jors tant que li dolors soit apaisie et soit asseurez d’aposteme chaut, puis rencomence selonc ceste maniere qui est devant tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if you cannot collect all of these things at that hour, then make a plaster over the eye with soothing substances to alleviate the pain, and leave it there for some days until the pain is soothed and you are certain of warm abscesses, then begin again according to this method until it is healed.
et c’est li forme des forces:	And this is the form of treatment:
de la fistule de l’oil	Of the eye fistula
Li mire si nomment «arissati» fistule:	The physician named it "arrissati" a fistula:
quant tu la cures per cautere et par medicine ague ardant selonc ceu que j’ai devant dit, et elle n’est mie sanee, si est engien en li que tu fendes sus l’aposteme, lai ou il doit meurer, et trai toute la moistor que i est, tant que li os soit descovers.	when you treat it with cauterization and medicine for a burning abscess as I have mentioned before, and it is not healed, if there is puss inside that you must cut above the abscess, where it should die, and remove all moisture until the bone is exposed.
Et quant li os iert descovers, et tu verras la corruption et la noiror, si la reis a tout l’estrument de coi ci est li forme;	And when the bone is exposed, and you see the decay and blackness, take all the instruments that are shaped like this one;
et est apelez «aspre chief», et soit fait de feir inde a I chief reont, et soit pointoiez si com une lime si com il est en la presente forme:	and it is called an "aspre chief", and should be made of iron with a point at one end, and sharpened like a file as shown in the present illustration;
Et met sus lou leu de l’os corrumput, puis le torne entre tes dois, et presse ta main un poc tant que tu saiches que celle corruption est rese;	And place it on the location of the corrupted bone, then turn it between your two fingers and press with your hand a little until you feel that the decay has been removed;
et fai ceu aucune fois, puis restoure lou leu de medicines exiccatives.	and do this sometimes, then restore the place with drying medications.
se li leus est soudez, et char i naist, et li cors de la bowe est soudez, et remaint ensi XL jors, et il ne renovele et n’est mie apostemez, et accidens mavais n’i vient, saiches qu’il est sanez;	if the place is welded together, and scar tissue forms there, and the body of the wound is joined, and remains so for forty days without reopening or becoming infected, and no ill accidents happen, then know that it has healed.
se ceu non, si n’i a autre engien que de ramener la fistule au pertus dou neif selonc ceste forme:	but if not, there is another procedure to draw the fistula back through the navel hole according to this method:
et est que tu descuevre de l’os la seconde fois par fer, et par medicines agues, et quant il iert descovers si prent I foret selonc ceste forme, et soit li chiés de fer a III angles, et li fust soit atenuis jusc’a chief si com tu vois ci:	and that you uncover the bone again with iron instruments and sharp medicines. When it is uncovered thus take one drill according to this form where the head of the iron has three angles, and the shaft tapers down to a point as you see here:
puis le met sus l’os delez lou larmier, et esloigne ta main de l’oil I poc, puis torne a tot le foret tant qu’il perce l’os et le sent li malaides par ceu que li vens en ist s’il tient sa main sus son neif;	Then place it above the bone near the armpit, and move your hand away from their eye one inch. Then turn with all of the auger until it pierces the bone, feeling the patient as you do so because wind will go inside them if they keep their hand on their knee;
et pues restoure lou leu de medicines seches, si com je t’ai ensigniet, et quant li char naist et endurcist li leus, si vait li matiere au neif;	And then restore the place with dry medicine as I have taught you. And when the flesh rises and hardens the places, so does the matter come to the knee;
si est plus legiere chose au malaide.	It is something lighter for the patient.
de l’issue de l’oil	From the exit of the eye
Quant li eulz apert fuer dou tout en tout, et il ne vient point de destorbier au nef, ne amenuisement, si covient que tu lies lou malaide;	When the eye opens fully without any disturbance to the kidney or weakening, then you must bind the patient.
puis le saine, puis li met ventouses ou haterel sens ferir por succier, puis met sus l’oil I liien fait d’acaice et de aloe et d’encens et de sarcocolle, et puis estrain l’oil, et l’emplaustre sus de bendes et de drapelz;	Then cleanse it, then apply cupping without iron to suck, then put on the eye I a poultice made of acacia and aloe and incense and saraccolle. Then bind up the eye with plasters on bandages and cloth.
et li maniere des drapelz si est que tu preignes drapelz assez molz, et double chescun en IIII, et puis met l’un sus l’autre selonc la quantiteit que li eulz en ait mestier;	and the manner of the dressings is such that you take soft enough cloths, and fold each into four, then place one on top of the other according to the quantity that the eyes need.
puis l’estrain par desus d’un bendeil dur forment, et rencomence les ventouses por succier sens ferir;	then strain it above with a hard bandage, and repeat the cups to suck without wounding;
puis oste les ventouses et laisse l’oil estraint jor et nuit, et se li liiens amolist, si covient que tu l’estraignes mout;	then remove the cups and leave the eye strained day and night, and if the bandage loosens, you must tighten it greatly.
puis oste lou liien aprés le jor et la nut, et se tu vois l’oil repairier, c’est boin;	then remove the bandage after the day and night, and if you see the eye improving, it is good.
se ce non;	if not;
si rencomence l’emplaustre et les drapelz et lou liien et les ventouses tant qu’il soit sanez.	If it starts again, apply the poultice, the dressings, the bandage, and the cups until it is healed.
dou derrompement de toile uvee	Of tearing of tough membrane
Quant disruptions vient en la toile uvee, puis apert, et vient fuer des papieres si com I grain de resins, et est espoantauble a veoir;	When ruptures occur in the black membrane, it then opens up, and comes out like paper-thin pieces resembling grains of resin, and is terrible to behold;
adonques se tu la vues coper, li ovraiges est telz que tu boutes une aguille en la racine des la partie desoz jusc’a celi desus, puis boute une autre aguille ou il ait I fil double des la partie dou larmier;	then if you see it cut, the procedure is such that you insert a needle into the root of the lower part until reaching the upper part, then insert another needle where there is a double thread of the arm;
et la fai percier, et laisse la premiere aguille selonc la disposition;	and make it pierce through, leaving the first needle in place according to its position;
puis cope lou leu dou fil double et lie une partie de l’uve entor, et l’estraint bien, puis estrai l’aguille et met sus l’oil lainne moillie en abun d’uef;	then cut the place of the double thread and tie a part of the membrane around it, securing it tightly, then remove the needle and apply wet linen moistened with egg white;
et le laisse tant que li filz chiece avec l’uve, puis cure l’oil de choses confortans tant que li plaie soit sanee;	And let it remain until the son of a dog whelps with its litter, then treat the eye with comforting things until the wound is healed.
et aucune fois li plaie est restrainte par l’uve chescune part d’un cercle de drap, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And sometimes the wound is covered with an egg on all sides by a circle of cloth until it is healed.
Et se li eulz done grant apparance, si le perce au spatumile subtil qui viegne em parfont de l’oil, et corre la moistor albuginé et dessende li eulz, et entre ens tantost;	And if the eye gives great appearance of trouble, pierce it with a subtle spatule that comes out through the eye, and remove the white moisture, lowering the eye immediately;
puis l’estrai tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then extract it until it is healed.
de la bowe de l’oil	of the eye's bowels
Ceste maladie qui est apelee «alcunnati» nen est fuers que bowe qui est assemblee en l’oil, semblant a aigue dessendant, et ce n’est mie aigue;	This disease which is called 'alcunnati' is nothing but the bowels that are assembled in the eye, appearing as descending water, but it is not water.
et li maniere de l’apparance de l’ovraige si est que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege appareilliet et droit, puis prent le chief entre tes mains de II pars, et lou muef tant que tu voies la bowe venir au desus a tes eulz;	and the way of appearance for this work is that you make the patient sit on an equipped and straight chair, then take their head between your two hands, and move it until you see the bow coming above your eyes;
puis soit ens fichie, et ne dessende et soit descombree li lumiere, et voie li malaides les choses si com il soloit;	then be careful, and do not lower or cover the light, and let the patient see things as they usually would;
et s’elle ne dessent desoz, saiches que c’est aigue, et se li dessendemens de la bowe n’est appareilliez si com nos avons dit.	and if it does not descend downwards, know that it is acute, and if the bending movement is not equipped as we have said.
si fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, puis prent le spatumile subtil et fent sus la toile cornee I poc par la continuation de la conjunctive avec la toile cornee et la corone, tant que li bowe isse;	make the patient sit between your hands, then take a thin spatula and make an incision on the corneal tissue with one stroke along the line of the conjunctiva to the corneal tissue and the cornea until the bow is exposed.
et quant elle ert issue, si distille en l’oil aigue chaude mellee a miel, ou aigue ou fenugreic est boillis et miel, puis soit curee d’autre cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	and when it has come out, instill warm water mixed with honey into the eye, or water boiled with fennel and honey, then treat it further until it is healed.
des aigues de l’oil	Eye waters
Nos avons jai les semblances des aigues en la division, et ceu qu’il covient por percier;	We have seen the likenesses of waters in their divisions, and what is required to pierce them;
si en oevre selonc la santeit.	so act according to what is healthy.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains croisiet, fuers de la lumiere por le soleil, et li lie l’oil sain et estreint mout fort;	You must make the patient sit between your crossed hands, away from light so that the sun does not shine in their eye, and bind their healthy eye tightly shut.
puis met la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre se li eulz est senestres, ou a ta main destre se li eulz est destres;	Then place the paper from your left hand to their eye if it is their left eye that is affected, or from your right hand if it is their right eye.
puis prent en ta main destre, se li eulz est senestres, l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda», ou a ta main senestre, se li eulz est destre;	Then take into your right hand, if the eye is left-sided, the instrument called "almagda," or in your left hand, if the eye is right-sided;
puis met la pointe de l’estrument delez la corone par la groissece d’un rait en celle blenchor de l’oil a la partie dou menor larmier, puis boute l’estrument qui est apelez «almagda» vertuousement, et trestorne ta main tant qu’il perce en la blenchor de l’oil, et sente que almagda viegne a la chose vuide;	Then place the tip of the instrument near the cornea in alignment with the thickness of a line on that white part of the eye towards the lower tear duct, then push the instrument called "almagda" skillfully, and turn your hand so it pierces into the white of the eye, feeling as if "almagda" comes to an empty space.
et covient que li mesure de la voie almagda soit au parfont de la mesure des l’espaice qui est des la prunele jusc’a la fin de la noirour;	And it is necessary that the path of "almagda" be exactly equal to the space from the pupil to the end of the black part.
et c’est li corone de l’oil;	and this is the crown of the eye;
si verras l’os en celle papiere por la clarteit de la toile cornee, et pues met l’estrument jusc’a leu ou li aigue est, puis l’espresse desoz une voie aprés autre.	you will see the bone in that paper due to the clarity of the cornea, and you may put the instrument until it reaches where the water is, then express it underneath one voice after another.
se li aigue dessent maintenant, si voit li malaides devant lui et l’estrument en son oil.	If the swelling subsides now, the patient sees it before them and the instrument in their eye.
Aprés repose I petit, et se li aigue remonte la seconde voie, met la fuer avec l’estrument, et quant elle est ens fichie et ele ne monte, si estrai almagda legierement en tornoiant ta main poc et poc;	after put it back in place gently, and if the water rises again through the second path, apply force with the instrument until it is fixed and no longer moves upwards, then slowly extract the almogda by turning your hand to and fro;
et puis remette en aigue un poc de seil gemme, et leive de ceu l’oil dedens.	then put some salt gem water into it again, and remove this from the eye inside.
Puis met par defuer l’oil estoupes ou lainne moillie en oile roset et en abun d’uef, et lie avec l’oil sain.	Then apply to the eye dressings or moist wool in rose oil and egg white, binding it with a healthy eye.
Nos, et cil qui sont de nostre tens, mettons sus comin broiet avec abun d’uef.	We, and those of our time, apply ground cumin with plenty of egg white on top.
Et se almagda n’i puet entrer en l’oil par sa duresce, car il i a de teilz homes qui ont trop durs les eulz, si covient que tu preignes l’estrument qui est apelez «alberit», de coi ci est li forme:	And if the almagda cannot enter the eye due to its hardness, as there are some men with very hard eyes, then you must take the instrument called 'alberit', of which this is the shape:
Et perce donques la conjunctive soulement, et n’aler mie trop em parfont, mais fai I leu subtil, puis i boute almagda, si com nos avons dit;	and then pierce the conjunctiva alone, do not go too deep but make it subtle, and then insert the almogda as we have said;
et au complissement de l’uevre appareille au malaide I dorteur avenant, en coi il dorme sus son dos en I leu tenebrous;	And upon completion of the work, prepare for the patient a comfortable bed where they may lie on their back in a dark place;
et soit deveez de toz movemens, et preigne legieres viandes, et ne mueve son chief ne a destre ne a senestre, et soit liiez selonc sa disposition jusc’a tier jor;	Be free from all movement, eat light foods, do not move your head either to the right or left, and remain bound according to their condition for three days;
puis le deslie en cele maison meisme tenebrouse, et esprueve sa veue, et lou fai veoir aucunes choses, et puis li remet lou lien jusc’a septime jor;	Then unbind them in the same dark room, test their vision, and make them look at certain things. Afterwards, rebind them until the seventh day;
et ne covient mie que tu faices ceu en l’oure de la cure ou aprés l’incision maintenant, mais il covient que tu aliges ceu, por ceu que li aigue monte hastanment.	And you must not do this during or after the incision of the wound right now, for it is necessary to keep them calm due to the quick rising of fluid.
se apostemes chaus vient, que tu desliies l’oil devant le septime jor, et l’adrece de ceu qui assouaige aposteme;	If an abscess becomes hot, you must open it before seven days have passed, and treat it with a remedy for abscesses.
et quant il est apaisiez, si deslie la veue et met sus sa faice I orilliet por covrir aucun jor, et soit adés en celle maison tenebrouse.	And when it has calmed down, you must open the eyelid and apply a small bandage to cover it for one day, and remain in that dark room afterward.
Et puis isse de la maison poc et poc, et se convertisse en ses cas;	Then go out of the house often and often, and convert into those cases.
et saiches que nulz deciples ne se doit entremettre en cest cas.	And you should know that no disciple should interfere in these matters.
Et uns vint a nos qui estoit de la Yrach, qui nos dist que en som pais faisoit om almagda perciet, a coi on succe l’aigue, mais toutevoie je n’en vis onques nul en nostre terre, ne je ne lou lis onques en livres des anciens;	And there came to us someone from Iraq, who told us that in his country they make pierced amulets for which water is extracted, but I have never seen any such thing in our land, nor have I ever read about it in the books of the ancients.
et par aventure c’est une novele chose.	And perhaps it is a new thing.
Et ce sont les semblances des formes de almagda, por ceu que cil qui ne les conoit les voie;	And these are the appearances of the forms of almagda, for those who do not know them will see them;
et soient d’arain proprement:	and they are properly made of brass:
Et soient li chief d’aus de ceste meisme subtiliteit, et li derriene en III angles ague.	And the top part of this should also be made from the same subtle material, while the bottom end is three-sided in shape.
de la char sor le neis	From the flesh above the nose.
Aucune fois naissent ou neis chars ajostees diverses, de coi il i a aucunes qui semblent scorpions a mout de piez;	Sometimes there arise joined together various cars, of which some appear as scorpions with many feet;
et si i a de telz ou il ait char enchancree de fuxe color, et si a char souef de bone color.	And if there are such ones with chariot embellished by swift colours, and if it has soft body of good colour.
En celle donques de ces chars qui est souef, et ne mie enchancree, covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains encontre lou soleil;	In this one then of these chariots which is soft, and not embellished, you must make the patient sit between your hands facing the sun;
et oevre ses narines, et giete l’oncine a celles chars, et les trai fuers;	and work his nostrils, and apply the unguent to those parts, and treat them forcibly.
pues cope ceu que tu em pues sostenir au spatumile subtil agut d’une part, tant que tu saiches que celle char est toute ostee.	hold what you can support with the fine-pointed spatula from one side, so that you know this flesh is entirely removed.
Et s’il en remaint aucune chose c’on ne puisse coper, si l’ovrez a tout I des estrumens subtil legierement, si qu’il n’i demoure rien;	And if there remains anything that cannot be cut, open it with all the subtle instruments lightly, so that nothing is left.
et se sans te sormonte, ou aposteme chaus, si lou secort si com il covient;	and if it overwhelms you without warning, with an abscess so fierce, then cauterize it as is necessary.
et se c’est apostemes malignes, si te haste et lou cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez et soient ostees toutes les chars, puis giete ou neis aisil et aigue ou vin.	and if they are malignant abscesses, hasten and cauterize them until the blood is extinguished and all flesh is removed, then apply very fresh and sharp wine.
Se li neis oevre, et moistors en vient jusc’a palais, saiches qu’il est sanez;	If it does not work, and moisture reaches up to the palate, know that it is healed.
et se moistors ne perce si com il covient, saiches qu’il i a char nee en l’os desus, a coi li estrumens ne vient mie por taillier:	And if the moisture does not perforate as it should, know that there is cartilage in the bone above, to which the instruments do not reach for cutting.
adonques covient il que tu i boutes I fil de lin un poc gros, et soit noez de mains nous, et ait entre chescun nout d’espaice I doit ou moins;	Then you must insert a piece of flax thread slightly thicker than usual, knotted by hand, with about one finger's width between each knot.
et mette li malaides lou chiés dou fil en son neif a som pooir, et traie en odorant tant qu’il viegne par lou neif dedens la bouche;	Have the patient grasp the end of the thread in their fist and pull it with all their might until it comes out through the nostril into the mouth.
et maintes fois font ensi li enfant as escoles, et c’est legiere chose a celui qui le vuet faire;	Children at school often do this, and it is an easy thing for those who wish to try it.
puis tien le chief qui vient par lou neif a une main, et l’autre chief qui vient par la bouche a l’autre main, et saiche l’un aprés l’autre en soiant as nous qui sont ou fil.	Then hold the head that comes out through the nose with one hand, and the other head that comes out through the mouth with the other hand, and pull each after the other being careful not to damage the cord.
Fai ceu tant que tu saiches que li nout ont corrompue celle char, puis trai lou filz, essue le sanc, et moille lou fil en oignement egiptien, et le remet derechief au neis si com devant;	Do this so that you know the night has corrupted that flesh, then draw out the child, wipe away the blood, and wet the cord with Egyptian ointment, and return it to the nose as before.
fai ceu III jors ou plus, tant que li oignemens corrode tout ceu qui est demorez de char;	Do this for three days or more, until the ointments have completely eroded all that remains of the flesh;
et puis met ou neis une caine de plonc aucuns jors tant qu’il soit sanez, et s’il a mestier de medicines sechans, si en use;	Then place in the nose a plug of flax for some days until it is healed, and if necessary, use drying medications.
et c’est li forme de l’estrument por purgier lou chief, a coi on distille les oiles et les medicines ou neis:	And this is the form of the instrument to purge the head, for which oils and medicines are distilled into the nose.
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, semblant a une lampe overte, si com une cainne, et li conduis ausi;	And it is made of silver or copper, resembling an open lamp, just like a tube, and it leads in the same way.
et se tu vues, si fai une cainne close, et soit li estrumens plains por espurgier lou chief;	and if you see, make a closed tube, and let the instrument be full to purge the head;
et ait I mainche au chief por lou tenir quant on chaufe l’oile ou aucune liquor.	and have one handle at the head to hold it when heating oil or any liquid.
de la char sor le neis	From the flesh above the nose.
Maintes fois naist au chief dou neis une maladie qui est apelee «telul», et croist et devient grans adés, tant qu’il est vis chose au regarder;	Many times there arises in the head of the nose an illness which is called 'telul', and it grows and becomes large afterwards, to such a degree that it is an ugly sight to behold;
