et por ceu covient que tu lou copes au comencement, et l’oste tout fuer, puis met sor leu lou cautere ou la medicine ardant;	and for this you must cut it at the beginning, and remove all flesh, then place a hot cautery or burning medicine on it.
et s’on le tarde a coper tant qu’il soit grans, si pren warde s’il est durs, de fuxe color, de povre sens:	and if you delay cutting it until it becomes large, take note if it is hard, of dark colour, and lacks feeling.
si ne lou touchier mie de fer car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, car quant on le cope aucune fois, si en vient grant malice au malaide;	do not touch it with iron, for it is an aggravated abscess, because when you cut it once, great harm comes to the patient.
et se li apostemes est de soef touchement, non mie de fuxe color, et tu vois c’on le puisse tout coper, si vuide le malaide et lou cope sens paor, et cure le leu de choses sechans et restraignans.	and if the abscess is soft to the touch, not dark in colour, and you see that it can be completely cut away, then evacuate the patient and cut it without fear, and treat the area with drying and constricting substances.
quant li neis est copez et cosus	when the nose is cut and sewn
Saiches que quant solutions de continuation vient en une de ces cartillagines ovraiges, i profite poc, fuer que en aucuns homes.	Know that when bone-joint treatments come to one of these cartilage works, it profits little, except in some men.
Il covient donques cant ceu avient a aucun, si regarde se li plaie est fresche a tout son sanc;	It is necessary then, when this happens to anyone, to consider if the wound is fresh with all its blood.
et adonques ajoste les II levres a une costure, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	And then align the two lips [of the wound] for suturing, then treat it until it is healed.
et se les levres sont ja desevrees d’une part et d’autre, si covient que tu escorches toutes les parties de lor keur tant qu’elles sainent, puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et l’estraint, et poudre sus poudre de sanc de dragon, et encens broiet;	And if the lips [of the wound] are already separated on both sides, it is necessary that you excise all parts of their core until they bleed, then bring together the two lips for suturing, and compress them, apply a powder composed of dragon's blood and powdered incense.
et met sus les poudres une piece d’emplaustre de fort ou d’autre emplaustre soudant, et le laisse tant qu’il chiece par lui, puis le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Place a piece of strong plaster or another adhesive poultice on top of the powders and leave it until it sticks by itself, then treat it with ointment until it is healed.
Li maniere de la costure si est que tu assembles la solution:	The way of sewing (a wound) is such that you bring together the edges.
ou par aguilles, si com nos avons dit en la costure dou ventre;	or with needles, as we have said in the sewing of the belly (wound).
ou par fil, si com je le t’ai fait savoir.	or by thread, as I have made you aware.
des apostemes des levres	From abscesses of the lips
A mains homes avient dedens les levres aposteme dur, semblans a grains de veces, et menor et plus grant;	Within the lips, abscesses form by hand, resembling small grains or bumps of various sizes.
adonques couvient que tu tornes les levres, et fendes sus chescun nout, et le prent as pinceures et le cope en chescune partie;	Then it is necessary to turn back the lips of the wound, incise each boil or bump, grasp them with forceps and squeeze out their contents.
puis emple lou leu aprés l’incision de vitriole broiet, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	Next apply ground glass or fine powder after the incision to stop any bleeding that may occur.
et puis lou leive d’aisil, et cure lou leu de choses seches tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then leave it easily, and treat the area with dry things until it is healed.
de la char des gencives	The flesh of the gums
Maintes fois naist sus les gencives char ajostee, que li ancien apelent «albulus»;	Often there appears on the gums hardened matter that the ancients call "albulus";
si covient que tu la sostienes as tenailles, et la cope a sa racine, et laisse corre la bowe ou le sanc;	So it is necessary to hold it with tongs, cut it at its root, and let the bowel or blood flow out.
puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet, ou autres poudres restraignans et desiccatives;	Then put on the area ground vitriol or other restraining and drying powders.
et se celle char revient aprés l’incision, et maintes fois avient, si la cope la seconde fois, et la cauterize:	And if that matter returns after the incision, which often happens, cut it a second time and cauterize it.
si ne revient mie aprés le cautere;	If it does not return after the cautery.
et ce sont les formes des estrumens por coper.	And these are the forms of instruments for cutting.
des sordens	of wounds
Aucunes fois sont assemblees au chief des dens, dedens la bouche entre les gencives, escorces qui sont laides et aspres;	Sometimes hard and rough shells are gathered in the head of teeth within the mouth between gums, which is unsightly.
et aucune fois sont li dent noir et citrin et vers, tant que li corruption vient a la gencive, et sont li dent puant;	And sometimes the teeth become black and yellow and green until decay reaches the gums, making them foul-smelling.
si covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide entre tes mains, et ses chiés soit en ton saint, et reis les dens ou les escorces aperent, tant qu’il n’i demore rien;	You should make the patient sit between your hands with their head in yours and extract the teeth or shells that appear until there is nothing left.
et ensi fai de la noiror et de la verdor, et de la jaunice et des autres taiches, tant qu’elles soient mondees;	And thus do the same for blackness, greenness, yellowness, and other stains until they are cleaned.
et s’on oste ceu que i est a la premiere rasion, c’est boin;	And if you remove that which is at the root cause, it is good.
se ceu non, si rencomence a rere le secont jor et lou tier, tant que tu aies tout reis;	If not, start again from the beginning on the second day and the third, until you have everything back in place;
et saiches que li dent ont mestier de diverses formes d’estrumens por reire, selonc ceu que li oevre lou demoustre, por ceu que li raseur dont on reit defuer les dens ont autres formes que cil dont on reit entre les dens;	And know that teeth require various shapes of tools to remove, depending on what the work requires, as the rasp used to clean outside the teeth has a different shape than those used between the teeth;
et cestes formes et autres soient avec toi appareillies.	And these shapes and others should be prepared for you.
Il covient quant tu cures lou dent de sa dolor que tu tardes dou traire tant com tu pues, car ce ne doit om mie faire;	When treating tooth pain, one should delay extraction for as long as possible, as it should be avoided if at all possible.
car c’est une substance mout haute jusc’a donc c’on n’ait point d’excusation dou raier.	As it is very valuable, one should only extract teeth when there is no other option.
Adonques quant li malaides est constrains dou traire, si covient que tu soies certains dou dent doillant.	Then when the patient is compelled to extract (the tooth), you must be certain about which tooth is causing pain.
Maintes fois desoit li dolor lou malaide, et cuide qu’elle soit ou dent saint, et fait traire le boin dent;	Many times the pain deceives the patient, and they think it is in a healthy tooth, so they have the good tooth drawn.
et toutevoie ne se depart mie li dolor per ceu, tant que li malvais estrais, car nos l’avons ja veut faire a ces sainors;	and yet the pain does not leave them for this reason, as the bad tooth remains, for we have already seen it in these people.
et quant tu es bien certains dou dent doillant, si covient que tu escorches entor lou dent a tout i. spatumile fort por warder la gencive de toutes pars;	and when you are certain which tooth is causing pain, it is necessary to scrape all around the tooth with a spatula. Use force to protect the gums from all sides.
puis le mues a tes dois ou as tenailles subtilz au premier poc et poc, tant qu’il soit bien eslochiés, puis i afferme bien les tenailles;	then loosen it with your fingers or the delicate pincers with gentle pricks and pricks until it is well loosened, then firmly close the pincers.
et soit li chiés dou malaide en ton saint entre tes genous, et lou tien bien si qu’il ne se mueve.	and let the patient's head be in your lap between your knees, holding it steady so that it does not move.
Aprés estrai lou dent droitement sens brisier, et s’il ne saut fuer, si prent aucun de ces estrumens et le boute dedens de chescune part legierement, et lou remuef si com tu as fait premier.	After extracting the tooth correctly without breaking it, and if it cannot be removed, then take one of these instruments and gently insert it into each side, moving it around like you did previously.
Et se li dens est perciez et mengiez, si covient que tu l’emplisses de drapelz, lai ou li pertus sont;	And if the tooth is pierced and worn down, you must fill it with threads where the holes are;
et si l’estraint subtilment as tenailles, que il ne brise a l’estraindre;	and if you carefully extract it with tongs, do not break when extracting it;
et covient mout saigement ovrer entor la gencive por deschaucier lou dent.	and one must work very diligently around the gum to dislodge the tooth.
Et te done bien en warde que tu ne le brises, et en remaigne une partie, et reveigne au malaide par la malice de la racine plus grans dolors de la premiere.	Be careful not to break it, leaving a piece behind, for then the patient will return with even greater pain from the root.
Et te warde que tu ne faices mie ensi com font li ignorant sainor, qui par lor haste et par lor hardiesce brisent aucune fois le charreit, et n’i amenistrent mie ceu que nos avons conteit;	And beware not to act like the ignorant surgeon who, due to their haste and boldness, sometimes breaks something in the jaw, and fails to treat what we have explained.
mais font venir aucune fois par l’oquison de ceu grant maladie por les racines que i demorent, ou por lou charreit qu’il brisent, si com nos avons sovent veut;	but they cause severe illness through the hole due to the roots that remain or the jaw that is broken, as we have often seen.
et quant li dens est trais, si lavez lou leu de vin ou d’aisil et de seil;	and when the tooth is drawn, wash the place with wine or vinegar and salt;
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, que sovent avient, si emple lou leu de vitriole broiet;	and if there is bleeding from the tooth, which often happens, pack the place with powdered green vitriol.
et se ceu ne vaut, si le cauterize.	and if that doesn't work, cauterize it.
Les formes des estrumens, a coi om muet les dens premier, soient a longes pointes et a gros mainches, qu’il ne doublent mie quant tu trairas le dent;	The shapes of the instruments, with which one moves teeth first, should have long points and thick handles so that they do not bend when you are drawing the tooth.
et ce sont les formes:	and these are their forms:
Et soient de gros membres si qu’il ne ploient mie au traire, et soient de fer inde bien fait, et soient dentez por mues tenir.	And they should have large handles so that they do not bend when you extract it, and they should be well-made iron with teeth to hold [the tooth].
de la racine des dens	From the root of the teeth.
Quant li racine demoure au traire, si covient que tu mettes sor le leu coton moilliet em burre I jor ou II, tant que li leus soit amolis, pues i boute les tenailles qui sont apelees «algefri», de coi li chiés semblet bec de soigne;	When the root remains when drawing [the tooth], you must place moist cotton mixed with butter on the site for one or two days until the tissue softens, then insert the tongs which are called "algefri", making the mouth resemble a bird's beak.
et soient dedens faites ausi com une lime et c’est li forme:	and let them be made inside as well like a file, which is its form.
Et se les racines ne vuellent issir a tout ces tenailles, si covient que tu descuevre la char tot entor la racine, et i met l’estrument qui est apelez «althali», c’est a savoir palainche, de coi ci est li forme:	And if the roots do not want to come out with these pincers, then you must uncover all the flesh around the root, and place there an instrument which is called 'althali', that is to say, a saw, of this form:
Et soit fors et gros si qu’il ne brise mie, et se li racine saut par ceu, c’est boin;	and let it be strong and thick so that it does not break, and if the root jumps because of this, it is good.
se ceu non, si t’aide de toz les estrumens, de coi les formes vienent ci aprés:	if not, help yourself with all the instruments, from which the shapes come hereafter:
Et si s’aide on de cest estrument qui ait II rains, de coi ci est li forme:	And if one helps with this instrument which has two edges, of which the form is thus:
et d’autres ferremens qui sont devant en la rasion des dens, et de cest estrument qui semble unes grans tenailles, dont ci est li forme:	and other iron instruments which are placed in front of the teeth, and of this instrument which resembles large pincers, of which the form is thus:
Et soit cist estrumens fors qu’il ne puisse brisier, et saiches que mout d’estrumens de dens sont;	and let this instrument be strong so that it cannot break, and know that there are many dental instruments.
et ausi d’autres estrumens, qui ne sont mie contez;	and also other instruments which are not listed here.
et li saiges maistres subtilz trueve par soi meisme son estrument, selonc ceu que ses ovraiges et li maladie li demoustre, car il i a de teilz maladies ou li ancien n’enseignerent point d’estrument por la diversiteit d’au;s et s’om brise point dou charreit ou des autres os, ou il porrit, si i cerche as estrumens qu’il i covient, que je t’ai dit, et t’aide des gestes, de coi ci est li forme:	and skilled master physicians find their own instruments by themselves according to what their work and the illness show them, because there are so many illnesses for which the ancients did not teach an instrument for its diversity of use; if a bone is broken or any other bones could be, look for the appropriate instruments I told you about, and help with gestures, this is how they are formed:
Et soient gros et bien tenant por tenir l’os, qu’il n’eschaipe, mais le puisse tenir et oster;	And [the bandages] are thick and hold well to keep the bone in place so that it doesn't slip out but can be held and removed.
et puis restoure lou leu de medicines convenant a ceu, et s’il ait en l’os porriture, et elle est petite, si la reis a tout cest estrument:	Then restore the place with medicine suitable for this purpose, and if there is any decay in the bone that is small, then use all these instruments:
Quant li dent apperent ne mie selonc lou cors natureil, et li forme est laide, et meismement en femmes puceles, si covient que tu saiches se li dens est neis aprés lou dent, et n’est mie en droit leu, et on ne lou puet soier ne limer:	When the tooth appears unlike natural teeth and its form is ugly, especially in young women, you must know if the tooth was born after other teeth, and it isn't in the right place; such a tooth cannot be treated or filed.
adonques lou raie;	Therefore remove it.
et s’il est aers avec lou dent, si prent cest estrument dont ci est li forme, et est semblans a I petit bec, et soit de fer inde agut en som:	And if it is hollow with the tooth still attached, take this instrument that has the form of a small sharp beak and is made of iron.
Et lou cope poc et poc em mains jors por la duresce dou dent, et por ceu que tu ne mueves les autres, et s’il est apparans c’on le puisse limer, si lou lime d’une teil lime com ci est li forme:	And strike it several times with a hammer for the hardness of the tooth, and so that you do not move other teeth. If it is apparent that it can be filed down, use this tool shaped like the one described here to file it:
et est ausi com li lime de coi on fait les aguilles;	And it is like a file from which needles are made;
et en lime lou dent poc et poc em mains jors legierement, si qu’il ne se mueve tant qu’il chiece;	And with the file we polish teeth gently from time to time, so that they do not move until they heal.
puis la plaine en la fin a tout aucun raseur, et se li dens est trop trenchans et il blece la lengue, si covient limer l’aspreteit tant qu’il soit igalz, si qu’il ne blece la lengue ne ne corrompe la parole.	Then the whole surface in the end to all raspers, and if the tooth is too sharp and it wounds the tongue, one must file its roughness until it is even so that it does not wound the tongue or corrupt speech.
quant li dent lochent	When teeth loosen
Quant li dent devant lochent, ou par percussion ou par cheoir, et li malaides ne puet presser sus ceu qu’il menjue qu’il ne chient, et tu les as curez de medicines restrignans, et ceu ne vaut;	When the front teeth are loose due to impact or a fall, and the patient cannot bite down on them without them falling out, and you have treated them with constrictive medicines, but it is not effective;
si les covient restraindre d’un fil d’or, car li filz d’argent devient vert et porrit, mais li ors ne se mue onques;	They must be secured with gold wire, for silver wire turns green and rots, but gold never changes.
et soit li filz moiens ne trop gros ne trop menus, selonc la quantiteit de l’espaice entre les dens;	and let the thread be neither too thick nor too thin, according to the size of the space between the teeth.
et se tu vues adrecier les dens, si pren lou fil et lou boute double entre les II dens sains, puis met les chiés entre les dens meus, s’il en i a I ou plusors, tant que tu veignes saigement jusc’au dent sain d’autre part;	and if you wish to straighten the teeth, take the thread and double it between two healthy teeth, then place the ends of the thread over the misplaced tooth or teeth so that you can pull it gently until it aligns with a healthy tooth on the other side.
puis rencomence la coverture jusc’a la partie ou tu encomensas, et estrains ta main subtilment et saigement, tant qu’il ne se mueve point;	then begin the process of covering it again up to the part where you started, and extract your hand gently and carefully so that nothing moves.
et soit ta lieeure a la racine dou dent si qu’il ne puist eschaper.	and let the thread be tied at the root of the tooth so it cannot escape.
Puis cope les chiés dou fil a unes tenailles, et les assemble, et les repont entre le dent sain, et le met ensi qu’il ne blece la lengue;	Then cut the ends of the thread with some small scissors, and gather them together, then place it back between the healthy teeth so that it does not hurt the tongue.
et puis le laisse ensi estroit tant com il puet demorer, et s’il deslie, ou li filz ront, si l’estraint d’un autre fil;	and then leave it tight as much as it can stay, and if it loosens, or the thread breaks, hold it with another thread;
si demorrait et servira ensi tout son tens, et c’est li forme des dens et li figure de l’adrecement des II dens sains, et des II meus, si com tu vois:	if it stays put and serves thus for its entire time, and this is the shape of teeth and the arrangement of two healthy teeth, and two misaligned ones, as you can see:
Et quant li dent chiet, si lou remet on en son leu, de fres en fres, si com nos avons dit;	And when the tooth falls out, it is placed back in its place, fresh after fresh, as we have said;
et ne s’en entremette mie qui n’est saiges et soffrans, et aucune fois fait on la forme d’un dent d’os de vaiche, et lou met on au leu ou li defaute est, et l’estraint on si com nos avons dit, et demore et sert ensi lonc tens.	and do not let anyone who is not skilled and careful get involved, and sometimes a tooth is made from cow bone, and it is placed in the spot where there is a missing one, and it is held as we have said, and it stays put and serves thus for a long time.
de coper lou liien de la lengue	to cut loose the tongue's bond
Aucune fois est cist liiens qui vient desoz la lengue ou naturez, que on naist ensi;	Sometimes this ligament comes from below the tongue naturally, which is how one is born.
ou par accident de plaie soudee;	or by an accidental wound that has healed over;
et li ovraiges est telz que tu oevre la bouche dou malaide, et ait sa teste en ton sain, et li lieve la lengue;	and the treatment is such that you open the mouth of the patient, and have their head in your hand, lifting the tongue;
puis cope lou liien nervous dou large, tant que li lengue soit desloie de son tenement, et se il i a duresce ou nout, et c’est de soudement de plaie, si i boute l’uncine et cope dou large celui liement;	then cut the nerve of the tongue, so that it is separated from its place, and if there is hardness or swelling, and it is due to a sudden wound, then insert a hook and cut widely into this ligament;
et garde que li fendure ne soit mie trop em parfont, por l’artere qui est desoz;	and be careful that the incision is not too deep, to avoid damaging the artery beneath;
et quant tu as fait, si leve le leu d’aigue rose et d’aisil, ou d’aigue froide, puis met desoz la lengue une tente de lin;	and when you have done this, lift the place with rosewater and oil, or cold water, then place a linen cloth underneath the tongue.
et la teigne li malaides chescune nuit, que li leus ne puisse soder.	and let the patient be bathed each night so that the wounds do not close up.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si met sor le leu vitriole broiet;	and if bleeding occurs, apply crushed vitriol onto the wound;
et se li sans te vaint, si le cauterize au cautere lentiginout, qui est boin a ceu;	and if blood loss persists, cauterize with the light-colored cautery, which is beneficial in such cases;
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez,	then treat it with another remedy until it is healed.
et se tu lou vois de fusse color ou noir ou dur, si que li malaides ne lou sent, si n’i touchier point, car c’est chancre;	and if you see it become discolored or turn black or hard, and the patient does not feel it, do not touch it, for it is cancer.
et s’il est declinans a blenchor, et il i a moistor, si i giete l’oncine, et lou fent d’un spatumile subtil, et lou delivre d’une part et d’autre;	And if it declines towards blanching, and there is moisture present, throw an ointment on it, make a slit with a small spatula, and release it from one side to the other.
et se li sans te vaint a ton ovraige, si met sus vitriole broiet tant qu’il soit estainchiez, puis revien a ton ovraige tant que tu traies tout fuer;	And if the blood rushes to your work, apply crushed vitriol until it stops, then return to your task and treat everything thoroughly.
puis leve lou leu d’aisil et de seil, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then lift the place with ease and silk, and treat it with other remedies until it is healed.
des apostemes de la gorge	From abscesses of the throat
Aucune fois vient dedens la gorge boces qui sont apelees «godath», et les apele on proprement les II amandres, et quant tu les cures, si com nos avons dit en la division, et elles ne sont sanees, si pren garde:	Sometimes lumps arise in the throat called "godaths", properly known as the two tonsils. When you treat them as we have said before, and they are not healed, take heed:
se c’est apostemes dur de petit sens et de fusse color, si ne lou touchier mie de fer.	If this abscess is hard with little sensation and a pale colour, do not touch it with iron.
Et s’il est rouges et li racine est grosse, si ne lou touchier mie de fer, ausi por lou decorrement de sanc;	And if it is red and the root is swollen, do not touch it with iron, also due to the discharge of blood;
mais lou laisse tant qu’il soit meur, et adonques tu lou partiras, ou il rompirait par soi;	But leave it until it is ripe, and then you will remove it, or it may break itself.
et s’il est de blainche color reont, et li racine est subtilz, si aies apareilliet l’estrument por coper, mais regarde premierement se li apostemes chalz repose et est apaisiez.	And if it is of white colour and the root is subtle, prepare the instrument to cut, but first check if the abscess rests warm and is calm.
Adonques fai seoir lou malaide devant lou soleil, et ses chiés soit en ton sain, et li oevre la bouche et lou preigne li serjans entre ses mains, et presse la lengue desoz a tout l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme;	Then have the patient sit facing the sun, with their head in your lap, and open their mouth while you hold the instrument between your hands, pressing the tongue down so that it is out of the way.
et soit d’argent ou d’arain subtil ausi com uns coutelz:	and let it be of silver or fine brass like a knife;
Cant tu presses la lengue a tout cest estrument, et tu vois l’aposteme, si pren l’oncine et lou fiche en l’amandre, et la trai fuer au desus plus que tu pues;	can you press the tongue with all these instruments, and when you see an abscess take the hook and insert it into the almond, then pull hard upwards as much as you can;
et trai aucune chose des toiles avec, puis la cope a l’estrument, de coi ci est li forme, que semble unes forces;	and pull out any matter with it from the wound, then cover the instrument with a cloth which is the same shape and looks like tongs;
et toutevoie li chief sont corbé, et l’un endroit l’autre, et sont molt agut, et est fait de fer inde ou d’andainne:	and however the head is bent, and one side to another, and it is very sharp, and made of iron or steel;
Et se tu n’as cest estrument present, si lou cope as tenailles, de coi ci est li forme:	And if you don't have this instrument ready, use the tongs instead, which are shaped like this:
Et soit trenchans d’une part, et d’autre part nom;	And be sharpened on one side, and left blunt on the other side;
et quant tu as copeit l’une des amandres, si cope l’autre selonc cele meisme maniere, et aprés l’incision gargarize li malaides aigue chaude, et aigue et aisil, et se decorremens de sanc avient, si gargarize li malaides aigue, ou escorces de pomes grenates soient cuites, ou fuelles de mirte, et semblans choses, tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	and when you have treated one almond, treat the other in the same manner, and after the incision gargle the patient with hot water, and water mixed with honey, and if there is bleeding, then gargle the patient with only water, or with boiled pomegranate rind, or myrtle leaves, and similar things, until the bleeding stops;
puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	then treat it until it is healed;
et aucune fois naissent en la gorge autres apostemes que les II amandres, si les cope donques ensi com les II amandres igament.	and sometimes other abscesses appear in the throat besides the two tonsils, so treat them just as you would the two tonsils equally.
Et je medicinai une femme d’un aposteme que li estoit neis dedens la gorge, c’est a savoir I aposteme de petit sens;	And I treated a woman for an abscess that had formed inside her throat, namely a small one;
et avoit jai bien pres close toute la gorge, si que li femme ne pooit expirer por le conduit qui estoit estoupez, et ne pooit ne mengier ne boivre, et fust morte s’elle demorast ensi I jor ou II.	and had almost completely closed her throat, so that the woman could not breathe through the blocked passageway, and she could neither eat nor drink, and would have died if she remained like that for one or two days.
Et li apostemes estoit jai si montez qu’il avoit fuer mis II rains par les II pertuis dou neis.	The abscess had risen so much that we had to insert two tubes through the two nostrils.
Je hastai donques tantost, et fichai en l’un I oncine, puis lou traï fuers, et en traï grant porcion de bowe;	I quickly rushed forward, and stuck an ounce-weighted arrow into one [of the stones], then drew it out, and a large portion of bowel came with it.
puis refis autreteil en l’autre pertus dou neis, et li ovrai la bouche et li pressai la lengue;	then I inserted [an arrow] again on the other side of the nose, then opened his mouth for him and pressed on his tongue.
aprés fichai l’oncine en ces apostemes, et en copai une partie, et n’en issit fuers que un poc de sanc;	after that I stuck the arrow-weighted [tool] into his abscesses, and cut a part of it away, but only a little blood flowed out.
et ensi fut destoupez li conduis de la gorge la femme, et comensa maintenant a boivre aigue et puis vin, et ne cessai de taillier de cel aposteme par lonc tens;	And so were the windpipes of her throat removed, and now she began to drink water and then wine, and did not stop cutting this abscess for a long time.
et li apostemes recroissoit adés, et remplissoit lou leu que je avoie vuidiet, tant qu’il refut mout gros;	And the abscess would return, filling the place I had emptied until it became very large again.
adonques je l’engignai et lou cauterizai dedens la gorge:	Then I instructed her and cauterized within the throat.
ensi demora sens croistre;	It remained without growing further.
et me partis de ces parties, et ne soi que Deus fist de li aprés moi.	And I left these areas, relying on God for what happened next.
de l’uve	Of the eye
Quant reume dessent a l’uve, et elle est enflee et elle est longe, si est apelee «perpendiculaire»;	When the kingdom descends into the grave, and it is swollen and elongated, it is called "perpendicular".
et s’elle est desoz grosse et reonde, si est apelee «uve».	And if it is below [the eye] and large and round, it is called a "bag".
Quant elle est curee si com nos avons dit en la division, et li cure ne profite mie, et tu vois que li chaus apostemes est apaisiez, et elle est subtilz, si covient que tu la copes;	When it is cured as we have said in the division, and the treatment does not benefit, and you see that the surrounding abscesses are calmed, and it is delicate, then you must cut it.
et celle qui est reonde assemblee et n’est mie longe;	and this one which is round, gathered [together], and not long;
et elle est sanguine ou de fusse color ou noire, si covient que tu eschues l’incision de li.	and it is bloody or of false colour or black, then you must avoid cutting into it.
Car il i a grant peril sus lou malaide.	For there is great danger to the patient.
Il covient donques, quant tu la vois, selonc la maniere que j’ai dit, de sa blenchor et de sa longesce, que tu faices seoir le malaide devant lou soleil, et li presse la lengue a l’estrument dont nos avons fait la remembrance ci devant;	Therefore, when you see it, according to the manner I have described, of its whiteness and length, you must make the patient sit facing the sun, and press their tongue with the instrument that we mentioned before.
puis fiche l’oncine en l’uve, et la trai desoz, et la cope a I des II estrumens que j’ai dit en l’incision des II amandres.	Then insert the lancet into the cavity, draw it downwards and cut with the first of the two instruments that I mentioned for incising the testicles.
Et covient que tu ne coper mie fuer que la superfluiteit qui est outre le termine natureil;	And you must not cut any flesh beyond what is superfluous outside the natural limits
car se tu en copes plus, si grieves a la voix, et a la parolle;	For if you cut more, it harms the voice and speech
et aprés l’incision, use de ceu que nos avons dit en l’incision des II amandres, et le cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And after the incision, follow what we have said about incising the testicles, and treat it until it is healed.
Et se li malaides a paor dou coper, si covient que tu i use d’engien a la cauterization de li sens paor.	And if the patient is afraid of cutting, then it is necessary to use an instrument for cauterization to alleviate their fear.
Et li maniere dou cautere si est aigue ague.	And the manner of the cautery is hot, very sharp, and penetrating.
Et est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain, et puis li presse la lengue a l’estrument que nos avons dit ou chapistre de cautere, et confis avec aigue vive chaus, si qu’elle ne soit mie trop espesse ne trop clere;	And the patient should place their head in your lap, then press their tongue with an instrument that we mentioned in the chapter on cauterization, moisten it with hot water, neither too thick nor too thin.
et en emple le chevement de cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme:	and apply this completion of the instrument to it; thus is its form:
Et ait ou chief une cheveure ou om met la medecine, si com li chevemens d’une cuillier, et met l’estrument a tout la medicine sus l’uve;	And place on the head some hair whereon one places the medicine, just like with the hairs of a spoon, and place this instrument over all the medicine onto the eye.
et li malaides soit gisans sus son costeit, si que li salive et li muscillaige corre de sa bouche de la medicine dedens, si qu’ele ne dessende a la gorge, et lou blece;	and let the patient lie on their side so that saliva and mucus flow from their mouth with the medicine within it, lest it descend into the throat, damaging him.
puis tien ta main a tout la medicine et la presse sus l’uve, la quantiteit de la moitiet d’une houre, tant que tu la vois nercie et li mordications de la medicine soit apaisie;	then hold your hand over all the medicine and press it onto the eye for half an hour, until you see it darken and the stinging of the medicine subsides.
et se tu vues, pren coton et l’envoloupe sus aucun estrument, et moille lou coton en la medicine, et boute l’estrument a tout le couton en la cainne desus, tant que li coton s’aerde sus l’uve;	and if you can see again, take some cotton and roll it over an instrument, then dip the cotton in the medicine and place the instrument with all the cotton on top of the eyelid until the cotton adheres to the eye.
et fai ceu sovent, tant que li cauteres soit parfais, puis la laisse elle seche, et chiet aprés IIII jors ou V.	And do this often, so that the cautery is perfect, then let it dry, and fall off after four or five days.
Et se tu as mestier de rencomencier lou cautere de la medicine, si le rencomence, et aprés le cautere l’essue entor l’uve, de couton embut em burre, et mundifie ceu qui est entor de la medicine;	And if you need to restart the medical cautery, then restart it, and after the cauterization wipe around the wound with cotton soaked in butter, and clean what is around the affected area.
et soit arosez d’aigue froide, et soit curez de gargarismes tant qu’il soit sanez.	And be rinsed with cold water, or cured with gargles until it is healed.
Ceste cure est plus save de l’incision, ne que li cautere;	This treatment is safer than the incision, not the cauterization;
s’elle est curee de fumigation selonc ceste maniere, pren calament et ysope et origanum et rue et camomille et avronne et semblans herbes, et les assemble toutes ou aucunes d’eles en I pot, et i met aisil, et fai bullir;	If it is treated with fumigation in this way, take chamomile and hyssop and oregano and rue and marigold and similar herbs, mix all or some of them into a pot, add vinegar, and boil.
et li potz soit bien gluez de fort terre, et enmi le pot ait I estrument cheveit selonc ceste maniere:	and the pot is well glued with strong clay, and inside the pot place one instrument shaped like this:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain, et soit li uns des chiés boutez en la bouche dou malaide tant que li vapor monte a l’uve par la caine, tant que li uve soit mortifie;	and it is made of silver or brass, and one end of the instrument should be inserted into the patient's mouth so that the vapour rises up to the eye through the nose, until the eye is withered.
aprés lou rencomence sovent, tant que li uve seche, et garde que tu ne faices ceu au comencement de l’avenement de l’aposteme chaut, car plusors choses i avienent;	after you repeat this often, until the eye dries out, and be careful not to do this at the beginning of the onset of the hot abscess, as many things can happen.
et ne faire mie ceu fuer que a la declination d’aposteme chaut.	and do not attempt this unless on the decline of the hot abscess.
Et se cist estrument n’est presens, si pren une caine et met dedens lou chief une craiffe d’uef, si que li bouche au malaide n’ait mie trop chaut;	And if this instrument is not available, take a nose and insert within the head a fragment of egg shell, so that the patient's mouth does not become too hot.
car li craiffe d’uef ne lait mie la vapor grever la bouche, et c’est bone cure ensamble salut.	For egg white does not let vapors harm the mouth, and it is a good treatment together with health.
Maintes fois s’aert a la gorge os ou espinee de poisson, ou aucune chose;	Often there is something stuck in the throat, like a bone or fish spine, or some other object.
si covient donc que tu traies ceu que tu pues veoir, et li presse la lengue au soleil a tout l’estrument, si que tu voies mues la chose;	So you must therefore extract whatever is visible, pressing the tongue against the front of the mouth with an instrument so that you can see and move the object.
et ceu que ne t’apert mie et est reponus en la gorge, covient que tu faices vomir le malaide ainsois que li viande soit cuite en l’estomac;	And for that which is not visible and remains in the throat, you must make the patient vomit before the food is fully digested.
par aventure si istra li chose aerse par le vomissement;	Hopefully, this will cause the object to be expelled through vomiting.
ou li malaides englutisse une piece d’esponge, ou une piece de navel, ou une racine de laitue, ou I morceil de pain sec;	Or the patient has swallowed a piece of sponge, or a piece of bread crumb, or a lettuce root, or a piece of dry bread.
et lie a l’esponge I fil, et puis la transglutisse;	Et tie to the sponge a thread, and then swallow it.
et quant elle venra au leu, si s’aerdra, et puis trairas fuer;	And when it reaches its place, it will untie itself, and then you will pull out the thread.
et s’elle ne vient fuer de ceu que nos avons dit, si pren I estrument de plonc selonc ceste forme:	And if it does not come out by what we have said, then take a plumb instrument of this form:
Et soit li estrumens corbés au chief si qu’il puist plus legierement entrer en la gorge, et ait le chief en haut leveit;	And let the instrument be bent at the head so that it may more easily enter into the throat, and keep the head raised upwards.
et warde que tu ne touchier l’epiglote, que li tous ne li viegne, ne ne bouter mie l’os dedens;	And take care not to touch the epiglottis, for if you do, he will choke and push the bone inward.
et mues vaut que li malaides i boute l’estrument, por ceu qu’il seit mues ou li chose est aerse;	And it is better that the patient pushes in the instrument, so he knows where things are.
si la boute aval, ou il la traie fuer a tout l’estrument igalment, tant qu’elle soit fuer.	If the swelling goes down, or it is drawn out by force with all instruments equally, until it is fully extracted.
de la sansue de la gorge	Of the blood of the throat.
Aucune fois est medicinee li sansue, si com j’ai dit en la division, par la cure de medicines;	No remedy in medicine is without side effects, just as I mentioned earlier regarding the treatment with medications.
et quant ceu ne profite mie, adonques regarde en la gorge dou malaide au soleil, puis que tu li presses la lengue a l’estrument que je t’ai dit.	And when the remedy does not work, then look into the patient's throat in sunlight and press their tongue with an instrument as I have instructed you.
Et se tu vois la sansue, si la trai a tout I petit uncine, ou as tenailles subtilz que valent a ceu.	And if you see the leech, draw it out with a very small hook, or use delicate pincers suitable for the task.
Et se ceu ne vaut, si pren une caine chevee, et la boute en la gorge dou malaide, puis boute ou chevement de la caine I fer chaut, et fai ce sovent.	And if this does not work, take a hair plait and insert it into the patient's throat; then attach the end of the hair to a heated iron, and do this frequently.
Et se teigne li malaides d’aigue toute jor.	And if the patient is afflicted by water every day.
puis pren plein I voirre d’aigue froide, et oevre la bouche, et la giete ens sens englutir, et la mueve a sa main sovent;	Then take a full glass of cold water, open the mouth, pour it in so they swallow, and move their hand frequently.
et si tost com li sansue sent l’aigue, si chiet.	And as soon as the remedy feels the water, remove it.
Et s’elle ne chiet si com nos avons dit, si subfumige lou malaide d’asefetide, a l’estrument que j’ai dit en la fumigation de l’uve;	And if it does not fall out as we have said, then smoke the patient with asafetida using an instrument as I mentioned in the procedure for fumigating the eye.
fai ceu maintes fois, car elle cherra sens targier.	Do this many times, for it will fall without injury.
Et li maniere de la fumigation si est que tu preignes I pot ou il ait charbons vis, et soit li pos covert d’un coverseil perciet en mileu, et en celui pertus soit li chiés de l’estrument;	And the method of fumigation is that you take a pot with live coals, and cover it with a perforated lid in the middle, and insert the head of the instrument into this opening.
puis i giete ta fumigation, et li malaides mette lou chief de la cainne en sa bouche, et cloie la bouche, si que li fumee n’en isse mie, mais viegne jusc’a la sansue;	Then pour your fumigation into it, and have the patient place the end of the tube in their mouth, closing it so that no smoke escapes but instead goes right up to the tonsils.
et la sansue cherra maintenant, et s’elle ne chiet, si rencomence la fumigation par maintes fois;	And now the tonsil will fall out, and if it does not, then repeat the fumigation many times over again.
et soffre li malaides soif, et menjuce choses salees et als, et ne boive point d’aigue;	And let the patient suffer thirst, eating salty things and similar items, but not drinking water.
et adonques li iert mestier qu’elle isse fuer par cest governement.	And then she would need to go through this treatment.
Et li forme de l’estrument a coi on trait la sansue, si est, quant on la puet veoir, semblans a tenailles corbés por mues entrer en la gorge;	And the shape of the instrument used to remove the leech is like curved pliers so that they can be inserted into the throat.
et ait semblance au bec de soigne, et i ait asperiteit de lime, si que ceu qu’elle prent, elle ne puet lassier;	and it resembles the beak of a stork, with the roughness of a file, such that whatever it grasps, it cannot release.
et vez ci la forme:	And here you see the form [of this instrument]:
li chapistres des apostemes	The chapters of abscesses.
Mout de semblances d’aposteme sont, selonc ceu que li remembrance vient ci aprés d’un et d’autre en cest livre, et sont diver en perforation et en taille;	Many kinds of abscesses there are, as the following passages in this book about one and another suggest, they vary in their perforations and incisions.
et c’est en II manieres dont l’une est en sa semblance meisme, et de ceu qu’il tient moistor.	and it is in two ways, one of which is similar in its appearance, and what holds moisture.
Et li seconde maniere si est por les leus ou il sont au cors.	And the second way is for their locations where they are in the body.
car li apostemes dou chief est autres que cil dou fondement, et li apostemes dou leu charnut est autres que cil qui vient en jointures, et chescuns ait son jugement en l’uevre.	Because abscesses of the head are different from those of the fundament, and abscesses in fleshy places differ from those that appear in joints, each requiring its own judgment when treating them.
Et si a apostemes c’on ne doit mie percier, tant que li bowe est meure selonc son acomplissement;	And if abscesses must not be pierced until the bowels are dead according to their completion.
et si a de telz qu’il covient percier quant il sont crut, et ne meurent mie selonc lor acomplissement, si com aposteme qui sont delez jointures.	And if these ones must be pierced when they are ripe, and do not die according to their completion, as abscesses that are near joints.
Car quant apostemes vient delez jointures, et on le laisse tant qu’il est porris entor, par aventure si sont corrumput li liien et li nerf de la jointure, par coi ce est cause de contraction en celui membre.	For when abscesses occur near joints, and they are left until the surrounding area is rotten, perhaps the ligaments and nerves of the joint have been corrupted, which causes contractions in that limb.
Ou li aposteme est delez lou membre principel, et se tu tardes la perforation tant qu’il soit meurez, si nuira au membre principeil;	Where the abscess is near the main member, and if you delay the perforation until it dies, then it will harm the main member.
ou il est delez lou fondement, si le perce on ainsois qu’il soit meurs;	When it is near the foundation, pierce it before it dies.
et ne covient mie que tu perces aposteme crut sens digestion acomplie, fuers que celui qui est delez lou fondement, qu’il ne porrisse em parfont, et soit alongiez dedens, et i viegne fistule;	And it is not necessary to pierce ripe abscesses without completed digestion unless the one near the foundation which would rot completely and lengthen within and a fistula will form.
et ne puisse saner en grant termine.	And cannot heal within a long period of time.
Et covient que tu saiches l’oure de la perforation de l’aposteme qui est meur selonc l’acomplissement, et c’est quant li dolor est apaisie, et li departemens de la fievre, et l’amenuisement de la dolor et de la roujor, et dou debatement et de l’aguisement dou chief de l’aposteme, et les autres signes;	And it is necessary that you know the stage of the abscess's perforation which is ripe according to its development, and this occurs when the pain subsides, the fever breaks, swelling diminishes, redness fades, softening and pointing occurs at the apex of the abscess, and other such signs appear;
et covient que tu faices seoir la perforation ou plus dependant leu de l’aposteme, et la ou il apert mues;	and you must allow the abscess to develop where it has opened up, or is most prone to open, and where pus appears.
et soit li perforation dou lonc dou cors, et se li apostemes est as mains ou as piez, ou en jointures et au ners et as arteres, et en toz leus igalz ou il n’a point de ploieure.	whether the abscess is located in a fleshy part of the body or on the hands and feet, at joints, nerves, arteries, or any place equally accessible where there are no folds.
En ces que ploient, par selonc celui membre.	In those that bend, according to this member.
Et quant apostemes est en leu charnut, si vaut mues que tu laisses la perforation tant qu’il soit confermez en digestion acomplie, si com nos avons dit.	And when an abscess is in the fleshy place, it is better that you leave the perforation until it is confirmed with complete digestion, as we have said.
Car se tu lou perces devant ceu, si iert alongiez li cors dou venim de lui, et est plains de mout d’ordure;	For if you pierce it before this, then the body of the poison from him would be elongated, and it is full of much filth.
et par aventure endurcissent les levres et li parfondetez de lui.	and by chance harden the lips and its deepest part.
Et si a aucun aposteme que sont perciet selonc le large dou cors, selonc ceu que li membres en ait mestier.	And for any abscess that is pierced according to the width of the body, according to what the member needs.
Et covient que tu amenistres em petis apostemes, petis pertus;	And you must treat small abscesses with small punctures.
et en grans apostemes, grans pertus, et maintes fendures selonc la semblance de la grandor de l’aposteme;	in large abscesses, make large punctures, and many incisions according to the likeness of the size of the abscess.
et si a de tels apostemes ou il covient chever lou keur, et coper;	and if at such an abscess where it is necessary to cut out its heart, and excise.
quant il est jai devenus ausi com I drapelz, et est amortis, si covient faire ausi com on fait as bubes:	when it has become like leather, and is dead, then you must do the same as with bubbles:
et si a de telz que sont fendut en III angles, et si a de telz dont on cope ausi com la fuelle de mirte, si com apostemes des angres;	And there are some that are split into three angles, and there are others where you cut like the leaf of myrtle, as with abscesses in gangrene.
et si a de telz ou on fait une reonde taille, et autres tailles et semblant copeure.	And there are some where you make a round incision, and other incisions and similar cuttings.
Cil qui n’ont point de chief, si com aposteme souef superficial, il covient que tu lou perces plainnement;	Those without a head, like soft superficial abscesses, you must pierce fully through;
et covient quant li apostemes est gros, et il a coillit grant bowe, et tu lou perces, si ne traire mie toute la bowe en celle houre, mais en trai une partie;	And when the abscess is large, and it has developed a thick core, and you pierce it, do not extract all of the core at once, but remove only part of it;
puis estoupe l’aposteme jusc’a l’autre jor, puis en trai aucune chose derechief;	Then pack the abscess with wool until the next day, then extract the remainder promptly;
fai ceu par maintes fois de greit en greit, tant que li bowe isse toute;	Do this many times from one end to another until the bowels are completely empty.
meismement se li malaides est de foible vertut, ou femme portans, ou petis enfes, ou viez hons decrepites.	Especially if the patient is of weak constitution, or a pregnant woman, or small children, or elderly people in poor health.
Car li esperis tressaut aucune fois avec l’issue de la bowe, que par aventure muert li malaides, et tu ne t’en persois.	For spirits sometimes convulse with bowel movement, which may cause the patient's death, and you will not perceive it.
Eschuez donques cest chapistre par grant cautele, et quant tu as perciet ton aposteme, si essue la plaie, et regarde se li plaie de l’aposteme est petite;	Examine this chapter carefully with great caution, and once you have pierced the abscess, then dry the wound, and check if the abscess wound is small.
et se c’est une tailleure plainne, si amenistre tentes de lin ou de viez coton;	And if it is a full-blown fistula, then apply tents of linen or old cotton.
et se c’est uns grans apostemes, et il i a mout de pertus, si covient que tu boutes en chescun une tente si qu’ele viegne l’une contre l’autre;	And if it is a large abscess with many openings, then you must insert a tent into each one so that they come up against one another.
et se tu as copeit en l’aposteme une partie dou cuir, et tu l’as cheveit entor, si covient que tu l’emplisses de viel couton ou de rasure de dras de lin sens moistor, et le lie jusc’au tier jor;	And if you have cut into the abscess and removed a piece of skin, then you must fill it with old cotton or shredded linen cloth without moisture, and bind it until the third day.
puis l’oste, et le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then remove the binding, and treat with ointment until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc avient a ton ovraige, si amenistre aigue froide et aisil, et moille I drapeil, et met sor le leu decorrant par maintes fois.	And if bleeding occurs during your work, bring cold water and apply it gently, dampen the cloths, and place them over the bleeding site repeatedly.
Et se li decorremens de sanc persevere, se i amenistre governement et cure, et les poudres que j’ai dit em mains leus en cest livre, et se c’est ou tens d’iver, et li leus ou li apostemes est est mout nervous, si couvient que tu mettes sus tentes et drapelz moilliez en vin et en oile chaut;	And if the discharge of blood persists, provide treatment and ointment, and the powders I mentioned in various places throughout this book, and if it is during winter, and the wound or abscess is very raw, then you must apply moistened tents and cloths with warm oil and wine.
et se c’est en esteit, et li leus est charnus, si covient que tu mes sus drapelz moilliez en aigue et en oile, ou en vin et en oile froit, jusc’au tier jor, si com nos avons dit;	And if it is in the summer, and the wound is fleshy, then you must apply cloths moistened with water and oil, or cold wine and oil, until the third day, as we have said.
et puis deslie l’aposteme et l’essue et le cure, si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then unbind the abscess, wipe it clean, and treat it as necessary until it is healed.
Et ceu covient il conoistre universement en cures des apostemes:	For this one must universally understand in the treatment of abscesses:
or vos ai dit coment on doit aler avant as cures des apostemes, et vez ci le chapistre.	Now I have told you how one must proceed before treating abscesses, and here is the chapter.
des soros	sores
Ou keur dou chief vienent petis apostemes, et sont manieres de nous que sont en toiles, ausi com li josier d’une geline, et mout en i a de semblances.	Where small abscesses come from on the head and are like threads, just as the yolk of an egg is, and there are many similar cases.
Il en i a de gras et de telz ou il a moistor ausi com poulz;	There are some that are fatty and soft where there is also moisture like pus;
et si a de telz qui sont dur et pierous au taillier, et n’i a point de doutance se li artere n’i fait contraire.	And if you find ones that are hard and stony when cut open, and there is no doubt if the arteries do not act contrary to this.
Et li ovraiges de la taille si est que tu esprueve a tout I estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», de coi li forme vient ci aprés, quel chose il contient.	And the work of cutting into stones is such that you should test all instruments which are called an "entromissoire", from whence its form comes after, what it contains.
Car s’il contient moistor, si lou fent par desus dou lonc.	For if it contains moisture, they do so above the long bone.
Et quant li moistor est vuidie, si escorche sens rien laissier la peil qui contient celle moistor, car il revient adés quant on i laisse rien;	And when the moisture is drained, scrape away any remaining skin containing this moisture, for it will return if you leave anything behind.
puis plonge coton en oignement egiptien, s’il est presens;	Then dip cotton in Egyptian ointment, if it is present;
se ceu non, en aigue et en seil, et en emple la plaie, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor;	If not, dip it in water and salt, apply to the wound, and leave it until the next day;
et ceu corront ceu qui est demorez dou nit.	And this will correct what remained from the night.
Et pues rencomence lou coton, si com devant, le second jor, et lou tier, tant que tu saiches bien qu’il ne demoure point dou nit;	And you can repeat the process with cotton, as before, on the second day and again on the third, until you know that nothing remains from overnight.
puis cure la plaie d’oignement a ceu convenauble, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound with an appropriate ointment until it is healed.
Et se li apostemes tient I nout gras, si le cope selonc ceste forme, dou lonc;	And if abscess has become filled with pus, open it lengthwise in this manner:
et i giete tes oncines, et l’escorche de toutes pars, et met toute ta cure de traire fuer la cotte ou il gist;	And I remove your fingers, and scrape away all skin, and pay close attention to draw out the fluid where it lies;
et se li artere te fait contraire, si fai ceu que je t’ai dit aprés.	And if the artery opposes you, do as I have told you afterward.
Et ausi fai de l’aposteme s’il est pierous, et dou taillier et dou curer si com je t’ai dit.	And also do this for the abscess if it is malignant, and about cutting and treating as I have told you.
Et li taille sus l’aposteme pierous et le moiste, si est plus legiere, car il sont de poc de sanc.	And the incision on the malignant abscess and the moist area is lighter, for they contain little blood.
Et si a aucuns de ces apostemes ou chief ou il n’a point de moistor, et de ces fut I apostemes que je copai ou chief d’une vielle femme;	And if there is no moisture in some of these abscesses or at the top where there is none for an old woman's head;
et trovai l’aposteme ausi com une piere xourde, aspre et blainche, et ne pooit brisier;	and found the abscess just like a hard stone, rough and white, that could not be broken;
et s’on en eust ferut aucun, on li eust ausi bien fait plaie com d’une piere.	and if one had made an incision there, it would have been just as painful as a stone.
En autres apostemes venans ou chief, fuer que ces qui vienent as chief des enfans et as racines des oreilles, li overture si soit toz jors au plus dependant leu, por mues issir la bowe;	In other abscesses coming to the head, especially those that come to a child's head and at the base of their ears, open them always as low down as possible so as to remove the pus.
et les cure si com il covient.	and treat them as necessary.
des scrophules	Des scrophules
Maintes fois avienent cist aposteme au col, et desoz les asseles, et ens angres, et aucune fois vienent autre part ou cors, et sont mout, et sont enjanrees l’une avec l’autre.	Maintes fois viennent ces abcès dans le cou, et sous les aisselles, et dans la poitrine, et parfois ils apparaissent ailleurs sur le corps, et il y en a beaucoup, et ils sont interconnectés les uns avec les autres.
Et chescune scrophule est proprement dedens sa cote, si com li nout et li aposteme dou chief, si com nos avons dit;	And each scrofula is properly within its own area, just like the nodules and abscesses of the head, as we have said;
et les semblances de ces scrophules sont maintes.	and there are many similarities between these scrofulas.
Il i a de teles que contienent moistor, et si a de malignes qui ne vuellent obeir a santeit.	There are some that contain moisture, and there are others which are malignant and do not want to obey the rules of health.
en celle donques que tu vois de bone disposition au tochier, et est semblans a la color dou cors, et muet de chescune part et n’est mie aerse as ners dou col ne a l’artere ne au conduit, et n’est mie parfonde;	in those where you see good positioning to touch, and it resembles the color of the body, and it moves from each side without being exposed to the veins of the neck or the artery or the windpipe, and it is not deep;
si covient que tu la copes par desus, et l’escorche de chescune partie, et estent les II levres dou keur as oncines, se tu en as mestier, si com nos avons dit en apostemes dou chief;	you must cut it from above and peel off each part, extending the two lips of the wound with scissors if you need to, just as we have said for abscesses of the head;
et la trai poc et poc, et soies seur que tu ne coper lou nerf ne la voine, et ne soit mie li spatumile agus ne trenchans, que li mains n’eschaipe, et ne voise trop avant, que tu ne coper mie ceu que tu ne dois.	And strike repeatedly with the spatula, and be sure that you do not cut the nerve or vein, and let the spatula's edge not be sharp nor cutting, so that the hand does not escape, and do not aim too far ahead, lest you cut what you should not.
Et se tu copes la voinne ou l’artere, et ceu ne te laisse ovrer, si met en la plaie vitriole broiet, ou aucunes poudres que restainchent sanc, et estraint la plaie;	And if you cut the vein or artery, and it does not stop bleeding, apply crushed vitriol to the wound, or some powders that staunch blood, and bind up the wound tightly.
et la laisse tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et soit amollie li plaie, et encomence a porrir.	And let it be until the abscess is healed, and the wound softens, and begins to rot.
Et quant li sans est estainchiez, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que tu l’acomplisses;	And when the blood is staunched, return to your work until it is complete.
puis quier a ton doit indice s’il i demoure nules petites scrophules, si les cope et les munde.	Then look with your index finger to see if there are any small scrofulae remaining; remove them and clean them.
Et s’il a en la racine de la scrophule voinne grant, si ne covient mie que tu copes celle scrophule en sa racine, mais la lie d’un fil double fort, et la laisse cheoir par li, sens nuisement;	And if there is a large wound at the root of the scrofula, you should not cut that scrofula at its root but bind it with a strong double thread and let it fall off by itself without causing harm.
puis emple la plaie de viel coton plongiet en oignement egiptien, puis la cure.	Then clean the wound with old cotton dipped in Egyptian ointment, then treat it.
Et se tu copes toute la scrophule, si covient que tu assembles les II levres de la plaie, et les cout maintenant, puis qu’il n’i a point demoreit de superfluiteit por la grandor de la scrophule.	And if you cut out the entire scrofula, then you must bring together the two lips of the wound, sewing them now since there is no extra space due to the size of the scrofula.
si covient que tu entendes a coper la racine de li, et traire fuer, et la cout si com nos avons dit.	It is necessary for you to understand that it involves cutting the root of it and pulling out its hair, then sewing as we have said.
Celles scrophules que tienent superfluiteit, perce lai ou il apert meure;	For scrofulae that persist with superfluidity, make an incision where it seems to die out.
et la perce ensi com celle devant dite, en dependant, puis i amenistre tentes avec oignement et semblans choses, si qu’elle corrompe ceu qui est demorez de la corruption;	And pierce it in the same way as previously mentioned, below it, and introduce tenting with ointment and similar things so that it drains away what remains of the corruption.
et quant li plaie est bien mundee, si la cure d’oignement enjanrant char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the wound is well cleaned, treat it with ointment to promote flesh growth until it heals.
de squinance	For eczema
Li ancien dirent et parlerent de la tailleure de la gorge;	The ancients spoke of the operation on the throat;
mais je ne vis onques en nostre terre qui la feist, et c’est li escripture de lor parole.	But I have never seen anyone in our land do it, and this is the writing of their words.
A ces qui ont squinance, il covient que li fendure de la gorge qui est apelee «epiglote» soit eschuee;	For those with difficulty breathing, it is necessary that the cleft of the throat, which is called the epiglottis, be cleared.
et c’on ne faice aide par ceu, por ceu que toutes les voines et li pormon dou malaide sont a ces qui ont aposteme chaut en la bouche, ou en la gorge ou en II amandres.	And if no help is given through this method, it is because all the veins and passages of the patient are affected by the abscesses hot in the mouth, or in the throat or on the tonsils.
Quant li maladie est en la chenal dou pormon, il covient coper l’epiglote por fuir la perdition qui vient de l’estranglement.	When the illness is in the channel of the passage, it is necessary to cut the epiglottis to avoid the danger that comes from suffocation.
Il covient donques, quant nos volons fendre l’epiglote, que nos le fendons desoz III cercles ou IIII une petite fendure dou travers, entre les II cercles ou par la quantiteit de la fendure dou syfac, ne mie en la cartillaige;	It is necessary then, when we wish to split the epiglottis, that we split it below three circles or four with a small transverse slit between two circles or according to the amount of the slit of the superficial cartilage, not in the cartilaginous part.
et cil leus si est covenaubles a la section de l’epiglote qu’il n’i a point de char, et li vasseil sont lonc d’enqui.	And these two are suitable for the section of the epiglottis where there is no flesh, and the vessels are long enough.
Et se li maistres est paourous, si covient qu’il estende le cuir de la gorge a tout l’oncine, puis fende lou keur tant qu’il viegne a la cheneil;	And if the master is afraid, it is necessary that he stretches the skin of the throat on all sides, then splits the heart until it reaches the windpipe;
et eschue les vasselz de sanc, se tu vois aucune chose, et puis cope lou syfac, si com nos avons dit;	And purge the blood vessels, if you see anything, then cut the superficial cartilage as we have said;
et est demostrez par la section dou fleume de la cheneil ki saut fuer par le leu qui est rompus, et par la defaute de la voix;	And it is demonstrated by the obstruction of the windpipe that comes from its place which is broken, and by the failure of the voice.
et laisse la plaie overte une piece.	and leave the wound open for a moment.
Et quant li houre est passee de coi on doute l’estranglement, assemble les II levres de la plaie dou keur, et la cout toute soule sens la cartillaige;	And when the hour has passed in which strangulation is suspected, bring together the two lips of the wound from the heart, and stitch it all up without touching the cartilage.
puis aministre medicines qui font naistre char, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then administer medicines that promote flesh growth until it is healed.
Albucasim dist c’on ne faice ce jusc’a tant que li gorge est toute estoupee, et li malaides est jugiez a mort, et li defaut li alaine.	Albucasis says one should not do this until the throat is entirely stuffed up and the patient is judged to be dying, when all hope of breath has been lost.
Adonques cope on l’epiglote por ceu que li malaides ne puet alener, et il respire par la plaie, et ensi est gardez de mort;	Thereupon cauterize the epiglottis for patients who cannot breathe and are breathing through their wound, thus saving them from death.
et por ce commanderent li anciain a laissier la plaie overte tant que li malice de la maladie soit passee, et elle est passee en III jors ou en IIII Et adonques il comanderent a coudre la plaie et curer, tant qu’elle fut curee;	and for this reason the ancients recommended leaving the wound open until the evil of the disease has passed, and it passes in three or four days. Then they would command to close the wound and treat it until it is healed.
et je vos dirai ceu que je vis.	And I will tell you what I saw.
Je vis que une damoisele prist I coutel, et le ficha en sa gorge, et copa partie des chenelz dou pormon;	I saw that a damsel took a knife, and thrust it into her throat, cutting part of the windpipe;
et je fui apelez por li curer, et la trovai ausi com morte.	And I was called to treat her, but found her as good as dead.
Je descovris la plaie, et trovai le sanc qui en estoit issus, et soi bien qu’elle n’avoit mie copeit voine ne conduit fuer que la gorge, et li vens issoit fuer par la plaie.	I uncovered the wound and found blood pouring from it, I knew she had not cut a vein or pierced her throat, and air was escaping through the injury.
Je me hastai, et cousi la plaie, et la curai tant qu’elle fut sanee;	I hurried, sewed up the wound, and treated her until she was healed.
et n’avint a la damoisele fuer qu’elle fut roge de voix, et revint aprés a sa disposition;	And all the damsel had was a hoarse voice, and she soon recovered fully.
por ceu di je que en la tailleure de l’epiglote n’ait mie paour.	Because of this, I say that one need not fear incisions to the epiglottis.
de la grosse gorge	On swelling of the throat
Cist apostemes est apelez «hernie de gorge», et est uns grans apostemes en color d’une jaisse, et est molt en femmes;	This abscess is called 'throat hernia', and it is a large abscess in the colour of jaundice, and it often occurs in women.
et est selonc II manieres:	et it is according to two manners:
naturez, et accidens;	natural, and accidental;
ou natureil n’a point d’engien.	or natural has no engine.
Et li accidens est selonc II manieres, de coi l’une est semblans a gras nous, et li autre maniere est semblans a aposteme qui vient de nous d’artere;	And the accidental is according to two manners, of which one resembles fat near us, and the other manner resembles an abscess that comes from our artery;
et il i ait paour, et ne covient mie ovrer de feir fuers que en celi qui est petite, et le prueve et cerche a tout l’intromissoire:	and there is fear, and it is not advisable to operate with fire except in the small one, and prove and search all the surroundings:
se tu le trueves ausi com I nout gras, et ne pent a nulle voine, si le cope, si com on cope les nous, et le trai a tout sa coife, s’il en i a point;	if you find it as our natural fat, and cannot reach any vein, cauterize it as we cauterize the nose, and treat all its surface if there is no incision;
et encerche bien tot, et le cure si com il covient, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	And cauterize quickly, treating it as required until it is perfectly healed.
des nous	From us.
Maintes manieres de nous sont, dont je dirai toutes les semblances;	There are many ways of doing this, all of which I will describe in detail;
et or covient que je die toute la difference qui est entre nout et issue.	And here it is appropriate for me to explain the distinction between our method and theirs.
Je dis que issue est chalors et fievre tenans, tant que li ebulicions est passee, et est acomplie li porriture;	I say that theirs is one of heat and fever until the boils pass, and the pus is complete;
adonques repose li fievre et li chalor.	And then the fever and heat subside.
Avec lou nout n’a ne chalor ne fievre ne dolor, et contient I syfac, qui est ses propres sac et est selonc la color dou cors, et encomence ausi com une jaisse, et devient gros;	Our method has neither heat nor fever nor pain, but involves a swelling which is its own sack and takes the colour of the body, starting like a scab and growing larger;
et sont selonc II semblances, ou grais, ou moiste, et mout de color sont si com j’ai dit en la division.	And they are of two types, either dry or moist, with much variation in color as I have mentioned earlier.
Il covient, quant tu viens a la cure dou nout, que tu esprueves et l’enquier premierement a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «entromissoire», selonc ce que sa forme venra ou chapistre qui est aprés.	When you come to our treatment, it is necessary that you first examine and inquire about all the instrument called "entromissoire", according to its form as described in the following chapter.
Et li maniere de l’inquisicion des apostemes des nous est que tu preignes ou plus moiste leu que tu trueves en l’aposteme, et torne tes dois poc et poc, tant que tu saiches que li estrumens ait perciet le keur, puis que ce soit selonc la grandor de l’aposteme;	The method of inquiring about the abscess is to take the moistest part that you find in the abscess, and turn your fingers back and forth until you feel that the instrument has pierced the core, then do so according to the size of the abscess.
puis estrai l’entromissoire, et pren garde en ceu que saut fuer.	Then remove the instrument, taking care not to pull it out abruptly.
Se moistor corrans cort, queil color elle ait, si le fent si com j’ai dit des autres apostemes;	If the discharging moisture is running short, whatever its color may be, treat it as I have said for other abscesses.
et se aprés l’entromissoire nen vient moistor, saiches qu’il est gras, si le fent donques en croix, et le prent as pinceures, et l’escorche legierement de chescune part et warde la cotte ou il gist que tu la traies saine avec le nout;	And if after removing the instrument there is no moisture, know that it is greasy, so treat it in a cross-like manner, take the pincers and lightly strip away the skin on each side, and remove the scurf where it lies until you draw out healthy tissue with the nut.
et se tu ne la pues traire saine, si la trai par pieces si qu’il n’i demoure rien.	And if you cannot draw it out whole, then draw it piece by piece until nothing remains.
Car s’il i demoure rien, si revient li nous par maintes fois;	For if anything is left behind, the wound will return many times.
et s’il en demore un poc, et li sans te grieve, si emple la plaie d’aucunes poudres corrosives agues, et estraint la plaie, et met sus choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	And if even a little remains and the blood bothers you, then fill the wound with some sharp corrosive powders, bind up the wound, and apply warm abscess-soothing things, and treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
et se li nous est grans, si cout les II levres de la plaie, et le cure de ceu qui enjanre char.	And if the wound is large, then cut the two lips of the wound, and treat it with something that encourages flesh to grow.
et se li voine batans t’est contraire ou autre si te haste et emple le leu de vitriole broiet, et lou laisse liiet II jors ou III, tant que li plaie porrisse, et repose li ebulicion dou sanc;	And if the striking vein is contrary to you or otherwise troublesome, then hasten and apply crushed vitriol, leaving it on for two or three days until the wound festers, and halting the boiling of blood.
puis revien au coper ceu que i est demoreit dou nout.	Then return to cut off what has remained of the night.
Vez ci les formes des estrumens entromissoires, et sont de III manieres:	Look here at the shapes of the insertion instruments, and they are of three types:
grans et moien et petit;	Large and medium and small;
et s’en i a III quarrez qui sont apelez «albaret», et I qui est apelez «breb», et s’en i a de III manieres:	And there are three squares which are called "albaret", and one which is called "breb", and they are of three types:
grant, moien, et petit, por encerchier les apostemes de fistule;	Large, medium, and small, to probe abscesses and fistulas;
et sont ausi com les aguilles dont on cout les sorceles, et sont d’arain citrin, ou de fer, ou d’argent, et mues valent cil qui sont jaune, et sont plus esprovez de plonc noir por encerchier les corbeures de fistule;	And they are like the needles with which we sew up wounds, and they are of brass, or iron, or silver, but those that are yellow are more valuable, and they are especially useful for probing dark-coloured fistulas;
et sont de III manieres:	And they are of three kinds:
grans, moiens, et petis, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce des pertus.	large, medium, and small, according to the quantity of the width of the openings.
Les formes des oncines sont de mout de semblances, si com tu vois ci:	The shapes of the "oncines" (a term for an unknown object) are very similar, as you see here:
grans, moiens, et petis;	large, medium, and small;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures de III manieres ausi;	And if there be "oncines" which have two curvatures of three kinds also;
et si a oncines qui ont III corbeures, et sont ausi de III manieres;	And if there be "oncines" which have three curvatures, and they are also of three kinds;
et si a oncines qui ont II corbeures, et oncines d’une corbeure soulement, et sont de III manieres;	And if there be "oncines" which have two curvatures, and those with one curvature only, and they are of three kinds;
et tuit cist sont necessaire en lor leu.	And all these are necessary in their place.
Li chief de ces a coi on fent sont trenchant, et de telz i a qui ne taillent mie fuer que d’une part, dont on escorche les nous, por ceu c’on ne cope la voine ne le nerf;	The heads of these have what one does with them are sharp, and there are some that only cut from one side, which peels off the veins because it doesn't cut into the vein or nerve.
et de ces intromissoires sont les alemeles reponues en mainches, si que li malaide ne s’en persoivent a l’overture des apostemes;	And these introducer are the levers that respond in many ways so that the patient does not perceive them when opening abscesses.
et sont de III manieres:	And they are of three kinds:
grant, petit, et moien, si com tu vois;	Large, small, and medium, as you see it.
et n’en use on mie fuer que en leu charnut, si com jambes, et bras, et mameles, et as angres, et en semblans leus;	And one should not use them except in fleshy places such as legs, arms, breasts, and similar areas.
et aucune fois fait on I autre estrument petit, semblant a escorces de fistices, selonc ceste forme, a coi on estainche sanc:	And sometimes one makes another small instrument, resembling the bark of fig trees, according to this form, with which one stops the blood.
et le met on aucune fois au leu qui saine a copement des voines, et as arteres, et aucune fois reont selonc ceste grant forme:	and it is sometimes placed where healing occurs through the closing of veins and arteries, and other times according to this larger form:
Aucune fois enflent les mameles d’aucuns homes quant cil encomencent estre corrumput, tant qu’eles semblent mameles de feme;	Sometimes the breasts of some men swell when they begin to be corrupted, so that they resemble the breasts of women;
et demorent laides et enflees, et qui les vuet curer, si le covient soier selonc ceste forme des ceste ligne .b. jusques a .g.:	And they remain ugly and swollen, and for those who wish to cure them, one must proceed according to this form along the following lines: b. up to g..
puis escorche la graisse, et emple la plaie de medicine enjanrant char, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie a costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee;	Then scrape away the fat, fill the wound with flesh-healing medicine, then bring together the two lips of the wound with stitches, and treat it until it is healed.
et se li mamele cline aval, et est amolie por sa grandor si com il avient as femmes, si la fent en II costelz desus, par II semblans fendures;	And if the breast hangs down, having become soft due to its size like in women, open it into two parts above with two similar incisions.
de coi l’une soit tenans a l’autre a la fin de l’une et de l’autre, si que li plus grans ligne conteigne la menor selonc ceste forme, des ceste ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.;	where one end is attached to the other at the very end of each, so that the larger line contains the smaller according to this form, from this line .b. up to line .g.
puis escorche le cuir qui est entre les II levres, et oste la graisse, et i amenistre ceu que nos avons dit de costure et de poudres, et ceu qui est necessaire en la cure, tant qu’il soit sanez;	then scrape the skin between the two lips, remove the fat, and apply what we have mentioned about sutures and powders, and provide whatever is necessary for healing until it is cured.
et s’il n’est sanez, ou li incision n’est mie toute faite, por ceu que li malaides ne vuet reposer, ou por le decorrement de sanc, si covient que tu emplisses la plaie de coton moilliet en oignement corrosif;	and if it is not healed or the incision is not complete due to the patient's reluctance to rest or blood loss, you must fill the wound with moist cotton soaked in a corrosive ointment.
et le laisse tant qu’il menjuce le remenant et la graisse, puis le cure tant qu’il soit saneis.	leave it until the remaining flesh and fat contract, then treat it until it is fully healed.
des apostemes des asselles	From abscesses of the armpits
Cist apostemes que vienent desoz les asseles sont manieres de scrophules dures ou il ait cotes, et s’en i a que contienent moistor.	These abscesses that come from under the armpits are like hard scrofula with sides, and if there is one containing moisture.
