Cil donques qui contienent moistor covient qu’il soient copez selonc ceste forme, des la ligne .b. jusc’a la ligne .g.:	Therefore, those that contain moisture should be cut according to this form, from line b to line g:
Et quant toute li bowe qui est en l’aposteme est vuidie, si emple la plaie de viel coton, et la laisse jusc’a l’autre jor, puis oste tout le coton, et cure d’oignement avenant a ceu tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the entire mass within the abscess is emptied, fill the wound with old cotton, and leave it until the next day; then remove all the cotton and treat it with ointment until it heals.
Et se li apostemes est de semblances de scrophules, si le fent si com nos avons dit en fendures des scrophules, et se li plaie rent bowe, si amenistre cautere si com nos avons dit devant.	And if the abscess is like a scrofula, treat it as we have said for scrofula slits; and if the wound contains mass, apply cauterization as mentioned earlier.
de la routure de l’artere	Of an artery's rupture
Quant li artere est route, et li cuir est soudez qui est sus, si en vient maintes fois apostemes, et tout aussi avient il a la voine enflee et aposteme;	When the artery is ruptured, and the skin above it is sealed together, there often arise abscesses, and likewise when the vein becomes swollen and infected.
et si le conoist on ensi quant c’est por l’artere, si est li apostemes lons em parfont;	and if you recognize it as such, when the abscess is long in appearance due to an artery injury...
et quant tu le sens a tes dois, si sens I estraignement;	...and when you feel it with your hands, there is a tightness or constriction.
et quant c’est por la voine, si est reons defuer aparans;	...if the swelling is on the vein, you will see raised red spots appear.
et c’est folie de coper cest aposteme, et meismement quant il est desoz les asseles et as angres et ou col et em mout d’autres leus, et est mout grans.	...it is foolish to cut this abscess, especially when it lies beneath the axillae and shoulders or on the neck in many places, and is very large.
Il covient donques eschuir la cure de fer, et celui qui est a chief covient eschuir ausi, et en celui qui est d’enfleure d’artere fent par desus le cuir dou lonc;	It is necessary, therefore, to avoid the treatment of iron, and for those who are at the head, it should also be avoided. In the case of swelling caused by an arterial rupture through the skin along its length,
puis oevre la taille as oncines, et depart bellement l’artere des toiles, tant qu’ele soit descoverte;	Then operate on the hip with scissors, carefully separating the artery from its membrane until it is fully exposed;
puis boute desoz li une aguille, et la fai percier jusc’a l’autre costeit, et estraint l’artere d’un fil double en II leus, selonc ceu que je t’ai ensigniet en l’estraction des II arteres qui sont en temples;	Then push a needle from one side through to the other and secure the artery with a double thread in two places, as I have taught you for extracting the two arteries located at the temples;
puis point le leu qui est entre les II liens d’un intromissoire tant que li sans en isse qui i est, et soit deliiez li aposteme;	Then puncture the area between the two ligatures with a probe until the blood there is released and the abscess is drained;
puis amenistre la cure que enjanre bowe, tant que li liien chient;	Then apply the treatment that stimulates healing, until the binding falls off.
puis cure ceu d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then treat those with swelling next to it, until they are healed.
et se li apostemes est por la taille de la voinne, si covient que tu teignes a ta main ceu que tu pues de l’aposteme a tout le cuir, puis boute l’aguille desoz le leu que tu tiens a ta main, et la fai percier, et i ait I fil double, si que tu le trais de l’autre costeit;	And if the abscess is due to the size of the vein, you must hold with your hand what you can of the abscess and all its skin, then push the needle underneath the place that you are holding in your hand, make it pierce through, and have a double thread so that you can pull it out from the other side.
puis lie l’aposteme, si com je t’ai dit, ou liien de l’une de II pars as II chiés dou fil;	Then bind the abscess, as I have told you, with a bandage from one side of two parts to the other shoulder.
et se tu doutes que li filz n’isse fuer, si i reboute une autre aguille a tout I fil desoz tout l’aposteme a l’incision de la premiere aguille, et estraint les filz en IIII leus;	And if you doubt that the thread will not hold, push another needle through all of the thread underneath the abscess to the incision of the first needle, and tighten both threads in four places.
puis cope l’aposteme tant que li superfluitez en isse, puis cope la superfluiteit dou keur et laisse ceu qui est liiez;	Then cut the abscess until all surplus matter comes out of it, then excise any redundant heart tissue and leave that which is attached.
puis met sus I drapeil moilliet en vin et en oile, puis li amenistre cures de tentes et d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then apply moistened bandages with wine and oil, then treat it with tenting and ointments until it is healed.
des apostemes des ners	Of abscesses from nerves
Ausi com aposteme vienent en l’artere et en la voine, vienent aposteme as ners quant il sont ferut, ou par trop grant travail, et semblans choses.	Likewise abscesses occur in arteries and veins, abscesses form on nerves when they are injured or through excessive hard work, and similar things.
Et ceu avient plus sovent as adjutoires et as dois et en toz leus ou il ait jointures, et c’est I grief apostemes, et sa color semble la color dou cors, et est em plusors dispositions sens dolor;	And this occurs more often in the shoulders and hands, where there are joints, and it is a grievous abscess, its colour like that of the body, and it causes pain in various states.
et quant on l’estraint forment, si sent li malaides dolor, et n’est mie em parfont dou cors, mais desoz lou keur;	And when it is tightly constricted, the patient feels pain, and it is not in a perfect part of the body but beneath the heart.
et muet bien de toutes pars, et ne va ne avant ne arrier, ne desoz ne desus, et celui qui est en jointures ne covient mie coper par fer:	And it moves well in all directions, neither forward nor backward, downward nor upward; and that which is in the joints should not be cut with an iron instrument.
par aventure i vanroit contraction;	Perchance there would be constriction.
et cil qui est ou chief ou ou front, fent le cuir au spatumile.	And that which is at the head or forehead, make an incision with the spatula.
Se li apostemes est petis, si le tien a unes tenailles, et le cope en sa racine;	If the abscess is small, hold it with some tongs and cut its root;
et s’il est grans, si le sospent a l’oncine, et l’escorche, puis l’oste et assemble la plaie a la costure, et lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it is large, suspend it with the hook and peel its skin, then remove it and sew up the wound, treating it until it heals.
des grosses boces pendans	Large boils hanging down.
Aucune fois avient en ventres et ne mie autre part thelul, et est une maladie qui est apelee «funge» par la semblance d’aus, et est li racine subtilz, et li chiez gros;	Occasionally there is an eruption on bellies and nowhere else like pimples, and it is a disease called "fungus" due to its resemblance to mushrooms, with subtle roots and large heads.
et en i a de petis et de mout grans;	And there are some small and very large ones;
et je vis I home qui en avoit II ou ventre qui estoient plus semblans a funges que ai autre chose, et n’i avoit point de difference, et estoient blanc, et avoient menue racine, et estoient jai fendut, et en corroit adés moistor.	And I saw a man who had two on his belly which were more like mushrooms than anything else, and there was no difference, they were white, and had fine roots, and were light green split open, and moisture came out of them immediately.
Je les copai et trovai en l’un XVIII onces pesant, et en l’autre VI З., et li ovraiges en l’incision si est que tu regardes se li malaides est moistes, et li color de l’artelul est blainche et moiste et de subtil racine;	I cut them and found that one weighed eighteen ounces, and the other six pounds, and the work in this incision is such that you consider if the patient is moist, and the color of the substance is white and moist with a delicate root;
si le cope au spatumile large, et soient en ta presence li cautere au feu.	If you cut it with a broad spatula, let the fire cautery be in your presence.
Car au taillier vient maintes fois trop grans decorremens de sanc, et se li sans te vaint, si te haste donques dou cauterizer;	For when cutting it often causes too much blood to flow, and if the blood defeats you, then hurry up and cauterize.
et se tu vois le malaide espoanteit et paourous de l’incision dou fer, si prent I fil de plonc bien fait, et en lie l’artelul si com nos avons dit, et le laisse II jors;	and if you see the patient frightened and fearful of the iron incision, then take a well-made linen thread, and bind it to the wrist as we have said, leaving it for two days.
et puis le restraint, et ne cesser d’estraindre lou fil de plonc tant qu’il cope l’artelul, et chiece par lui sens travail;	then restrain them, and do not cease tightening the linen thread until it reaches the wrist, and each time by its motion.
et se les racines sont grosses, si a paour au coper meismement por le ventre, mais tu em pues bien coper la moitiet, puis le cauterize qu’il ne reviegne;	and if the roots are thick, there is fear of cutting them especially in the belly, but you may well cut half, then cauterize it so that it does not grow back.
puis cure la plaie, et garde que tu ne coper le thelul qui est de fuxe color et de povre sens et de lait regart.	then treat the wound, and make sure you do not cut the tendon which is of a light colour and poor texture like milk.
Car c’est uns apostemes enchancrez, et je venrai a la cure de chancre ci aprés.	For this is an abscess aggravated, and I will come to the treatment of cancer thereafter.
quant li boude ist fuer	when it breaks open at once.
Se li apparance de la boude vient par cautere de plaie ou de fendure de syfac, et est sus le ventre et en ist aucuns des bouez, si com il avient en autres routures, ou de sanc qui cort de voines ou d’arteres selonc ceu qui est devant, ou de ventositeit;	If the appearance of swelling arises from a cauterization for a wound or incision on an abscess, and it is on the belly and some of the bowels are involved, as occurs in other injuries, due to blood flowing from veins or arteries according to what has been mentioned before, or because of windiness
et se c’est par la routure dou syfac et par l’issue dou bouel, si est li color de l’aposteme semblans a la color dou cors, et est legiere chose sens dolor, et apert de diverse issue.	And if it is due to the rupture of an abscess and discharge from the bowel, then the colour of the abscess resembles that of flesh, and it presents as a mild condition without pain, appearing with various discharges.
Et se c’est por l’issue de l’intestine, adonques est il plus divers, et quant on le presse a ses dois si se repont, et puis revient, et par aventure si est sarrez, et agrandist mout a l’entree dou bain et por fort travail.	And if it is due to an outbreak of the intestine, then it becomes more diverse, and when you press it with your fingers it will retract, but come back, or possibly it would be tightened, and greatly enlarged at the entrance of the bath after strong labor.
Et se c’est por moistor, c’est legiere chose, et apert bien quant tu le presses a ta main, ne ne constraint mie;	And if it is due to moisture, it presents as a minor issue, which becomes evident when you press it with your hand but does not require restriction.
et se c’est por sanc, si apert par ces signes li apostemes gros et dur, et est fichiez selonc une quantiteit;	And if it is due to blood, it presents with these signs: large, hard abscesses, and it manifests in a particular quantity.
et se c’est por ventositeit, si est souef au tochier, et li ovraiges si est que tu regarde se li apparance est por le sanc de l’artere, ou de la voine, ou ventositeit.	And if it is due to windiness, it is soft to the touch, and the work [treatment] consists of determining whether it appears related to arterial blood, venous blood, or windiness.
Si covient que tu laisses la cure.	You should leave the treatment alone.
Car il en a doutance et paor, si com je t’ai dit ou chapistre des apostemes, por l’artere et por la voine.	For he has doubt and fear, as I told you in the chapter on abscesses, regarding arteries and veins.
Et se li apparance est por l’intestine ou lou boueil, si covient que tu comandes au malaide qu’il teigne son alaine, et soit estendus tout drois, puis seigne d’enche tout entor la boude;	And if it appears related to the intestines or stomach, you must instruct the patient to hold their breath and lie completely straight, then bleed them around the navel entirely.
puis le comande a gesir sovin entre tes mains, puis va entor le leu que tu as signiet a tout le spatumile, puis estent la moitiet de l’aposteme au desus a tout le grant uncine;	Then have them lie frequently between your hands, then go around the marked place with all your fingers, then extend half of the abscess above to just before the big toe.
puis le lie entor d’un fil fort, ou d’une corde de fort soie fermement, et soit li nous dou liien assolz;	Then bind it around with a strong thread or a sturdy silk cord firmly, and let the knot be on top.
puis oevre la moitiet de l’aposteme estendut sus le liien, et i boute ton doit indice, et quier l’intestine;	Then operate on half of the abscess extended along the tendon, insert your index finger, and search for the intestine.
se tu le trueves pris dou liien, si le deslie, et boute l’intestine au defuer dou ventre;	If you find it trapped by the tendon, untie it and push the intestine outside of the belly.
et se tu trueves le boueil, si le prent a l’oncine, et en cope la superfluiteit;	And if you find the mouth, grab it with tweezers and cut off any excess.
et se li artere te fait contraire, ou li voine, si vai belement entor, puis revien a ton ovraige et pren II aguilles, et i boute II fors filz, et boute les II aguilles entor ceu que tu as fait en crois que tu feis percier;	And if the artery or vein opposes you, go carefully around it, then return to your work and take two needles, insert two lengths of thread, and thread the two needles through what you have pierced.
puis estrain l’aposteme en IIII leus sus les aguilles, et se tu vues, oste les aguilles, et laisse lou leu tant qu’il porrisse, et chiece li char morte par soi;	Then draw the abscess four fingers-breadth above the needles, and if you see fit, remove the needles, leave the place until it rots, and cut away the dead flesh as needed.
ou tu la cope quant elle iert subtiliie et porrie, puis le cure de ceu qu’il covient, et cheve l’aposteme si com nos avons dit;	Where you cut it when it is thin and rotten, then treat what needs to be treated, and remove the abscess as we have said.
et estrai le sanc ou la moistor que tu trueves, puis cure le leu de ceu qu’il couvient, et soude le leu.	And drain the blood or moisture that you find, then treat the area as required, and weld the place.
dou chancre	From chancre
Nos avons dit en la division les semblances de chancre, et coment on i doit ovrer par medicines, et coment on doit eschuer la cure de fer;	We have spoken about the similarities of cancer in the division, and how one must operate with medicines, and how one should avoid iron-based treatments;
et disons le chancre enjanreit en la marris, et grant cautele a en la cure, et dirent li ancien que quant chancres est en leu ou on le puet raier si com chancre qui est em mameles, et en la cuixe, et en semblans leus, et le doit tout oster quant il est en l’encomencement;	And we say that cancer engrained in the breast and requires great caution when treating it. The ancients said that when cancers are found where they can be scraped off like cancer of the mammary glands or on the thighs, and similar areas, one must remove all of them at their onset.
et quant il est grans et anciens, si ne covient mie que tu l’aproches, car je n’en poi onques nul saner;	and when it is large and old, you must not approach it, for I have never been able to cure anyone of it.
ne nulz n’en sana onques devant moi.	no one has ever healed from it before me.
Et li ovraiges, quant il est en leu ou on le puet oster, si com nos avons dit, est que tu purge aucune fois le malaide de cole noire;	And the work, when it is in place or can be removed, as we have said, is to purge the patient once with black bile;
puis le fai sainier s’il ait manifeste repletion, puis afaite le malaide I boin leu por faire l’ovraige;	then make him bleed if there is evident congestion, then prepare the patient in a good place to perform the operation;
puis giete tes oncines ou chancre, et le cheve de toutes pars, et l’oste de toutes pars sens rien laissier;	then remove your tumors or cancerous growths, shave his head completely, and take it away entirely without leaving anything behind.
et laisse corre le sanc tout fuer, et espreint bien le leu a ta main ou a aucune chose, et se li decorremens de sanc te fait contraire de l’incision de l’artere ou de la voine, si le cauterize tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	allow the blood to flow freely and ensure you have thoroughly cleaned the place with your hand or an object, if the direction of blood flow opposes that of incision of the artery or vein, then cauterize it until the bleeding stops.
puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat with another treatment until it is healed.
de ydropisie	From dropsy
Nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’idropisie, et en queil maniere li assemblee de l’aigue est faite, et les signes de chescune semblance, et la cure qui est faite par medicines, et cele qui est curee par fer:	We have mentioned in the division the similarities of dropsy, and how the collection of water is formed, and the signs of each resemblance, and the treatment that is done with medication, and those that are treated with iron:
si est eclites soulement;	Thus it is written only.
et ne doit on touchier de fer en ces II semblances:	And one should not use iron in these two resemblances:
c’est a savoir, tympanites et yposarche, car c’est mortelz chose;	That is to say, tympanites and yposarche, for they are mortal affairs;
donques quant tu medicines ceste semblance de ydropisie qui est apelee «eclites» de medicines, et li cure ne profite, si regarde se li malaides est foibles, ou s’il ait autre maladie que ydropisie, si com toust et solution de ventre et semblans choses;	Therefore, when you treat this type of dropsy called "eclites" with medication, and the treatment is not effective, consider if the patient is weak or if they have another illness besides dropsy, such as diarrhea and stomach disorders, and similar conditions.
si n’i touchier de fer, car il i a doutance;	If you touch iron, for there is doubt.
et se tu vois le malaide de fort vertut, et il n’a autre maladie que ydropisie soulement, et il n’est mie trop jones ne trop vielz, si dois ensi ovrer:	And if you see the patient of strong constitution, and he has no other illness but solely dropsy, and he is neither too young nor too old, then you must operate like this:
lieve le malaide droit sus tes mains, et li ministres presse le ventre em boutant l’aigue a la plus basse partie dou pis, puis pren le spatumile espinous selonc ceste forme:	Lift the patient directly above your hands, and have an assistant press on the belly by pushing water to the lowest part of the abdomen; then take the sharp-pointed spatula in this manner:
Et soit trenchans de II pars.	And divide [it] into two parts.
a pointe, et toutevoie ne soit mie si entrans qu’il puist venir jusc’a l’intestine quant on le fiche ens, et ne le puist blecier;	With the pointed end, yet it must not be so sharp that it can reach the intestine when inserted, and might cause injury.
puis regarde se li ydropisie est enjanree devers les intestines:	Then examine whether the dropsy is caused by fluid around the intestines.
si covient que tu fendes ensus de la boude III dois droit desoz sus lou poignil;	So you must cut above the bump three fingers directly above the wrist.
et se li ydropisie est por la maladie dou foie, si soit ta fendure au senestre de la boude III dois;	and if the dropsy is caused by liver disease, let your incision be to the left of the bump three fingers.
et se c’est por la miuce, si soit a destre, et ne covient mie que li malaides gise sus la fendure que les superfluitez ne corrent a celui foible leu;	and if it is due to wetness, let the incision be on the right side, and it is not suitable for the patient to lie over the wound so that excess fluid does not run into that weak spot.
puis perce tout le cuir a l’estrument, et le boute, et lieve ta main a tout le spatumile entre le cuir et le syfac ausi com en escorchant a la quantiteit d’une ungle ou enqui entor;	Then pierce through the skin with an instrument, push it in, and lift your hand up along the spatium bile between the skin and the fascia just like when you are skinning something to the depth of a fingernail or so.
puis perce lou syfac tant que li spatumile viegne au leu vuit, et c’est li leus de l’aigue, puis le trai fuer, et i boute cest estrument de coi ci est li forme:	Next, pierce the fascia until you reach an empty space; this is where water gathers. Then draw it out forcefully and insert this instrument into that spot, which should be shaped like this:
Et est semblans a une caine d’argent subtil, et est d’arain ou d’archaut legier, et a en la partie desoz I petit pertus;	And it is similar to a slender silver tube, and made of light brass or copper, with a small hole at the bottom part.
et ou costeit d’une part, III pertus;	and on one side three holes;
et II d’autre part, et I d’autre;	and two on the other side, and one more.
et est li chiés tailliez si com une penne, et c’est li forme de l’incision dont li escrivains taille la penne:	and the head is carved like a feather, which is similar to how scribes cut their quill pens.
au chief desus est li alemele, si que quant li estrumens vient a l’aigue, si dessent maintenant sus l’estrument;	at its top is the handle, so that when the instrument reaches the water, it now lowers onto the tool.
vuide la donques la moitiet ou la tierce part, car se tu en vuides plus qu’il ne covient en celle houre, par aventure si muert li malaides por la resolution de son esperit de l’arme, ou il chiet paumez, ou il aproche a la mort;	empty it half or a third of the way because if you empty any more than necessary at that time, perhaps the patient will die due to loss of spirit from the blood let out, or they faint, or they near death.
mais en vuide selonc la quantiteit de sa vertut, et selonc ceu que les dispositions de la vertut dou malaide signifient, et ses poulz;	but empty it according to its quantity of virtue, and according to what the patient's constitution signifies about his virtue, and his pulses.
puis trai l’estrument et retien l’aigue, et elle est retenue maintenant por le keur qui estoupe le pertus qui est sus le syfac, de coi j’ai parleit, que tu perces selonc ceste maniere;	then draw out the instrument and retain the water, and it is retained now for the heart which blocks the orifice that I mentioned, when you pierce it in this manner;
puis rencomence l’estrument l’autre jor, se tu vois le malaide soffrant ceu, et trai de l’aigue une petite quantiteit;	then use the instrument again the next day, if you see the patient suffer thus, and draw out a small quantity of water;
fai ce aucun jor, et te garde de foloier tant qu’il ni demore mais c’un poc d’aigue.	do this each day, and take care not to draw out too much water at once but only a little bit of it.
Et se tu doutes sus le malaide, et tu i lais mout d’aigue, si le cure de la sepulture ou sablon chaut, et par mout sueir ou bain et au soleil, et se teigne de boivre;	and if you are in doubt about the patient, and leave too much water inside them, it will overheat their burial shroud or hot sand, and through excessive sweating or bathing and under the sun, and prohibit from drinking;
et le cure de medicines desiccatives tant qu’il soit sanez, et cauterize sus l’estomac et sus lou foie et sus l’esplen aprés l’estraction de l’aigue, si com j’ai dit devant.	And treat with drying medicines until healed, then cauterize over the stomach and on the liver and spleen after extracting the water, as I said before.
de l’estopement de la verge	Of the stopping of the penis.
Aucune fois naissent enfant qui n’ont point de pertus en la verge, ou li pertus est petis, ou il n’est mie en son leu.	Sometimes children are born who do not have an opening in their penis, or the opening is very small, or it is not in its proper place.
Si le covient tantost qu’il n’aist percier a tout I spatumile molt subtil selonc ceste forme:	It must be pierced as soon as possible with a very thin spatula, following this form:
puis met ou pertus I clo subtil de plonc, et le lie et le tien ensi III jors ou IIII et quant il vuet faire urine, si soit ostez li clos, et faice urine, et puis li remet;	Then apply a small, fine tube to the bladder opening, and bind it, keeping it in place for three or four days. When he wishes to urinate, remove the tube, let him urinate, and then replace it.
et par aventure nen i couvient point, car li urine qui vient fuer ne lou laisse close.	And perhaps this is not necessary, for the urine that comes out will not leave the tube closed.
Cil de cui li pertus est petis, si est medicinez dou clo de plonc, si com nos avons dit, si s’eslargera.	If the orifice is small then this (i.e., the lead plug) has been medicated as we have said; it will enlarge.
Cil qui n’ont mie le pertus en lor leu sont bleciet, car aucun naissent qui ont le pertus au chief de la verge, por coi il ne puient pissier avant s’il ne lievent lor verge en haut;	Those who do not have the tube in its proper place are harmed, as none are born with a tube at the tip of their penis, which is why they cannot urinate without lifting their penis upwards.
et ne pueent enjanrer por ceu que li matiere ne puet venir jusc’a la marris, et c’est une male maladie.	And they cannot conceive because the matter cannot reach the marrow, and this is a severe illness.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos, puies estent le chief de la verge et le cope ausi com la taille d’une penne, si ke li pertus chiece em mileu, si com il covient;	And the method of treatment is that the patient lies on their back, then stretch out the head with a rod and the leg as well, like the length of a feather, so that the hole opens in the middle, just as it should be.
et te garde de decorrement de sanc qui i vient maintes fois, et s’il avient, si l’estainche de ceu qui estainche sanc, et cure la plaie tant qu’il soit sanez.	And take care to prevent the loss of blood which often happens, and if it occurs, stop it with something that stops bleeding, and treat the wound until it is healed.
des pustules de la verge	Pimples on the penis
Maintes fois vienent cist albathe en la verge, et est une apparance de char laide;	This inflammation often occurs in the leg, and it appears as an ugly sore.
et en i a malignes et non malignes;	And there are both malignant and non-malignant ones.
si covient que tu les preignes a I oncine subtil, et les cope et munde toutes, puis met sus coton moilliet en oignement egiptien;	You must take them with a thin lancet, cut and clean them all, then apply moistened cotton with Egyptian ointment.
puis le cure d’oignement diafinicon tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat it with refined ointment until it is healed.
Et se li albathe est maligne, de pute color et depuant, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere.	And if the cancer is malignant, of a foul colour and stinking, you must treat it with cautery.
Quant tu l’as copeit, et se li albathe est en som la verge, et en ait partie dedens la peil et partie defuer, si covient que tu oste l’albathe qui est dedens premier;	When you have cut it, and if the inflammation is on top of the shaft, and part of it is inside the skin and part outside, then you must first remove the inflammation that is inside.
et quant il est soudez, si le cure defuer.	And when it is sealed, treat it from the outside.
Car quant tu le cures ensamble, si n’est mie asseurez li chiez de la verge qu’il ne soit perciez, et vient noiror et corruption en son la verge et ou coion;	For when you treat them together, the head of the shaft is not secure and may be pierced, causing blackening and decay in the head of the shaft and glans.
si covient chever tout ceu qui est noir et corrumput, puis lie sus l’emplaustre de miel et de farine qui soit fait d’escorce de poumes grenates et de veces, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	You must cut away all that is black and corrupt, then bind it with a plaster made of honey and flour which is made from pomegranate bark and figwort, then treat it with other treatments until it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si amenistre le cautere lunaire selonc ceste forme:	And if bleeding occurs, apply the lunar cautery as follows:
Li cauteres si aide as II dispositions ensamble:	Cauterization assists the two positions together:
c’est asavoir, au decorrement de sanc, et a la corruption;	That is to say, in draining blood and corruption;
et se li chiés de la verge est corrumpus et retrais, si covient que tu boutes ou conduit de la verge une cainne de plonc, et pisse li malaides parmi;	And if the head of the penis is corrupted and retracted, you must insert a plumb-line into the penis and urinate the patient out.
et quant li pelz iert aerse au chief de la verge qui avient a ces qui n’ont mie esteit circoncis, ou il avient por plaie ou por aposteme, si covient donques que tu l’escorches a I estrument cheveit, tant que li liiens soit desliiez, et soit delivrez li chiez de la verge de toutes pars;	And when the skin is stuck to the head of the penis which happens in those who have not been circumcised, or there is a wound or an abscess, then you must therefore remove the skin with a sharp instrument, so that the tie is loosened and the glans of the penis is freed from all sides.
et se c’est grief chose de deviser ceu, si covient que tu l’escorches a I spatumile aucun poc dou chief de la verge et de la peil;	and if this is an important thing to discuss, then you must flay it with a spatula at any pock on the head of the penis and the skin.
puis dessevre belement entre II, et i met I subtil drapeil de lin moilliet an aigue froide, qu’il n’aerse derechief.	then carefully separate it between two [fingers], and put one thin damp linen cloth in cold water, so that it does not dry again.
de la circoncision	Of circumcision.
Circoncision n’est mie desliemens de continuation si com les autres plaies;	circumcision is not like the separation of continuity as with other wounds;
toutevoie quant nos faison ceste oevre de nostre volenteit, et proprement as enfans, si est mestier que nos faisiens la millor oevre, et la plus legiere a salut.	nevertheless when we do this work of our own will, and especially with children, it is necessary that we perform the best work, and the most gentle for their well-being.
Je dis que li ancien ne dirent mie la circoncision de lor enfans, car il n’en usent mie en lor loi, et n’en avons mais que ceu que nos avons aquis par experiment.	I say that the ancients did not practice circumcision on their children, for it was not used in their law, and we only have what we have acquired through experience.
Car j’ai veut la plus grant partie des maistres et des sainors qui faisoient circumcision entor I dal, et as forces, et a tout une novacule;	For I have seen the majority of masters and elders who performed circumcisions around one day, with forceps, and with all [their] instruments.
si fuioit li keurs car il i a II toiles, et par aventure si cope on celi desus et demore celle desoz.	If the heart were pierced by two wounds, and perhaps one of them is closed while the other remains open.
Or la recovient coper, et est li dolor double, et a la mundification qui est dou dal n’est mie asseuree li pointe dou membre;	Now it must be cauterized again, and the pain doubles, and during treatment the point of the member is not securely held;
et a la mundification de l’ungle par aventure eschaipe li fer, et corront l’uevre, et maintes fois naissent ensi qu’il n’ont mestier de mundification et je l’ai veut.	And during the treatment of the nail, perhaps the iron escapes and ruins the operation, and often they need no further treatment, and I say so.
De la mondification qui est faite as forces a tout le liien de fil ai je troveit la bonteit de l’experiment, car les forces taillent justement ausi bien desus com desoz.	Of the cleaning that is done with threads, I have found goodness in this experiment, for the threads cut as cleanly above as below.
Car quant tu presses ta main, si tailles igalment en I tout soul tens;	For when you press your hand with equal force on all sides, you cut cleanly straight through it;
mais que li filz soit bien estrois entor lou cuir;	But let the string be tightly wound around the skin;
et soit li maniere dou premier ovraige si est que tu faices penser l’enfant, s’il entent, que tu ne li fais fuer que liier le fil entor la verge tant soulement, et pues le fai esjoir en toutes les manieres que tu pues;	And let the manner of this first treatment be such that you make the child believe, if he is alert, that you are not going to force him to anything more than bind the string around his penis, and then you can have him sit in all the ways you wish;
puis le fai ester entre tes mains tout droit, et repont les forces entre tes mains ou desoz tes piez que li enfes ne les voie, ne aucun des estrumens;	Then make him stand between your hands straight, and shield the instruments from his view by covering them with your hands or placing them below your feet.
puis boute ta main a la verge et souffle ou keur, et la trai en haut tant que li chiés de la verge soit ens;	Then press your hand against the penis and blow into its core, drawing it upwards until the head of the penis is encased within you.
puis la mundifie bien de l’ordure qui i est assemblee, puis lie le leu signiet d’un fil double, puis la lie desoz I poc a I autre liien;	Clean it well of the dirt that has accumulated there, then bind its base with a thick thread, and secure this beneath another bond.
et la tien as II dois par la seconde lieeure au pouchet et au doit indice, et cope entre les II liiens, puis lieve le keur desus hastanment et trai le chief de la verge;	Hold it at two points by the second and third fingers, and grasp between the two bonds, then lift the core upwards gently and draw out the head of the penis.
puis laisse corre le sanc poc et poc, car c’est li muedres;	Allow blood to flow freely from it, for this is its medicine.
et met poudre sus et sus la poudre I drapeil glueit d’un moieuf d’uef cuit destempreit d’aigue rose, confit avec oile roset boin et fres, et lou laisse sus jusc’a l’autre jor, et le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and apply powder on top and over the powder a cloth glued with a cooked egg yolk tempered with rose water, mixed with good and fresh rosemary oil, leave it on until the next day, and treat it with another treatment until it is healed.
Li forme des forces a la mundification si est ceste:	The form of the force for the cleansing is as follows:
li dui chiés soient tenves et soient trenchans, et soient li chiés ausi grant com li mainche igalment:	the two blades should be turned and sharpened, and the blades should also be as long as the handles evenly:
li error de la mundification si est quant li keurs dedens fuit a l’incision;	the mistake of the cleansing is when the heart within escapes through the incision;
donques il covient que tu l’estendes a ton ungle, ainsois que li leus faice aposteme;	therefore you must extend it to your nail, otherwise the flesh will become abscessed;
et le cope igalment, et se tu ne lou pues tenir a ton ungle, si le tien as tenailles, et puis le cope.	And cut it evenly, and if you cannot hold it with your nail, then hold it with pliers, and then cut it.
Et s’il trespassent III jors, et ceu qui est desoz la verge est enflez, si le laisse tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et l’escorche legierement;	And if it exceeds three days, and that which is below the rod is swollen, let it be until the hot abscess is soothed, and gently peel off the skin.
si le cope si com tu pues mues, et te garde de la partie de la verge, ce ne li nuira niant.	then cut it as much as you can manage, and be careful not to damage the part of the rod, this will cause no harm.
Cure donques le leu de choses soudans plaie de poudre, que nos avons dit ou traitier des poudres, et s’on cope dou keur outre mesure, et il va au desus, si ne nuira point;	Treat the place of fresh wounds with powder, as we have said in the treatise on powders, and if it is cut from the heart too much, and goes above it, it will cause no harm.
cure le donques, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	treat it, as we have said, until it is healed.
dou retenement de l’urine	treatment of urine retention
Li retenue de l’urine si est d’opilation de piere, ou de sanc congeleit, ou de bowe, ou de char nee, ou de semblans choses, que nos avons dit en la division;	The retention of urine is caused by the obstruction of stones, or frozen blood, or a tumor, or flesh born anew, or similar things as we have mentioned in the classification.
et se li urine n’est desliie , et tu vois estre la retenue por la piere qui est jai ou col de la vessie, si covient que li malaides soit corbés sus ses genoulz;	And if the urine is not released and you see that the retention is caused by stones in the bladder or its neck, then it is necessary for the patient to lean forward on their knees.
et li soient mis li piez sor le dos, et estende son ventre de la partie desus lou dos, et restraigne li malaides s’alainne tant com il puet;	And his feet should be placed on his back, stretching out his abdomen from the upper part of his back, and hold the patient's arm as much as you can.
et adonques est constrains li colz de la vessie a l’expression de la piere au desus, por coi li urine est desliie e;	And thus the neck of the bladder is forced to express the stone above it, which then releases the urine.
et s’elle ne vient, si com nos avons dit, et li malaides sent grant dolor, si covient que tu i aministres extraction a tout l’estrument qui est apelez «siringue», de coi ci est li forme:	and if it does not come out, as we have said, and the patient feels great pain, then you must perform an extraction with all the instruments called 'syringe', of which this is the form:
et soit d’argent subtilz legiere chevee, si com li penne d’un oiseil;	and it should be made of fine, light silver, like the feathers of a bird;
et soit li caine d’une palme de lonc et demie, et soit subtilz au chief.	and it should have a handle one palm long, and be delicate at the top.
Et li maniere de l’issue de l’urine si est que tu pren I fil double, et lie au chief I poc de laine ou de couton, et boute le chief dou fil dedens la siringue;	The method of urine extraction is that you take a double thread, and tie at its end a small bag made from wool or cotton, then push the other end of the thread into the syringe.
et cope la superfluiteit de la lainne et le boute jusc’au chief de la siringue, puis oint la siringue d’oile ou de burre et d’aubin d’uef, et fai seoir le malaide sus I siege, et li arose la vessie et la verge d’oile moiste et d’oile d’olive et d’aigue tede;	cut away any excess wool and push it all the way up to the end of the syringe, then grease the syringe with oil or butter mixed with egg white, and have the patient sit on a seat. Oil their bladder and penis with moist oil, olive oil and warm water;
puis met legierement la siringue en la verge, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la verge, puis double la verge desus devers la boude;	Then gently insert the syringe into the penis until it reaches the root of the penis, then bend the penis upwards towards the scrotum.
puis boute la siringue avant jusc’a la vessie, et la sente li malaides venir jusc’a la chose vuide, et ceu n’est mie fait selonc cest ordre fuer que por ceu que li conduis ou elle vait est tors;	Then push the syringe forward until it reaches the bladder, and let the patient feel its passage until the action is complete, but this method isn't ideal as the instrument guiding it into place is bent.
puis estent le fil a tout la laine poc et poc, et li urine en suit la laine, puis l’estrai fuer, et fai corre l’urine;	Then stretch the thread through all the wool, back and forth, and the urine will follow along the wool, then remove it quickly, and make the urine flow.
et rencomence la siringue tant que li vessie soit vuidie, et soit aligiez li malaides.	Repeat the process with the syringe until the bladder is empty, and ease the patient's discomfort.
des maladies de la vessie	Of bladder diseases
Quant escorcheures ou sanc vient en la vessie, ou porriture i est assemblee, et tu i vues distiller aigues et medicines, si fai a tout l’estrument qui est apellé «clepsedre», et c’est li forme:	When scalds or blood enter the bladder, and putrefaction gathers there, if you wish to distill water and medicine into it, use an instrument called a "clepsydra," which is shaped like this:
Elle est close, et si a III pertus:	It is closed, and has three openings.
II d’une part, et I d’autre, si com tu vois;	II on one side, and I on the other, as you see;
et li leus chevez par coi li medicine cort soit telz qu’il estoupe bien la verge sens adition, si c’on em puisse traire la moistor, et bouter quant mestier est;	and the white hairs by which the doctor cuts may be such that they stop well the vein without addition, so that one can draw out the moisture, and sew when necessary;
et quant tu vues giter tes medicines en la vessie, met le chief dou keusteur en la moistor, et trai au traiant qui est ens;	and when you see your medicines fall into the bladder, place the head of the vessel in the moisture, and draw out what is inside while draining it;
si trairas la moistor au kesteur, et puis reboute fort le traiant ens;	you will draw out the moisture with the vessel, and then sew up strongly the opening within;
si entrera li moistors ens, et venra a la vessie maintenant, si que li malaides la sentira;	so the moisture will enter inside, and come to the bladder now, so that the patient will feel it;
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil dont on clisterize la vessie:	and this is the way of the subtle enema by which we enema the bladder;
si est ci:	For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and even; and if they prick at their base, hold the eyes steady so they do not move until they grow.
Et est d’argent ou d’archaut, et est li chiés plus haut;	And it is made of silver or iron, and the head is higher up.
et desoz a I sein ou li liiens chiet;	it drops to the side where the ligament falls;
puis pren une vessie de mouton et i met la moistor dont tu vues clisterizer la vessie, puis la lie entre les II seins forment d’un boin fil double, et chaufe I poc celle moistor sus le feu;	then take a sheep's bladder and fill it with the moisture you wish to use for enemas, then tie it between the two breasts with a good thick thread, and heat the pot containing this moisture over the fire;
puis boute le chief dou clistere en la verge, puis estrain ta main sus la vessie a tout la moistor avenanment, tant que li malaides sente que celle moistor est jai venue a la vessie;	then insert the head of the syringe into the urethra, then squeeze your hand over the bladder with all its moisture gently until you feel that this moisture has reached the bladder.
et se tu n’as la vessie, si pren une piece de parchemin, et en fai I cercle, et le perce rondement entor;	and if you don't have the bladder, then take a piece of parchment paper, make it into a circle and pierce it roundly all around.
puis boute I fil fort en ces pertus, puis assemble le cercle si com on assemble I dal, et met dedens ceu que tu vues d’oile et de moistor et d’aigue, et le lie en l’estrument;	Then push the thread strongly into these holes, then assemble the circle as one would a thimble, and put inside whatever you want of oil, moisture and water, and tie it to the instrument.
et fai si com tu as fait de la vessie, de presser a ta main tant que li moistor veigne a la vessie.	And do as you did with the bladder, pressing it with your hand until moisture comes to the bladder.
de la piere	of the stone
Nos avons jai dit en la division les manieres de piere, et l’estraction ensamble medicines;	We have already spoken of the types of stones in the division, and their extraction along with medical treatments;
et ai dit la difference entre la piere enjanree as rains, et toz les signes, et en queil piere on doit ovrer de taille;	And I have explained the distinction between gallstones caused by bile, and all their symptoms, and in which stones one must operate with cutting;
et en la vessie, et en la verge;	And for bladder stones, and those in the urethra;
et je le vos dirai apertement et briément.	And I shall tell you plainly and briefly.
Je dis que li piere qui est enjanree en la vessie si avient plus sovent as enfans, et c’est signe que li aigue saut de la vessie semblans a aigue en sa subtiliteit;	I say that the stone which is engendered in the bladder occurs more often in children, and it is a sign that the water flows from the bladder resembling water in its subtlety;
et i apert harene, et graite li malaides sa verge, et li pent maintes fois, et puis enroidist;	and it appears rough, and the patient feels grit in his penis, and he urinates many times, and then becomes blocked;
et a mout de ces saut li fondemens;	and often these cause the foundations to fail;
et est legiere li sanation des enfans jusqu’il ont IIII ans, et est mout grief en viellars, et est as jones moiene, a ces qui sont entre jonesce et viellece;	and the healing is light for children up to four years old, and it is very difficult in the elderly, and it is moderate for those who are young adults, for those between youth and old age;
et est li cure plus legiere de ces qui ont la piere grans, que de ces qui l’ont petite.	And the treatment is easier for those with large stones than for those with small ones.
Et quant nos venons a la cure, si couvient premier mundifier le malaide per clistere, por traire tout le fiens qui est as intestines.	And when we come to the treatment, it is necessary first to cleanse the patient with an enema, in order to draw out all the bile that is in the intestines.
Car il encombre aucune fois a querir la piere.	For sometimes it hinders the removal of the stone.
Puis prenez le malaide par les piez, et lou deboutez et movez au desoz, si que li piere dessende au parfont de la vessie, et saille aucune fois dou leu haut;	Then take the patient by the feet, lift them up, and move them downward, so that the stone descends to the bottom of the bladder, and sometimes it may come out on its own.
puis le fai seoir entre tes mains appareilliet, et ses mains soient desoz ses cuisses, si que li vessie soit toute declinans aval;	Have the patient sit between your prepared hands, with their hands placed below their thighs, so that the bladder is fully relaxed and extended downwards.
puis la quier et la touche dedens;	Then search for it and feel inside (the bladder).
se tu sens la piere en l’espaice, si te haste maintenant de taillier sus la piere.	If you feel the stone in your grasp, then hurry now to cut into the stone (to extract it).
Et s’elle ne chiet au touchier dou tout, si moille ton doi indice d’oile de la main senestre, se li malaides est enfes, ou ton doi moien, se li malaides est jovencelz acomplis;	And if it does not fall out upon touching, then moisten your index finger with oil from the left hand if the patient is an infant, or with your middle finger if they are a young adult.
et le boute en son fondement, et quier la piere, et quant tu la sens a ton doi, si l’amoine au col de la vessie;	and push it into its base, seek out the stone, and when you feel it with your finger, apply pressure at the neck of the bladder;
puis presse sus a ton doi, et la boute au defuer lai ou tu vues taillier.	then press down with your finger, and push it outward from where you intend to cut.
Et comande au ministre qu’il presse la vessie a sa main, et li comande qu’il estende a sa main destre les coions en haut, et a sa main senestre oste le cuir qui est desoz les coions en la partie ou on fait la taille;	And instruct the assistant to press on the bladder with their hand, and tell them to stretch the testicles upwards with their right hand, and with their left hand remove the skin that is beneath the testicles in the area where the cut will be made;
puis i boute le spatumile copant, de coi ce est li forme:	then insert the spatoula, cutting with it, which is shaped like this:
Et fent entre ceu qui est entre les coions et le fondement, ne mie em mileu mais au costeit de la naige senestre;	And make an incision between what is between the testicles and the anus, not in the middle but on the left side of the perineum;
et soit drois sus la piere, et tes dois soit adés ou fondement, et soit li taille dou traver si qu’ele soit large par defuer, et dedens estroite, selonc la quantiteit de la piere, ne mie trop grans;	and be straight on the stone, and your fingers should be nearby at the foundation, and let the handle [of the tool] go across so that it is wide from above and narrow inside, according to the size of the stone, not too large.
par aventure la presse si li dois qui est ou fondement, qu’elle saut fuer sens travail;	perhaps if the press hits your fingers which are at the foundation it might be without work [i.e., useless];
et saiches qu’il i a teil piere ou il a angles, et marges:	and know that there is such stone which has angles and margins [i.e., sides]:
si est griés a issir;	it should be ground to come out [i.e, removed].
et si a teil qui est souez, semblans a une glant, et reonde, dont li issue est legiere.	and if there is some which is below, similar to an acorn, round, with only a small outlet.
A celi donques ou il a angles et marge, fai la taille plus grant;	To that one then which has angles and margins [sides], make the handle larger.
et s’elle ne saut, si covient que tu estraignes sus as tenailles qui sont ausi com une lime au chief, por mues estraindre la piere si qu’elle n’eschaipe;	and if she does not jump [out], then you must extract it with pliers which are like a file on the head, to squeeze and extract the stone so that it does not escape;
ou tu boute desoz li I estrument subtil corbé au chief;	or you push underneath [the instrument] an agile tool curved towards the head;
et se tu ne la pues engignier ensi, si eslarge I poc lou pertus, et se li sans decort, si l’estrainche de vitriole;	and if you cannot manipulate it in this way, then enlarge the hole with a lancet, and if blood flows [from it], extract it with vitriol;
et s’il i a plus d’une piere, si boute premier la plus grant au col de la vessie, puis cope sus, puis le trai fuer, et les petites aprés s’il en i a plusors.	and if there is more than one stone, push the largest first into the neck of the bladder, then cut above it, then pull hard, and the smaller ones after that if there are many.
Et s’elle est mout grans, si la covient soier, et faire plus grant plaie.	And if it is very large, you must take care of it, and make a larger wound.
Car II choses avienent au malaide:	For two things happen to the patient:
ou il muert, ou li urine vient adés par lai que li leus ne puet souder;	where he dies, or the urine flows back through the opening where the bone cannot fuse;
mais toutevoie t’efforce dou traire, ou dou debrisier as tenailles, tant que tu la traies par pieces;	but still, try to extract it by pulling or chiseling with pincers until you remove it in fragments;
et quant tu as acomplit ton oevre, si emple la plaie d’encens et d’aloe et de sanc de dragon, et l’estraint, et met par sus I drapeil moilliet en oile et en vin, ou en oile et en aigue rose et aigue froide, por apaisier l’aposteme chaut;	and once you have completed your work, fill the wound with incense, aloe, and dragon's blood, compress it, and apply a moist cloth soaked in oil and wine or oil, rosewater, and cold water to soothe the hot abscess;
puis resovine le malaide sus son col, et ne desliier lou lien jusc’au tier jor.	then have the patient rest on his collarbone, and do not loosen the binding until the third day.
Et quant tu le desliies, si arose mout bien lou leu d’oile et d’aigue, puis le cure d’oignement dyafinicon et d’oignement basilicon, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when you untie it, thoroughly wash the place with oil and water, then treat it with ointment of daffodil and basilicon ointment until it is healed.
Et se apostemes chaus vient en la plaie et corrosions, et congelemens de sanc en la vessie, et soit par ceu retenue li urine, qui est conue en teil maniere que sans saut avec l’urine:	And if hot abscesses develop in the wound with corrosion and blood clots in the bladder, retaining urine that is released together with it:
boutes donques ton doi en la plaie, et estrai celui sanc, car s’il i remaint, si corront la vessie, et la porrit;	Push your finger into the wound, and extract that blood, for if it remains, it will inflame the bladder and cause infection.
puis leve la plaie d’aigue et d’aisil et de seil, et li aide en toutes les manieres que tu seis, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then cleanse the wound with warm water and salt, and treat it in every way you know until it is healed.
et covient que toutes les oures que tu le cures, que tu li lie les II cuisses, et assemble les medicines sus le leu.	And ensure that during every treatment you bind his thighs together, applying the remedies directly to the affected area.
Et se li piere est petite, et ele est ou conduit de la verge, et fichie ens, et li urine ne puet issir;	And if the stone is small, situated in the urethra, impeding urination, insert it there and lodge it within.
si le cure de ceu que je dis ainsois, que tu lou tailles maintes fois, est on escusez de la taille per ceste cure.	Should the treatment I describe fail to work, providing grounds for cutting it out entirely, you may do so multiple times according to this procedure.
Je ai ja ce proveit ensi.	I have already proven this thus.
Pren I foret de fer selonc ceste forme et soit a III angles fichiees en I tison:	If you forge an iron tool according to this form, let it have three sharp edges like a spike:
puis pren I fil et lou lie entor la verge desoz la piere, si qu’ele ne puist venir arrier en la vessie;	Take a thread and tie it around the penis below the stone so that it cannot go back into the bladder;
puis boute le foret en la verge legierement, tant qu’il viegne a la piere;	Then push the probe gently into the penis until it reaches the stone;
et torne le foret a ta main en la piere poc et poc, tant que tu puisses percier la piere d’autre part;	Turn the probe with your hand within the stone gently, until you can pierce through it from one side to another;
si venra tantost li urine, puis presse ta main sus ceu qui est demorez de la piere qui est dedens la verge.	Urine will come out immediately, then press your hand on what remains of the stone inside the penis.
Si est tantost brisie, et saut fuer avec l’urine, et est garis li malaides;	If it breaks immediately, and comes out with urine, then the patient is cured;
et se tu ne pues ce faire por aucune chose qui le deffent, si lie I fil desoz la piere et I autre desus, puis fent la verge endroit la piere entre les II liiens, puis l’estrai fuer, et deslie lou liien, et mundifie lou sanc congeleit qui est en la plaie;	And if you cannot do this for any reason that prevents it, then tie a thread below the stone and another above it, then slit the penis at the level of the stone between both threads, then extract it forcefully, and untie the thread, and clean the frozen blood from the wound;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat them until they are healed.
de la piere des femmes	From a woman's stone.
Poc avient que piere soit enjanree en femmes, et s’il avient aucune fois, si est li cure grief, et est deffendut por III choses:	Soon it happens that stones form in women, and if it occurs sometimes, then the treatment is severe, and it is prohibited for three reasons:
l’une est que per aventure li femme est vierge;	One reason is that perhaps the woman is a virgin;
et li seconde est c’on ne puet trover femme bien saichant qui se descuevre as mires, meismement quant elle est caste.	The second reason is that one cannot find a woman who is knowledgeable enough to examine herself internally, especially when she is chaste.
Et li tierce maniere si est que par aventure on ne puet trover femme bien saichant en cest art de mains;	The third reason is that perhaps one cannot find a woman who is skilled enough in this surgical art.
et li quarte maniere si est que li piere de la femme si est plus em parfont que li piere de l’ome, por coi il i couvient faire plus parfonde taille, et grant paour i a. Et se necessitez semont a ceu, si covient que tu preignes une mieresse bien sachant, et a poines la trueve on, et se tu n’en trueves, point si quier I caste mire subtil;	And the fourth reason is that the stones of women are deeper than those of men, which requires a more profound incision, and there is great fear. If necessity arises for this, then you must take an experienced midwife, and at once find her if she exists nearby, and if not found, do not seek out a chaste subtle midwife;
et li presente une baile bien saige en la vie des femmes, ou une femme qui saiche une partie de l’art, et li comande qu’ele faice ceu que tu li comandes de l’inquisicion de la piere;	and present her with a wise midwife for female diseases, or a woman who knows part of the art, and instruct her to do what you command regarding the examination of stones;
et regarde mout bien se li femme est vierge:	and look very carefully if the woman is a virgin:
adonques li covient bouter son doit ou fondement et querir la piere;	then it is necessary to insert your finger into her anus and retrieve the stone;
et s’ele la trueve, si la constraigne desoz son doit, et li recomande qu’elle boute son doit ou con la malaide, et quiere et presse sa main senestre sus la vessie forment.	and if she finds it, make her push the stone out from under your finger, and instruct her to insert her finger into the patient's vagina, then reach and press firmly with her left hand on the bladder.
S’elle la trueve, si covient qu’elle la mueve de greit en greit des l’entree de la vessie jusque desoz, tant qu’elle viegne a la racine de la cuisse;	If she finds it, she must gently guide the stone from the bladder's entrance to under it, until it reaches the root of the thigh.
puis cope sus la piere en la racine de la cuisse encontre le mileu dou con, lai ou il est mues apparilliet, et sent la piere en celle partie;	Then strike upon the stone at the root of the thigh towards the middle of the anus where it is felt, and feel for the stone in that part.
et ne mueve son doi desus la piere ou desoz, et soit li taille au premier petite;	and do not move your finger above or below the stone, and let the incision be small at first.
puis boute lou rait en la taille, se tu sens la piere si acroi la plaie tant que li piere puisse issir fuer, et saiches que maintes manieres de pieres sont:	then insert the tube into the incision; if you feel the stone, enlarge the wound until the stone can be extracted, and know that there are many types of stones:
c’est a savoir, petites et grans et aspres et souez, longes et reondes, et qui ont rains.	to wit, small and large ones, rough and soft, long and round ones, and those that have veins.
si saiches les semblances por savoir l’issue.	If you know the symptoms, then you will understand the outcome.
Et se li sans te vaint, si met au leu vitriole broiet, et li tien une houre tant que li sans soit estainchiez;	And if you feel faint from the blood loss, quickly apply crushed vitriol to it, and hold it there for an hour until the bleeding stops.
puis revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer, et aies des estrumens que je t’ai dit en l’estraction de la piere as homes por toi aidier en ton oevre;	Then return to your work, until the stone is out, and have the tools I told you about for extracting stones from men so they can help with your work.
et se li sans te vaint, et c’est de l’artere qui est copee, si met la poudre sus le leu et l’estrain de tentes et de bendelz, et ne rencomencier plus ceu, et laisse la piere et ne la traire mie, que par aventure morroit li malaide;	And if you faint from blood loss, and it's an artery that is cut, put the powder on the wound along with tent and banneret extract, and do not start again on this one, leave the stone alone and don't touch it, for fear of causing death to the patient.
puis cure la plaie.	Then treat the wound.
Et quant li chalor dou sanc est apaisie, et li leus porrist, si revien a ton ovraige, tant que li piere soit fuer.	And when the heat of the blood is calmed down, and healing takes place, return to your work until the kidney stone comes out.
de hernie carnouse	Of hernia cruris.
Ramice aquouse n’est autre chose que assemblee de moistor ou blanc syfac, qui est desoz lou keur des coions, que contient l’uef;	Ramus aqueous is nothing other than the assembly of moisture or white of egg which lies below the heart of calves and contained within the egg.
et est apelez «syfac», et aucune fois est proprement en la toile de l’uef, si c’on cuide que ce soit I autre oef;	And is called "albumen", and at times it properly lies in the membrane of the egg, which makes one think that there are two eggs.
et c’est li cuir dou coion entre lou blanc syfac que nos avons dit;	and this is the skin of the scrotum between the white part we have mentioned.
et ceu n’avient se poc non.	but that does not happen if you apply poultices.
Et li generation de cest ramice si est de foibleteit que vient as coions, et est espandue celle matiere.	And the generation of this ramus is due to weakness that comes from cows, and this matter is spread.
Et aucune fois si vient de percussion sus les coions, et ceste moistor si a maintes colors:	And sometimes it comes from blows to the testicles, and this moisture has many colours:
ou c’est color declinans a jaunice, ou c’est sans rouge, ou noir, ou aquous blans, et ce avient plus;	where it is discoloured towards yellow, or it is red-less, or black, or white and watery, and this happens more often.
et ce sont li signe de conoistre ceste assemblee, car s’elle est ou blanc syfac que nos avons dit, si est li apostemes reons, I poc lonc si com li figure d’un oef, et n’apert mie li coions, car il a moistor tout entor.	and these are the signs to recognise this condition, for if it is on the white part we mentioned, then the abscess is round like an egg, and does not open up the testicles, because they are covered in moisture all around them.
Et s’il a moistor en la propre toile, si est li apostemes reons avec une partie de l’uef, et por ceu pense on que c’est uns autres oef;	And if it is wet within its own covering, the abscess forms with part of the egg (pus), and thus one thinks that this is another egg.
et se li moistor est entre le cuir des coions et le blanc syfac, si le sent om bien;	and if the moisture is between the skin of the buttocks and the white part (flesh), one senses it well.
donques quant tu vues savoir la color de la moistor, si esprueve a tout l’intromissoire quarreit, de coi li forme est ci devant.	therefore when you want to ascertain the colour of the moisture (pus), test it at every part within, from which its shape is described above.
Selonc ceu donques qui vient aprés l’intromissoire, juge de ceu qui est dedens.	According to what follows this test, judge by what is inside.
Et quant nos la curons par fer, si covient que li malaides soit sainiez selonc som pooir et la repletion de son cors;	And when we treat it with iron (surgery), one must ensure the patient is healthy enough according to their strength and the fullness of their body.
puis le sovine sus son dos, sus une chose un poc haute, et met desoz lui mout de drapelz;	place them on their back, on something slightly elevated, and put much cloth underneath.
puis sié sus sa senestre, et comande au ministre qu’il sié a destre, et estende la verge a l’un des II costelz dou keur des coions;	Then sit on his left side, and instruct the assistant to sit on the right side, then extend the rod to one of the two ribs below the heart of the testicles;
puis pren le spatumile leit, et cope le cuir des coions parmi leu dou lonc jusque delez lou poignil, et soit ta fendure toute droite en devisant le cuir des coions jusc’a syfac blanc, et l’escorche subtilment selonc tom pooir;	Then take the small spatula, and cut the skin of the testicles from their base to the wrist, making your incision straight as you separate the scrotal skin until you reach the white membrane, then carefully peel back the skin according to your ability.
puis perce lou syfac plain d’aigue a I large pertus, et estrai toute l’aigue, et puis met tes oncines, et estent lou syfac amont;	Then pierce the white membrane with a water-filled syringe through the wide opening, and extract all of the water, then put in your hooks, and stretch the membrane upwards.
et ne touchier le keur des coions, mais que le syfac soulement;	And do not puncture the heart of the testicles, only the white membrane.
cope tout ou par pieces meismement le costeit de lui subtil, que se tu ne le copes bien saigement, si revenra li aigue;	Cope it all or by pieces especially its delicate side, for if you do not cut it properly and wisely, the water will return.
et se l’uef saut fuer a ton oevre, si le ramoinne en son leu quant tu avras acomplit l’uevre dou syfac;	And if the egg should happen to be at your work, put it back in its place once you have completed the operation of the sieve.
puis assemble les II leivres dou keur des coions a une costure, puis le cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then join the two books of the heart of cows with a seam, then treat it like other wounds until they are healed.
Et se tu trueves l’uef corromput d’autre maladie, si covient que tu lies les vasselz que sont suspensoire, en doutant le decorrement de sanc;	And if you find the egg corrupted by another disease, then it is necessary to bind the suspending vessels, taking care of the discharge of blood.
puis cope le coion a tout le suspensoire, et estrai l’uef, et le cure si com nos avons dit.	Then cut the cow with all its suspending parts, and extract the egg, and treat it as we have said.
Et se aigue est assemblee en II parties ensamble, saiches que ce sont II ramices;	And if the bone is broken into two parts together, know that these are two pieces.
si cope l’autre partie si com tu as fait la premiere igalment, puis essue lou sanc, et met en la plaie lainne moillie en oile roset;	cut the other part just like you did with the first one evenly, then wipe off the blood, and place into the wound damp wool soaked in oil.
et met defuer autre laine moillie en vin et en oile, et met sus les II coions, et met desus drapelz doublés, et le lie sus a tout le liien qui est selonc ceste forme:	and place over it other wool dampened in wine and oil, and put this on both sides, then cover with doubled linen cloths, and bind everything above with a bandage like so.
Puis pren II drapelz, et les emple de laine charpie selonc ceste semblance et soient assemblez par cousture en la gorle des braies, et li uns des chiés preigne sus le fondement jusc’au dos, et li autres a la partie dou poignil;	Then take two linen cloths, and fill them with wool batting made to look like this and join them by sewing at the waist of the breeches, and one piece should be placed under the buttocks down to the back, and the other over the arm pit.
et li autre dui chief sus les II angres, et soit toute assemblee li restreinture en la boucle dou braier;	And the other two straps on top of the two angles, and let all the restraints be assembled in the buckle of the belt.
et aucune fois est medicinee ceste ramice de cautere en leu de taille de fer, et est que tu preignes I cautere cultellaire subtil, et cope le cuir des coions, et soit eschaufez si com nos avons dit, si que li syfac blanc que contient l’aigue est descovers;	And sometimes this caustic remedy is used instead of iron cutting tools, and you must take a fine lancet cautery, slice the skin of the testicles, and let it be heated as we have said, so that the white tissue containing liquid is exposed.
si pren lou cautere selonc ceste forme, et perce celui syfac as oncines, et l’escorche a cest subtil cautere chaut:	Then take the cautery according to this form, and pierce that white tissue with curved tools, flaying it with this hot fine cautery.
Et lou cope en toutes les manieres que tu pues, tant que tu esraiches tout;	And slice it in all ways you can, until everything is scraped out.
et garde que li feus ne touche l’uef;	Be careful that the fire does not touch the testicle.
et saiches que ceste oevre est plus salve;	And know that this work is safer;
et mues gardans de decorrement de sanc, et muedres que li ovraiges de taille;	and take care to avoid blood loss, and remember that surgical work is delicate;
et se nulle chose te fait contraire, ou aposteme chaus ou decorremens de sanc ou autre chose, si cure ce qui te fait contraire, selonc ceu qui est devant dit.	and if anything opposes you, or an abscess appears, or bleeding occurs, or any other issue arises, then treat what is causing the opposition as per what has been previously stated.
Et se li malaides est paourous, et ne vuet atendre cest ovraige por son horribleteit, si amenistre perforation, si com je te di, et est que quant tu es bien certains par les significations que nos avons dit que ramice aquouse est lai, si fai seoir le malaide sus I siege leveit;	And if the patient is afraid and does not want to undergo this work due to its terribleness, then proceed with cauterization as I have told you, and when you are certain through the signs we have mentioned that the water has drained away, make the patient sit on a raised seat.
pues perce l’aposteme an la partie desoz a tout le spatumile large, et met la perforation dou lonc dou cors;	then pierce the abscess below in the part of the flesh that is widest, and make the incision as long as the body.
et soit larges li pertus, si que toute li aigue corre fuer;	And let the holes be wide enough so that all the water may flow freely.
puis met coton sus le leu, et le lie, et laisse por corre le remenant de l’aigue, puis le cure tant que li plaie soit sanee;	Then place cotton on the spot, bind it up, and let the remaining water drain out. Afterwards, treat the wound until it is healed.
et se li blainche toile ne laisse issir l’aigue en la bouche de la plaie, si covient que tu i boutes une penne ou l’estrument dont on trait l’aigue des ydropiques, de coi li forme est ci devant;	And if the white cloth does not allow the water to escape through the mouth of the wound, you must insert a feather or an instrument like that used to draw off water from dropsical patients, which is shaped as described before.
et eslarge I poc la plaie, et saiches que li aigue revient, et est assemblee aprés VI mois ou enqui entor, et quant elle est assemblee si com devant, et ensi passera li malaides ses jors.	Widen the pouch of the wound and know that the water will return. It is assembled after six months or thereabouts, and when it is assembled as before, thus shall the patient pass his days.
de l’aposteme des coions	Of abscesses on buttocks.
Saiches que en la section de ceste ramice a paor em plusors dispositions, por coi il me semble que mues vaut c’on la laisse;	Know that when cutting this branch, there is fear in many situations, which is why I think it's better to leave it be;
et je vos dirai l’ovraige et les semblances de l’aposteme.	And I will tell you about the work and similarities of an abscess.
Je dis donques que maint aposteme vienent ou cors, et meismement as coions;	I say that many abscesses come from the body, especially at the buttocks;
et c’est par mout de cas.	And it happens frequently.
C’est a savoir par superfluiteit aigre et ague, qui est espandue as coions, ou de percussion;	This is caused by excess acidity and bile that has spread to the buttocks or due to impact.
et est li color de l’aposteme selonc la color dou cors;	And its colour matches the colour of the body.
et ne trueve point de dolor, et est aposteme grief;	It does not cause pain, but is instead a deep abscess.
et par aventure est uns apostemes griés paourous et pierous, et de fuxe color, et aucune fois vient de nout d’artere, ou d’enfleure de voine.	And perhaps there is a large abscess that is frightening, stony, and dark in colour; sometimes it comes from an artery or vein swelling.
Quant c’est par nout d’artere, si est conus par la disposition d’aposteme chaut, quant tu la presses a tes dois;	When it is from an artery, it is recognized by the warm abscess's condition when you press it with your fingers;
et ne covient mie que tu i touches.	And do not touch it.
Cil qui est fais d’enfleure de voine est conus par sa disposition a l’expression dou touchement des dois, et puet om bien faire la taille sus ceste semblance, et sus les autres chars;	One that comes from swelling of the vein is recognized by its condition on touch, and one can successfully cut it open in this manner as well as other cases.
et est que tu cope lou keur des coions, puis estent l’uef en haut, et le trai fuer dou blanc syfac, et delivre lou suspensoire de toutes pars de l’uef.	And one must remove the heart of the vein, then extend it upwards and cut away any white matter inside, freeing all parts of the egg from its contents.
Se li uef est ja sodez avec ces chars nees, si covient donques que tu traies l’uef, et lou cope;	If the egg is already hard with these newly born chicks, then you must therefore treat the egg, and remove its contents.
et s’il est aers au syfac, ou en ceu qui est dedens les vasselz, si covient que tu delivre toute celle tenve, et la cope reondement.	And if it is hollow in the shell or what is inside the vessels, you must deliver all that waste and roundly break the shell.
Et se li naissance de la char est ou leu derrier, si covient que tu la copes toute, et estrai l’uef, si com nous avons dit.	And if the birth of the flesh is behind, you must cut it all away, and extract the egg, as we have said.
Et quant tes ovraiges est acomplis, si emple la plaie de laine moillie en oile roset et en vin, puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	When your work is completed, fill the wound with wet wool soaked in rose oil and wine, then treat it with other cures until it is healed.
de l’aposteme des coions	Of abscesses on buttocks.
Cis est uns apostemes envoloupez d’un envoloupement semblant a I borjon, avec le mollifiement des coions, et se muet li malaides griement quant il vait;	This is an abscess wrapped in a membrane similar to that of the brain, with softening agents for the tendons, and the patient suffers greatly when moving.
et li cure de ceste maladie si est bien pres ausi paourouse com ceste ci devant, et toutevoie nos vos dirons l’ovraige de li, selonc ceu que li ancien firent.	And the treatment of this illness is equally as fearful as the one before, yet we will tell you its work according to what the ancients did.
Il covient que tu faices seoir lou malaide sus I siege aleveit, puis li boute le suspensoire des coions aval a tes dois, a tout le vasseil qui sont prochien a la verge, et les teigne li maistres, et les estende forment;	You must have the patient sit on an elevated seat, then place the tendon suspension below your two fingers, to all vessels near the wound, and hold them firmly, stretching them strongly.
puis cope au spatumile trenchant large dou traver endroit les vasselz, tant qu’il soient descovert, et puis escorche de chescune part, si com nos avons dit en l’estraction des arteres qui sont en temples;	Then cut across the vessels with a sharp spathumile knife, making it wide enough to uncover them, and then peel back the skin on either side, as we have said in the extraction of arteries that are in the temples.
puis i fiche une aguille ou il ait I fil double, et le lie au premier leu ou li vis est venue, et le lie derechief a l’autre chief;	Then insert a needle with a doubled thread into it, and tie it to the first place where the bone has come out, then tie it again to the other end.
puis les cope em mileu droitement, selonc la longesce dou cors, et en trai les moistors corrumpues;	Then cut them in half straight down the middle, according to the length of the body, and remove the corrupted moisture.
puis cure la plaie si com les autres ou on enjanre bowe, si que aucun vassel chiecent que norrissent l’un des coions;	Then treat the wound like others where sinew is involved, so that no vessel should bleed out one of the knobs.
car par ceu n’i vient point de mal, et se a toz les vasselz vient vis, si covient traire les coions a tout les vasselz;	For this does not cause harm, and if all the vessels become blocked, then it is necessary to drain the knobs for all the vessels.
si que li oes ne perde son norrissement por l’incision des vasselz, et sechent et ne se puient aidier.	So that the wound does not lose its direction due to the incision of the vessels, they dry up and cannot be helped.
de la routure dou syfac	Of the fracture of the cheekbone
Li avenemens de ceste ramice si est par la section que vient ou syfac, ou l’estension sus le ventre en la partie des angres, por coi li intestine dessendent de celle routure a l’un des coions;	The events of this mishap are due to the rupture that occurs or the tearing open, or the expansion in the abdominal area near the groin, which is why the intestines descend from that rupture towards one of the testicles.
et ceste routure est ou dou syfac, ou de l’estension de li, et vienent ces II manieres de mout de causes:	And this rupture is either from the tear or its extension, and these two types of injury happen for many reasons:
ou de percussion, ou de saut, ou de braire, ou de levement de grief faix, et par semblans choses;	Or from impact, or jumping, or lifting heavy loads, and through similar actions;
et li signes quant c’est de l’estension dou syfac, si est qu’il avient poc et poc, en lonc tens, et ne vient mie soudainnement;	And the signs when it's an expansion in the groin area are that there is a progressive onset over a long period and it does not come on suddenly.
et est li apostemes igalz jusque vers le parfont, por ceu que li syfac apresse l’intestine.	And abscesses are equal to the surface, for it accelerates the intestine's progress towards them.
