Et li signes est quant c’est de la section dou syfac, qu’elle fait venir a l’encomencement dolor soudaine, et est li apostemes divers apparans, desoz le cuir pres, et c’est por l’issue de l’intestine et le cors au defuer dou syfac.	And the signs are that when it is caused by a section of the cheekbone, it leads to sudden pain at first, and abscesses appear in various places under the skin close to the surface, which is due to the intestine protruding from behind the cheekbone.
Et aucune fois dessent li cirbes avec l’intestine, et est retenus enqui, et fait grant dolor soffrir au malaide, meismement quant il est pressez.	And sometimes the muscles descend with the intestine, getting stuck there and causing great pain to the patient, especially when pressed.
Et en ces cures de fer a paor, por coi il s’en covient eschuir.	And in these iron treatments with fear, it is necessary to escape from them.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que tu comande ou malaide qu’il ramoine l’intestine a sa main au dedens en la plaie, s’il i puet rentreir;	And the method of treatment is that you instruct the patient to gather their intestines in their hand and put them back into the wound if they can.
puis soit sovinez sus son col. entre tes mains, et lieve les cuixes;	Then support his neck with your hands, lift up his thighs between your hands.
puis estent le keur au desus, et cope tout le cuir des coions dou lonc;	Then extend the heart above it, and remove all of the skin from the lower part of the belly to the thighs.
puis boute dedens les leivres de la taille uncines selonc ceu que tu en as mestier por ovrir la plaie, et soit telz que li oes em puist issir;	Then push in the hooks of the pincers according to your need for opening the wound and arrange it so that the rectum can come out.
puis escorche lou syfac que est desoz lou cuir des coions, tant que li blans syfac dur soit descovers de toutes pars;	Then scrape off the white superficial skin that is beneath the leather of the calves until it is completely exposed on all sides.
puis boute ton doi indice en ceu qui enseut lou coion, en ceu qui est entre lou blanc syfac qui est desoz lou cuir de l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac, et depart ceu qui est derrier l’uef, et entre lou secont syfac;	Insert your index finger into what follows the calf, which is between the white superficial skin beneath the leather of the egg and the second layer of skin, taking care to avoid what comes after the egg and separating it from the second layer.
et pues muef a la main destre dedens lou keur des coions, et estent lou blanc syfac en haut a ta main senestre, et lieve l’uef a tout lou syfac devers la taille;	With your right hand, move within the heart of the calves and stretch the white superficial skin upwards with your left hand while lifting the egg to expose all sides of the second layer.
et comande au ministre qu’il estende l’uef en haut, et deslie ceu qui est aers derrier le liement;	Instruct your assistant to lift the egg upwards while releasing what is held back by the binding.
et quier a tes dois s’il a point de l’intestine envoloupeit ou blanc syfac dur, et se tu en trueves aucune chose, si le boute au ventre desoz;	and seek with your hands if there is an intestinal hernia or white hard cicatrix, and if you find anything, push it back into the abdomen below;
puis pren une aguille ou il ait I gros fil fait de X filz, et la boute en la derriere partie dou syfac, qui est aprés lou cuir des coions;	then take a needle with thick thread made of six strands, and push it through the back part of the cicatrix, which is behind the skin of the belly.
aprés la taille, puis cope les chiés qui apperent des filz, tant qu’il i ait IIII filz;	after sizing it, cut the ends of the threads that appear, until there are four strands left.
puis les assemble l’un sus l’autre en maniere de croix, et en lie lou syfac, dont nos avons dit qui est desoz lou cuir des coions, d’un fort liien de II pars;	then join them one over the other in the form of a cross, and tie the cicatrix, which we said was beneath the skin of the belly, with a strong two-part knot.
puis envoloupe les chiés des filz, et les lie forment de II pars, si que nuls des vasselz que les norrissent ne puissent entrer en ous, que aposteme chaus n’i viegne;	then wrap the ends of the threads and tie them in a double knot, so that none of the vessels that nourish it can enter there, lest an abscess form.
et met derechief le liien selonc le premier liien lonc II dois de celui, et aprés ces II liiens laisse dou syfac qui est desoz lou keur des coions le grant d’un doi;	and place the new rope according to the first long rope two lengths of that one, and after these two ropes leave a space below the heart of the animals as wide as a thumb.
et aprés tout l’autre selonc la rondesce que li euf porte;	and after all the others according to the roundness that the egg provides;
puis cope en la partie qui est desoz le cuir des coions, tant qui li sans corre, et li bowe, si com nos avons dit ci devant;	then cut in the part below the skin of the animals until blood and bowel flow as we have said before.
puis amenistre laine moillie en oile, et met em plaies, et i amenistre le liien que nos avons dit.	then bring damp wool in oil and put it on the wound, then bring the rope we have mentioned before.
Et aucune fois est cauterizez li blans syfac que nos avons dit, aprés l’incision, par doutance de decorrement de sanc.	And sometimes, the white surface is cauterized as we mentioned earlier, after incision, due to fear of blood loss.
Car ce avient maintes fois, et laisse le liien tant qu’il chiece per lui;	For this happens often, and leave the rope until it breaks by itself.
et s’il tarde au cheoir, si soit arosez d’aigue chaude, et met sus ceu que nos avons dit, tant qu’il chiece;	and if it takes time to fall off, irrigate with warm water, then put on what we have said before until it breaks.
puis cure la plaie d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	Then treat the wound with another treatment until it is perfectly healed.
de hernie carnouse	Of hernia cruris.
En ceste ramice ne vis je onques nul qui osast faire la cure par fer.	In this branch, I have never seen anyone dare to treat it with iron instruments.
Et li ancien dirent qu’ele est faite si com li ramice qui est ensamble la vis, en teil maniere que tu lie les vasselz, aprés la taille sus ous legierement au desoz;	And the ancients said that it is done like a vine branch which grows together with a willow tree, in such a way that you bind the vessels after cutting them slightly below.
puis cope em mi, et cure l’aposteme de ceu qui oevre, tant que li vasselz chient;	Then cut into me, and treat the abscess of those who work on it, until the vessels fall out.
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And treat it as we have said, until it is healed.
Aucune fois vient routure ens angres, si com nos avons dit, et apert li leus;	Sometimes rupture occurs in the neck, as we have said, and the wound opens up.
et ne dessent nulz des intestines as coions, et s’il en i dessent, c’est poc, et repaire toutes houres;	And none of the intestines fall into the cavity, but if they do, it is an emergency, and repair them every hour.
et toutevoie s’il demoure trop en cest point, si croit li plaie ou syphac, tant que li intestine dessent;	and yet if it stays too long at this point, the wound or fistula grows so that the intestines descend;
et ceu avient par l’estension dou syfac qui est as angres, si com nos avons dit, car il est estendus, puis est mollifiez et enflez li leus et apert;	and this happens due to the extension of the fistula which is in the anus, as we have said, for it is extended, then it softens and swells the joint and opens.
et li cure si est par cautere, si com nos avons devant dit;	and the treatment is by cauterization, as we have said before;
et aucune fois est curee par fer en ceste maniere:	and sometimes it is treated with iron in this manner:
et est que li malaides gise sovin sus son dos entre tes mains, puis cope le leu de la routure enfleit dou large selonc la quantiteit de III dois;	and the patient often lies on their back between your hands, then cut the place of the rupture swollen from side to side according to the size of three fingers;
et puis estrai le syfac qui est desoz le cuir que l’ensuet, puis pren lou rait et lou met sor le leu apparant dou syfac;	and then extract the fistula which is underneath the skin that covers it, then take a red-hot iron and place it on the exposed area of the fistula;
et lou presse au parfont dou ventre, puis cout les II leus apparans dou syfac sus lou chief dou rait, et cout l’un et l’autre;	et press it at the bottom of the belly, then cut the two visible places on the skin above the head of the vein, and cut one after another.
puis estrai le chief dou rait, et ne coper point dou syfac ne n’estendre l’uef n’autre chose, si com je t’ai fait savoir en la cure de la ramice des intestines;	then extract the head of the vein, and do not cut the skin nor stretch out the egg or any other thing, as I have made you aware in the treatment of intestinal rupture.
puis le cure par la cure des plaies.	then treat it with the treatment for wounds.
Et quant tu copes les filz, si le mundefie et cure la plaie, tant qu’elle soit sanee.	And when you cut the boys' hair, clean it up and treat the wound until it is healed.
Li syfac est constrains, et n’a point d’apparance en la routure, et li cauteres est muedres en cest leu, et plus prochiens a salut.	The knife is forced in without breaking the surface, and cauterization is better suited here for healing.
de l’amollissement dou cuir des coions	of softening the skin of the calves
Maintes fois est amollis li cuirs des coions en aucuns homes, por ceu que les chars que sont dedens sont mollifiees, et est lait a veoir;	The skin of the testicles often becomes softened in some men because the flesh within is softened, and it can be seen.
et est mestier, quant on le vuet curer, c’on faice gesir lou malaide sus son dos, et li cope le cuir qui est mollifiez sus le cuir natureil;	And it is necessary, when one wishes to treat it, that the patient be made to lie on their back, and cut the softened skin over the natural skin.
puis assemble les II levres a une costure, et se tu vues, cout premier la superfluiteit dou cuir mollifiiez a III costures ou IIII fermement;	Then assemble the two lips at one seam, and if you see it first soften the excess of leather with three seams or four firmly.
puis cope entre les costures, et lou cure si com les autres plaies, tant qu’il soit sanez, et chient li fil.	Then trim between the seams, and treat it like other wounds until it is healed, then remove the thread.
dou chastrement	Chastisement.
Saiches que chastremens est escomeniez en nostre loi, et por ceu il me plairoit que je n’en parlasse mie en cest livre;	Know that amputations are forbidden in our law, and so I would prefer not to speak of them in this book;
et n’est necessaires fuer que por II manieres:	and they are only necessary for two types [of injuries]:
dont l’une est que li mires en saiche respondre quant on li demandera, et en saiche la cure;	one is when the physician knows how to respond when asked, and he knows the treatment;
et li autre, por ceu que nos avons sovent mestier de chastrement d’aucunes bestes por nos aidier, si com de bouc et de mouton et de chait et d’autres bestes.	the other is because we often need to amputate certain animals to help us, such as goats and sheep and cats and other beasts.
Je dis donques que chastremens est fais selonc II manieres:	I say therefore that punishments are done according to two manners:
ou par atraction, ou par fendure.	or by attraction, or by incision.
En celle que nos faisons par attraction, faisons nos seoir la beste en aigue chaude, tant que li coion soient mollifiez et pendant;	In this manner that we do by attraction, we make the animal sit in warm water until the tendons are softened and relaxed;
puis les preing a ta main, tant qu’il soient remis et que tu ne les sentes plus.	then take them with your hand until they are reset and you no longer feel them.
Du chastrement de taille:	Of the punishment of castration:
covient que tu teignes la beste, et li presse le cuir des coions a ta main senestre, puis lie le suspensoire, et cope sus chescun oef a I cop, quant tu les avras bien escorchiez;	You should hold the animal and press on the skin of the tendons with your left hand, then tie the suspensory ligament, and cut each testicle with one stroke once you have properly skinned them;
et i laisse aucun poc dou syfac et lou subtil syfac qui est sor les vasselz;	and leave a small wound and subtle ointment that is on the vessels.
et ceste maniere de chastrement est muedre que cele qui est faite par attraction, por ceu que a l’atraction demoure par aventure aucune chose des coions, par coi li beste desire luxure;	and this method of castration is better than that which is done by traction because in traction some part of the testicles may remain, causing the animal to still have lust.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’ele soit sanee.	then treat the wound until it is healed.
des hermofrodites	Ce sont des animaux qui ont les deux coions et les deux oefs, ou qui portent de chescuns une partie; et par le droit de nature est que li males n'aient pas les vases de la femele en eu cors, ne les females les vases de li males.
Hermofrodie est selonc II manieres as homes:	Hermaphrodite occurs in two ways among humans:
l’une si est que entre les II coions apert ausi com li figure de la nature d’une femme, ou il ait poil, et aucunes fois en cort li urine.	one is that between the two testicles there appears a natural structure like that of a woman's, with hair, and sometimes it secretes urine.
Et li autre maniere si est en femmes, et ait sus lou poignil ausi com une verge et II coions.	And another type occurs in women, situated on the forearm like a rod and two knobs.
Et li cure de l’ome et de la fame si est que tu copes les chars ajostees toutes, et les cure si com autres plaies;	And the treatment for men and women is that you separate all joined parts, and treat them like other wounds.
en la seconde maniere, des homes dont li urine saut par lou cuir des coions, si n’a point de cure.	In the second manner, for men whose urine spurts through their scrotum, there is no treatment.
de la tentigene	Of the swelling.
Tentigene est une chars ajostee sus la partie natureil, tant qu’elle est trop laide a veoir;	A tumor is flesh attached to the natural body part, making it too ugly to look at.
et aucunes femmes l’ont ausi grant com une main, et c’est li cure.	And some women have them as large as a hand; this is the treatment.
Il covient que tu teignes la superfluiteit de la tentigene a ta main ou as oncines, et la cope legierement;	You must hold the excess of the tumor in your hand or with pincers, and cut it lightly.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne, puis le cure d’autre cure tant qu’il soit sanez;	And do not go too deep, lest the blood flow out, then treat other treatments until it is healed.
et a une autre char que naist a la bouche de la marris, et l’emple, et par aventure saut fuer, et est selonc la semblance d’une kowe, et por ceu l’apelerent li ancien «maladie kowee».	And for another flesh that arises at the mouth of the anus, and swells up, and perhaps bursts open, and it looks like a cow's udder, thus the ancients called it "cow disease".
Si covient que tu la copes, si com nos avons dit la tentigene, et la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee.	You must cut it off, as we have said for a growth caused by itching, and treat it until it is clean.
de erratique	Of wandering.
Erratique si est quant li nature de la femme n’est mie percie, ou li pertus est petis;	Erratic it is when the woman's nature is not pierced, or the opening is small;
et est naturez par naissance, ou accidens par maladie que venue i est;	and it is natural by birth, or an accident caused by illness that has arisen there;
ou c’est par char ajostee, ou dou syfac subtil ou espés, et est fais em parfont en la marris, ou en costez, ou desoz, ou que soit;	whether it is through a wound inflicted by sharp or subtle instrument, and it is done perfectly in the center, on the side, below, or wherever it may be;
et deffent le concevoir, et l’enfantement, et par aventure les flors a avoir;	and they prevent conception, childbirth, and perhaps even the flowers to bear;
et li connoissance de ceu si est par le regart de la baile.	and one's knowledge of such is through observation of the womb.
Se li estoupemens est prochiens apparans, si quier a tes dois ou au rait.	If the obstructions appear nearby, then they will reach your fingers or rod [instrument].
S’il est dou syfac subtil, et il est prochiens as II leivres, si te haste, et la ront ensi:	If it is an instrument that is subtle, and it is close to the two cubits, then hasten and round it thus:
met tes II dois indices ensamble, et li femme soit sus son dos, espandues ses jambes;	Put your two index fingers together, and have the woman lie on her back with her legs spread.
puis estent les II leivres forment, tant que li subtilz syfac soit rons, et soit overs li estoupemens;	Then stretch the two lips wide apart until the soft tissue is exposed and over the gums.
puis pren laine, et la moille en oile, et la met sus le leu, et gise li femme a home chescun jor, si qu’il ne puist souder.	Then take wool, soak it in oil, and place it on the spot, having the woman lie at home each day so that it cannot heal.
Et se li syfac est dur et espés, si covient que tu lou copes au spatumile semblant a foille de mirte.	And if the tissue is hard and thick, you must cut it with a spatula similar to myrtle leaves.
Se li estoupemens est de char nee, si la sospent a l’oncine et la cope;	If the gums are of new flesh, suspend them with thread and cover it.
et aies les medicines estainchans sanc, si com acaice, sanc de dragon, encens, ensamble abun d’uef;	And have on hand hemostatic medicines in case of bleeding, such as dragons' blood, incense, mixed with egg white.
puis amenistre une caine de plonc large, si que li plaie ne puisse souder;	Then apply a wide copper rod so that the wound cannot heal.
et ensi soit longement, et li amenistre une tente de lin sec;	And thus let it remain for a long time, and bring him a dry linen tent.
puis soit curez d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then be cured with other treatments until you are healed.
Et quant en la marris vient char nee, si la covient coper selonc ceste maniere, se ce n’est apostemes enchancrez.	And when a new flesh grows in the wound, it should be cut according to this method, unless there are embedded abscesses.
Car a l’aposteme enchancreit qui est en la marris, ne doit on touchier de feir.	For an embedded abscess in the wound, one must not attempt to cut it open.
des emorroides	Of haemorrhoids
Emorroydes sont overtures de voines dont sans cort acostumeement, et quant les emorroydes sont vielles si devienent thelul;	Hemorrhoids are openings of veins that usually bleed, and when hemorrhoids are old they become tumors.
et nos avons jai dit en la division les semblances d’aus, et les signes, et je dirai ci celles qui resoivent curation.	And I have previously mentioned in the classification their similarities and signs; here I will describe those that can be cured.
Je di que les emorroides et li thelul, quant il sont em parfont en la marris, et il n’aperent au sentir, si n’est mie li cure par fer.	I say that haemorrhoids and thick growths, when they are completely inside the anus, and cannot be felt, should not be treated with a cauterising iron.
Cil qui sont a la bouche de la marris, c’on puet sentir, sont cil c’on puet curer.	Those who are at the mouth of the swamp, where one can feel, are those whom one can cure.
Il covient donques que tu mettes la femme en une maison froide, puis estent l’altelul as tenailles, et le cope en ses racines, puis poudre sus medicines restraignans sanc, si com acaice et sanc de dragon et encens, et semblans choses;	You must therefore put the woman in a cold house, then extend the tumor with tongs and cut it at its root, then apply powder made of blood-coagulating medicine such as dragon's blood and frankincense, along with similar substances.
puis boute ses piez a la paroit une houre, puis la met en aigue froide;	Then press her feet against the wall for an hour, then place them in cold water.
et se decorremens de sanc i vient, si la fai seoir en une decoction de sumac et d’escorce de pomes grenates et de gales et de semblans choses, et puis pren farine d’orge, et la confis avec miel et aisil, et en fai I emplaustre sus son dos.	And if there is discharge of blood, have her sit in a decoction of sumac and pomegranate peel with galls and similar things, then take barley flour, mix it with honey and egg white, and make an ointment to apply on her back.
Et se il estainche, c’est boin.	And if it stops, that is good.
Se ceu non, se li fai aerdre ventouses au dos et as mameles sens ferir;	If not, have her air out cupping glasses on her back and breasts without causing injury.
puis pren lainne, et la moille en jus de plantain ou en jus d’aglentier avec vin viel, et fai aerdre au leu.	Then take linen, dampen it in juice of plantain or hawthorn with old wine, and apply to the affected area.
Et quant li aposteme repose, si cure lou leu d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when the abscess heals, treat the site of injury until it is completely healed.
et celle qui est apelee «albathir» est rouge, et est semblans a I chief aspre, si le covient coper si com j’ai dit le thelul;	and that which is called "albathir" is red, and resembles an acrid head, it must be cut like the thelul as I said.
et puis lou cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and then treat until it is healed.
des apostemes de la marris	Abscesses of the marrow.
Maintes manieres d’aposteme vienent en la marris, si com chancre et aposteme pierous et herpes et estiomenes et fistules et emorroides et aposteme chaut, et plusors autres maladies que j’ai dit en la division.	There are many types of abscess that can occur in the marrow, such as cancer, stone abscess, herpes, tumors, fistulas, hemorrhoids, hot abscess, and several other diseases that I have mentioned in the classification.
Il covient donques que je die en cest traitier l’aposteme chaut qui vient en la marris, qui n’est mie des apostemes que coillent bowe;	I should therefore say in this treatise about the hot abscess that comes on the nose, which is not one of the abscesses that require bowels;
et se tu vues savoir l’ovraige de fer, si regarde se li apostemes est agus en l’encomencement de sa venue, et plain de chalor et de fievre, et s’il devient rouge se tu le pues veoir.	and if you want to know about the work of iron, look at whether the abscess is acute when it first appears, and full of heat and fever, and whether it turns red as you can see it.
Adonques ne te haster mie de percier, mais lou fais meurer tant que li dolor soit apaisie;	Then do not hasten to pierce it, but let it die until the pain is eased;
et puis fai seoir lou malaide sus I siege, et ait II petis sieges ou il se cline, et apoie sus son dos et assemble ses piez as parties defuer la jambe;	and then have the patient sit on a seat, and place two small stools for them to lean back against, supporting their back and bringing their feet together below the leg;
et soient ses cuixes espandues, et mette ses braz desoz ses genous, et les lie bien d’un boin liien;	let their thighs be extended, and place their arms underneath their knees, binding them well with a good bandage;
puis succe li baille devers lou destre costeit, et i amenistre l’estrument dont on oevre la bouche de la marris, de coi ci aprés vient li forme;	then turn them onto their right side, and bring the instrument for opening the marrow to it, of which afterwards comes the form;
et covient que quant tu i vues amenistrer cest estrument, que tu fiches le rait premier ens por savoir la parfondeté de la marris, si que ceu qui entre ens de l’estrument n’i viegne plus em parfont qu’il ne doit, et qu’il ne blece la malaide;	and it is necessary that when you bring this instrument to bear, you first insert a rod to gauge the depth of the marrow, so that what enters the patient from the instrument does not go too deep and harm them;
et se li estrumens est plus grans, si covient covrir la parfondesce de la marris de drapelz, si que li estrumens ne li grieve;	and if the instrument is larger, it should be covered with layers of cloth to protect [the wound] from its harm.
et covient qu’il mette le cornet de l’estrument au desus, et qu’il teigne l’estrument.	he must place the end of the instrument on top and hold the instrument steady.
Et quant li apostemes apert, et on lou fent a la main mol, si le covient coper au chief, au spatumile leit;	and when the abscess opens, it must be lanced with a soft hand, either with the lancet or the spatula.
et quant li bowe est vuidie, si covient que tu mettes en la plaie tentes moillies en oile roset, ou en oile vert sec;	and when the boil is empty, you must place in the wound moistened bandages soaked in rose oil or dry green oil.
et met la tente fuer de la plaie au parfont de la marris, et met par defuer sus la marris et sus le poignil lainne nette moillie en aigue ou malves soient cuites;	place the bandage outside of the wound over the depth of the abscess, and on top of the abscess and around the wrist place clean moist woolen cloth soaked in water or steeped in mallows.
puis le cure aprés II jors d’oignement avenant a ceu, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Then the cure after two days of treatment coming to this, until it is healed;
et aucune fois leve on la marris et la plaie par clistere d’aigue et de miel, et puis d’aigue ou racines de lis et aristologe longe soient cuites;	and sometimes we lift the swelling and wound with a cleansing enema of water and honey, and then with water or cooked roots of iris and long aristoloche;
puis reveigne a l’oignement.	then return to the treatment.
Et se li plaie est reponue en la marris, si covient que tu te gardes de cuire de fer, mais cure la si com nos avons dit en la division.	And if the wound is swollen with pus, you must avoid treating it with hot iron; instead, treat it as we have described in the section on [wound treatment].
de l’enfantement	Of childbirth.
Mestier est premier a la baile qu’elle conoisse la figure de l’enfantement natureil, et li signes si est quant tu vois la femme apresser aval, et desire odorer l’ar:	It is necessary for the midwife to know the natural process of childbirth and its signs; when you see the woman hastening downwards, and wishing to smell it.
adonques se haste li enfes de fuer issir;	then the child is eager to come out.
adonc saiches que cil enfantemens est selonc la figure natureil, et est li issue soz son chief, et li secondine avec lui;	thus you know that these births follow the natural pattern, and the child comes out headfirst, and the midwife assists him.
et quant tu vois ces signes, si covient presser legierement son ventre, si que li enfes isse tost;	and when you see these signs, gently apply pressure to their abdomen so that the child comes out soon.
car quant il dessent sus son chief, si ist li secondine avec lui, et est mondee li marris de ses superfluitez par bone mundification;	because when they descend onto the head, the midwife should assist them, and the husband should be prepared for any excesses through proper care.
et cist qui vient autrement ne vient mie naturelment.	and one who comes otherwise does not come naturally.
Car il vient aucune fois sus ses piez, et vient fuer li cors ou li chiés, et les mains, ou il vient sus son ventre, ou sovin, et est convertis par aventure sor son col, et par autres figures malvaises;	For sometimes it comes out onto the feet, and emerges either from the body or the head, and the hands, or it comes out of the abdomen, often turned accidentally towards the neck, and in other bad positions.
si est mestier a la baile qu’elle soit saige et subtilz en ces choses, et se warse d’error et de decevement, et je vos mostrerai toutes les figures coment on li doit aidier.	So it is necessary for the midwife to be wise and skilled in these matters, and avoid error and deception, and I will show you all the positions and how she must assist.
Se li enfes vient sus son chief par issue natureil, et li femme enfante griement, et li vertus de li est foible, si la fai seoir sus une selle, ou les femmes la tienent;	If the child is born on its head by natural means, and the woman gives birth with great difficulty, and her strength is weak, then have her sit on a saddle or be held by other women.
et arose sa nature d’oile ou fenugreic soit cuit, et puis boute li baile entre ses dois le petit spatumile dont ci est li forme:	And prepare her some oil of almonds or fenugreek that is cooked, then put between her fingers the small spatula which has this form:
et fende la secondine, et cope a son ungle tant que li moistors qui est ens corre fuers;	And split open the perineum, and scrape away at her fingernail until the moisture that collects there flows out.
et preint lou ventre de la femme tant que li enfes dessende, et s’il ne dessent, si covient clisterizer la femme de muscillaige de fenugrec avec oile de sisament;	And press the woman's belly until the child descends, and if it does not descend, then you must administer an enema of fenugreek mixed with sesame oil to the woman.
puis la fai preindre et esternuer de condisi, et tien sa bouche et son neis une houre:	Then make her inhale snuffs of ground cumin, and hold your hand over her mouth and nose for an hour.
si istra maintenant l’enfes.	Draw out the child now.
Et se les II mains issent fuer, si covient que tu les ramoinne legierement poc et poc;	And if both hands stick out [are dislocated], you must reset them gently back and forth.
et s’elles n’i puent entrer, si met la femme sus I siege, et li lieve les piés en haut;	and if they cannot be put back in [their socket], place the woman on a chair, and lift her feet up high.
puis deboute le siege sus terre, et teigne on la femme, qu’elle ne chiece au deboutement;	then raise the chair from the ground, holding the woman so she does not fall when it is lifted;
et se li mains n’i puet entrer, et li enfes muert, si li cope les mains au couteil qui est ci devant mis, et estrai l’enfant, et ramoine igalment.	and if the hands cannot be put back in [the socket], and the child is dead, then cut off the hands with a knife as described before, extract the child, and reset evenly.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses piés	of the birth of the child on its feet
Quant li enfes vient sus ses piez, si lou covient bouter en haut;	When the child stands up on their feet, you must push them upwards.
et puis le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit igalz;	and then turn it over and over until it is even;
puis preigne I des piez et l’estende poc et poc.	then take one leg and stretch it little by little.
Cant il saut jusc’as cuixes, si la comande a preindre, et la fai esternuer de condisi;	If it reaches the thighs, instruct him to jump up until he sneezes violently.
si saut fuer, se Deus vuet.	if jumping occurs, may God want it so.
Et s’il n’ist fuer si com nos avons dit, si le torne poc et poc, tant qu’il soit selonc la figure natureil.	And if it is not fever as we have said, then turn him on his side and side again until he is in his natural position.
Car adonques ist il legierement.	For then he will be lightly dislocated.
Et s’il ne vient fuer si com nos avons, dit si pren muscillaige de altee, et oile de sisament, et gomme fondue, et broie tout en I mortier;	And if it does not work as we have done before, then take some mullein from the roof, and oil of cassia, and molten gum, and grind everything in a mortar.
et met sus la nature de la femme dedens et defuer cest oignement, puis la fai seoir en aigue tede jusque desoz les costelz;	and put this ointment on the skin of the woman's body both inside and outside, then make her sit in warm water up to below the ribs.
et quant elle est moillifie desoz, se li fai I coliere de mirre, et li met desoz, et li laisse une houre;	and when it is moistened underneath, make him a collar of myrrh for it, and place it beneath, and leave it there for an hour.
puis la fai seoir sus I siege, puis la fai esternuer et estraint sa bouche et son neis, et li preint le ventre legierement, car li enfes saut maintenant.	then have her sit on a chair, then make her sneeze and hold her mouth and nose, and take her gently by the stomach, for now the child jumps.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus ses genous	From the birth of the child upon their knees.
Quant li enfes vient en ceste forme, si i mette li baile ses mains poc et poc;	When the child comes in this manner, have the midwife put her hands to it thus and thus.
puis soit sovinee sus son col, et li pendent li piez aval, et soit gisans sor I lit;	then let someone support her under the neck, and have her feet hanging down, and let her lie on the bed.
et plie ses mains poc et poc, et puis li preint les mains sus lou ventre, et li oste les cussins desoz, tant qu’elle soit appareillie aval;	and bend her hands like this and thus, then press her hands on the belly, and remove the pillows from beneath, until she is properly arranged below.
et se li enfes ne saut, si pren ses piez et li muef forment, puis li muef lou ventre amont, puis i boute tes mains;	And if the child does not jump, take his feet and move them vigorously, then massage his belly upward, finally place your hands on him.
et ewe l’enfant poc et poc;	And hit the child repeatedly.
et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse.	Instruct the woman to take hold of herself until the child comes out.
de l’issue de l’enfant qui vient dou large une main pendant	From the birth of the child, which comes from the wide part with one hand hanging.
I covient engignier a ramener la main:	I must devise a means of bringing back the hand.
s’on ne la puet ramener, si fai lever la femme, et aler;	If you cannot bring it back, have the woman get up and move around.
s’elle ne puet aler, si la fai gesir sus I lit, et li deboute les jambes forment;	If she cannot walk, make her lie down on the bed, and vigorously raise her legs.
puis amenistre lou muscillaige que j’ai conteit;	Then bring the massage oil I have described.
et s’elle n’enfante, si la fai seoir sus I siege, puis estudie au rameneir la main;	And if she does not give birth, make her sit on a seat, then help to return the hand.
et ewe l’enfant selonc la figure natureil, et la fai esternuer, et li comande qu’elle se preigne tant que li enfes isse fuer.	Then deliver the child according to its natural position, make her sneeze, and instruct her to hold herself until the baby is out.
de l’issue de l’enfant sus son col, et ait espandues ses mains, et sa faice tornee devers lou dos sa mere	From the exit of the child onto its neck, and has spread out his hands, and his face turned towards the back of his mother.
I covient que li baile teigne sa main, puis le torne poc et poc, et l’ewe legierement;	It's necessary for the midwife to hold her hand, then turn it gently back and forth, and deliver lightly.
et quant il est igalz, si met sus la nature muscillaige de altee et oile, si com nos avons dit, puis li comande qu’elle se mueve poc et poc;	And when it is equalized, put on the natural dressing of alum and oil as we said before, then instruct her to move gently back and forth.
et quant tu avras ce fait, si la fai seoir sus I siege, et li comande k’elle se preigne;	And when you have done this, make her sit on the seat again, and instruct her to hold herself.
et la fai esternuer.	And make them sneeze.
de ceste meisme maniere a tout la secondine	in the same way for every midwife
Quant il vient fuer en ceste maniere a tout la secondine, si cope la secondine a ton ungle, tant que li moistors soit vuidie;	When it comes up in this way at every heartbeat, cut the flesh between your fingers with your nail, so that the moisture is drained.
et se li enfes pent sus sa faice et sus son col, si la cope des la boude, qu’elle ne soit retenue, et muere li enfes;	and if the child has it on their face and neck, cut off the skin from their forehead so that it is not restrained, then kill the child.
puis boute l’enfant dedens, tant que tu l’aies mis si com il covient, et comande a la femme qu’elle se preigne aucune fois:	then push the child inside so that you place it correctly, as it should be, and instruct the woman not to move.
adonques si istra legierement.	so gently lift them out.
de l’issue des gemelz	Of the dislocation of the wrists
Saiches que gemeil naissent maintes fois, et aucune fois en naissent III ou IIII;	Know that twins are born many times, and sometimes even three or four are born together;
et ceu n’est mie estrainge chose, et poc avient.	And this is not a strange thing, but it happens often.
Dui sont estrainge chose, et ne vivent mie, se poc nom;	They have two strange things that do not allow them to live if they happen at the same time.
je sai ceu, qu’il soient multipliiet, et sont desevrez par lou syfac qui les devise, qui est liiez a la boude;	I know that they multiply and are divided by the knife that separates them, which is related to anger.
et aucune fois issent ausi naturelment com uns tous sous, si com nos avons dit.	And sometimes they occur naturally like any other thing under the sun, as we have said before.
Et s’il issent griement, si la cure si com nos avons dit, et soit li baile subtilz, et faice tost et legierement ceu qu’elle fait;	And if they occur severely, then treat it as we have said before, and let the surgeon be skilled, and act quickly and lightly.
et faice ensi com il vaut mues a salut.	And do so for his best chance of survival.
de plusors enfans	Of many children
Aucune fois sont formez en la marris I ou II ou III ou IIII ou V ou VI ou VII, ou plusors jusc’a XV, et sont tout formeit en forme d’enfant par le mesurement dou saige glorious, et couvient que li baile saiche tout ceu, car par aventure semblans chose li avient;	Some are formed in the womb at I or II or III or IV or V or VI or VII months of age, and they may form fully as a child by the measurement of their glorious wisdom, and it is fitting that the nurse knows all this, for perhaps similar things will happen to them.
si faice selonc ceu qu’il covient.	Do as you ought.
de l’enfant mort	Of the dead child.
Quant tu cures la femme de l’enfant mort ou ventre, si com j’ai dit en la division, et il ne vient fuers, et tu es constrains d’ovraige de mains;	When you treat the woman for a dead child in her belly, as I've said in the section on obstetrics, and it doesn't turn out well, and you are forced to use manual instruments.
si covient que tu saiches se li femme est de saine vertut, et n’ait accident ou elle ait paor de mort;	It is necessary that you know if the woman has no moral vices, and does not suffer any accidents or fear of death;
si covient que li femme soit sovinee sus son dos, et soit ses chiés enclins aval, et les jambes levees;	The woman should be positioned on her back with her head inclined downward, and her legs raised;
et li ministre la teigne de II pars, ou elle soit liie au lit si qu’elle ne soit traite au dessendement de l’enfant;	And the minister gives her two portions, or she is tied to the bed so that she cannot be treated for the child's descent.
puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	Then rub the wife's mouth with moist oils along with a mixture of althea, fenugreek, and flaxseed, then anoint her palms with these oils and mixtures.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere I leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu, et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	Then gently push her to one side, then move her to a place where she pushes the feet so that they are accessible for this, and take care if the child is equipped that it descends onto its head.
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez, et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	If the feet are stuck in its eyes or neck or mouth or palate or below the chin or in the throat or near the ribs, and if the descent is on its feet, then either prick it or pinch it in the softer parts.
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and he must hold the hook with his right hand, and place the curve between his two fingers of the left hand, and push all his hand lightly, and fix the hook in one of these places that we have said until it reaches the empty space.
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	and this is the form of the hook:
puis fiche encontre I autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	then fix another hook opposite it, or the third if you need them, so that the extractions are equal.
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then extend them equally by moving from one side to the other, to extract it, and let the hooks be serrated to hold it, just as this is the form:
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if any part remains, then anoint the wound with some of his fingers' oil and push those into that part, and pull out the other part.
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	And if any remains there, place this splint or higher, and do so until it comes out entirely forward.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement, si covient que tu envoloupes sus I drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	And if one hand comes forward of the other, and he cannot reset it due to tightness, then you must wrap it with a cloth until it fully extends.
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as II piés.	Then bind it at the wrist where the palm meets the heel or with a cord, and so you must do for the other hand and both feet.
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee, si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	And if the child's head is large and it is stuck during delivery, or there is an acute presentation of the head, then you must insert your spatulate finger between your two fingers, split open the head, and extract the presenting part.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	Where you grind it with the instrument called "almidach," from which its shape is formed, using the instruments or chapters that follow this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	And do likewise if the child has an unusually large head naturally;
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles, et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	Then pull out the bones with pliers, and if the head pops out and is caught by forceps, let it be split open until the moisture that accumulates there flows out.
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	And if it cannot come out, cut it up into pieces as much as you can manage.
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	And if it is swollen in the belly or below the ribs, you must pierce it until the moisture flows out.
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	And if the child is standing on its feet, then there is slight traction, and the guidance to the mouth of the womb is light.
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a I drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	And if it is tight in the belly or breast, you must extract it with cloth wrapped around the hand;
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	and open the abdomen or chest, let the moisture which is there flow out;
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure, si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	and if the other limb is removed but the head remains, push your hand deep into the socket and pull it down to the mouth of the socket;
puis i boute I oncine ou II, et le trai fuer;	then insert one or two fingers and draw it out forcefully;
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier, ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	and if the mouth of the socket is narrowed due to hot abscesses that have formed there, you should not try to force it open, but rather apply moist and greasy substances;
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	and apply plasters to him, and wrap them with moist, softening, and soothing cloths.
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	And if the child is lying on their side, and you can make them lie flat, then apply what we have said for a live child;
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	if there is no other option, then pull it apart piece by piece, leaving nothing of the afterbirth behind.
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	And once you have done this, apply what we have said for hot abscesses that appear in the buttocks;
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	and if bleeding occurs, apply cold compresses to restrain it, and provide further treatment.
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut I autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	And I saw a woman in whose belly a child had been dead then another was born on top of it, and the other died too.
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	After a long time, an abscess came on her neck, and swelled so much that it opened up, and began to emit a foul smell.
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	I was called to treat him, and I thought long, but could not heal the wound.
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	I applied a strong attracting plaster, and an bone came out, followed by others after several days.
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	I was greatly surprised, for the belly has no bones.
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	I thought it might be the bones of a dead child.
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em millor point;	I treated the wound, extracting visible bones, until the woman was in a better condition;
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	And the woman lived a long time like this, and there was still a little piece of bowels in its place.
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	And I have recorded this chapter only for those who, when the masters find an odd thing, know how to offer assistance.
dou ramener la marris a son leu	To bring the marrow back to its place.
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres;	Hereafter comes the form of the compress, for which you have the books;
et a II tornans as II chiés des II liiens.	And turn to II for II shoulders.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Nevertheless, the horns should be more slender than the restrainer, and they should be made of ebony or boxwood.
et soit li bouche dou fust I doi de large, et li marge des arbres I doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	And the mouth of the trunk should be two fingers wide, and the edge of the wood one finger, and in length a palm and a half.
et enmi les II liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	and between these two joints are two attachments of this same piece of wood, which are fixed to each other and about half a palm or slightly more in length.
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les II cornes.	and these two attachments are inserted into the mouth of the socket to open it when you turn both horns.
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	Another form, more refined and lighter in its resemblance to this one, can be made from ebony or boxwood, like the shape of pliers.
et ait as II chiés II ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et II dois de large;	and it has two attachments at each end, you see, one palm in length, with two sides of equal width.
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor I lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes, puis boute les II ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	and when you see that the socket needs to be opened with all of these instruments, have the woman sit on a bed, with her feet hanging down and her legs open wide. Then insert both attachments into the socket, keeping the head of the instrument below between her thighs.
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	Then work your hand with all the instrument, just as you did with equal pliers, according to the amount you want to open the mouth of the wound, so that it yields what it wants.
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances;	These instruments are all well-equipped, and their appearances are diverse;
et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	And when you see them prepared, the work is more urgent, and it is of greater benefit to men for their well-being.
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	If you do not despair of the instrument at your disposal, as their need is inexcusable.
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	When the afterbirth is retained during childbirth, you must instruct the patient to hold her breath and then make her sneeze forcefully, while holding your hands over her mouth and nose;
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	And if she can do this, it is beneficial.
Se ceu non, si prent I pot, et fai I pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	If not, take a pot and make a hole in the lid, then add herbs that can open the pores of the skin such as sage, rue, anise, chamomile, cassia bark, and marjoram.
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu;	All these herbs or some of them must be boiled in water inside the pot on the fire.
puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris, et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris;	Then put a funnel or opening from the pot into one nostril of the patient's nose and hold it so that the vapours enter inside.
puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	Then make them sneeze as we have said before.
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	If the secondary injury occurs.
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature, et quiere la secondine;	If it remains after this treatment and does not work, tell the nurse to wet her left hand in sesame oil or mule fat ointment then rub it inside. Finally look for a midwife.
et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	and when she has found it, take hold of it and stretch it little by little straightaway, so that the patient is not troubled during extraction;
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie;	but you must move it gently right and left, and then pull.
si venra et se desaerdra.	then it will come out and become dislodged.
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	And if the patient's mouth is narrow, we have mentioned the treatment of coughing and herbal fumigation;
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	and if none of what we have said works, take care not to be reckless when pulling.
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	but you must tie what is at the patient's mouth to the woman's thigh, then give her an enema of tetrapharmakon.
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer;	If it festers and returns, it will come again.
mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	However, when it festers and causes foul odour in the stomach and head, it injures the patient.
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu:	Therefore, one must apply suitable fumigations accordingly:
aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	None of the ancients have tried fumigation with watercress and dried figs.
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	The form of the instrument with which one fumigates the woman to stop her flowering and menses is as follows:
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	It is like seeing the reflection of a dog, with a subtle head in nature, and wide eyes over the fire.
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	And let the fumigation be over the coals, and the moth until it is wasted, then begin another.
de percier lou fondement	to perforate the fundament
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	Many children are born without their anus being pierced, but instead it is blocked by some subtle membrane.
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	Therefore, it is necessary for the surgeon to pierce this membrane with his finger, and not with a sharp spatula, taking care that the incision does not touch any other part.
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then apply soft wool moistened in wine and oil, and treat it until it is healed.
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	And if you doubt that it will not heal, insert a piece of lead wire into the hole, and leave it there for several days; remove it when the child wishes to go outdoors.
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme;	And sometimes this blockage occurs suddenly in a wound or abscess.
si covient coper celui soudement:	It is necessary to cut open this sudden blockage.
si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	Thus it should be treated, as we have said about the anus of a pig.
de la fistule dou fondement	From an anal fistula.
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;	Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des II parties, si a une fistule ou plusors;
et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe, et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans;	And when this ancient dislocation occurs, it creates, and even more so in a moist environment, white or subtle boils, and sometimes these are fistulas that have burst.
et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	And they are recognized by those who have experienced it or witnessed it through defecation or flatulence when the patient excretes, and sometimes a worm may jump out.
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge;	And if the fistulas penetrate all the way to the bladder, and even halfway up the penis;
et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	and reach as far as the hip joint, and even to the bone of the knee.
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	And thus one recognizes a bursting fistula in the anus, and one that is not bursting.
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	and it is that you insert your index finger or thumb, and insert a fine needle made of brass or iron into the fistula when there is no tortuosity.
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou I poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	And if there is tortuosity, insert a slender tent made of lead or horsehair until you feel the tent or hair with your finger.
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	and if you do not feel it, and there is no discharge of matter or wind coming from the opening as we have mentioned:
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie;	know that it has not perforated.
si te haste dou curer.	then hasten to treat it.
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	And when the fistula pierces through to the bladder or the urine duct, it leaks urine, and cannot be healed by medicine.
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	If it is perforated up to the hip joint, then the tent has come through to that place.
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	If there is no distortion and the source of pain is obvious, it is best to go directly to surgery, and ointment provides no immediate cure.
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	And in the case of persistent fistulas, there is no cure other than operation, and it is the foolish vanity of doctors that interferes.
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit, et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos;	In those cases where it is not persistent and not an old injury either, there is hope of healing with iron [instruments], as I have experienced, and the patient lies prone on their back between your hands.
et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	Lift the legs up to the hips, and incline the hips towards the stomach.
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	Then insert an iron probe, or bronze if there is distortion, until you find the location of the fistula.
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice, se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet;	If the patient feels it around their anus, you should insert your index finger there, feeling if it has pierced the tendon.
et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	And when you feel it between your finger and the skin or flesh, then know that it has pierced through.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	Do not strain yourself if you cannot heal it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	It is said that some can be healed well, but this happens rarely.
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	The aid one provides is to heat the fine cautery according to the width of the fistula, as mentioned earlier.
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement;	And insert it all heated into the fistula until it reaches towards the anus.
et faice ceu II fois ou III, tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	And do this twice or three times until you know that these chards are burned, which resemble a bird's feather;
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	Then treat the wet tents with butter until that chard falls off, then cure it with ointment, sealing and binding.
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien.	If he is thus cured, it is good.
Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	If this cannot be healed in any other way;
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	And if the wound is internal, and does not pierce all the way to the bone that lies at its base, and between your finger and the wound there is thick chard or scab, and you see an opening in this that leads to the heart of the injury;
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	Cut at the beginning of the fistula, pushing back to before the wound, then cauterize afterwards until you reach the head of the wound.
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra;	And the swelling will be relieved, and it shall fall.
puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	Then mend those faulty sores that seem like a bird's feather, leaving nothing behind.
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	And if the blood defeats you and escapes between your finger and the work, cauterize it with fire or astringent medication.
Car li cauteres de feu assemble II bones choses:	For the fire cautery combines two things:
c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	That is to say, the burning of these adjoining sores, and the stemming of blood and drying of moisture;
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	Then treat moist swellings with butter or ground substances until the skin turns pale, and remove burnt sores from the pale flesh.
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	Then treat open wounds with hardening ointments for hard tissue, and use dry medications.
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	For when it is restored, it is cured and does not return.
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	And if the fistula extends to the anus, and is away from the body, put your finger in the anus, and inquire there.
Se tu sens la tente, et entre II est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des III manieres:	If you feel the tumor and find that it has reached the skin or subcutaneous tissue, or is close to breaking through, but there are no signs of certainty or hope except for a path seen through one of these three methods:
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	either you cauterize it as we have said, or you cut deep into it, or if you can create a new wound and treat it like the initial one.
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	and do not go too deep as to cut the tissue that holds the base, and cause evacuation from there unwillingly.
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	then treat it as we have said before.
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	if by chance it is discharging, then remove the covering and clean after cutting near the base, either through incision or another sharp instrument.
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	Then challenge this evil fault which is in the wound, as much as you can;
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement:	Then study to restore the wound, and stop the fistula outside of the foundation;
si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	If it were a lighter thing for the patient.
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere:	And sometimes fistulas occur in this manner:
et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus, si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	And it is when you insert the tent into the fistula, and it is beside the foundation near the skin above, take a perforated tent with a pointed end in this shape:
Et i boute I fil tort en II, et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	And here you insert the wire bent at right angles in such a way that it enters through one hole and exits from another; then you advance the probe along the entire length of the wire into the fistula until it reaches its end.
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	If it is pierced in the margin of the foundation inside, then withdraw the thread from that perforation, just as you would insert your finger into the foundation;
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les II chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse I jor ou II;	and pull the head of the thread through, joining the two heads together, holding one to the other, and leave it for one or two days.
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	and do not loosen it at any time, until the thread touches these parts which are between them, and they fall away.
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	then treat the wound until it is sealed and healed.
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	If the fistula does not rupture, make it perforate by all means possible unless it is too deeply embedded.
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	For it is not suitable to operate on the wound if it is too deeply embedded and then treat it as we have said until it heals.
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	The shape of the spatula with spines that we use to make the fistula is very sharp on one side and cutting.
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	and not sharp on the other side for this reason that you do not cut what must not be cut; as you can see here.
des emorroydes	From the hemorrhoids.
Emorrydes sont selonc II manieres:	Hemorrhoids occur in two ways.
ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc, et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement;	Where they are inside the fundament, like grains of resin, and there are small and large ones, and around them is blood, and there may be one or more, and they protrude from the fundament and at the head of the fundament.
mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor, et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	But those that protrude have little moisture, and around them is either a bit of yellow water or a bit of blood, and they have the colour of the body.
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	And the treatment for those who have them inside the fundament is that you instruct the patient to strain themselves to go to the toilet, until the fundament is outside and the son appears.
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	If you hurry, grab it with tongs or hold it with your nail, then cut it at its root.
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a I drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	and if its hooks cannot hold due to moisture, it grabs [the wound] with a cloth, or cotton, or a piece of chamois.
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	it extracts them with your two hands, then cuts and applies some hot powders in place of cautery.
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, pues les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	or you cauterize them as described in the chapter on cautery, or treat with other methods until they are healed.
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	and if the foundation cannot come out, then administer a harsh enema to cleanse what is in the fundament so that it can be expelled fully.
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	when the patient feels better, and if the thread is drawn out of the fundament without resistance, then the treatment is light.
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	And it is that you grasp them with your nail or with pincers, then clip and clean them as we have said, until they are healed, and fear the incision by iron.
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere:	It is fitting that you arrange the suture in this manner:
pren I fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les II chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille, et si soit dou large;	Take a twisted thread, insert it into a needle, and then draw the thread through, make the needle pierce from the other side, and turn the two ends of the thread under the needle, so that it is wide.
et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse I por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	Tighten the thread firmly, then knot the thread and remove the needle, do this for all of them except leave one open to allow excess blood to flow.
puis met sus le fondement I drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	Then place on the base a moistened cloth with rose oil or wax, and put it on the base, and instruct the patient to rest.
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	Leave it on until it softens, and once it has softened, treat it with ointment and other remedies until it is healed.
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	To dry up the phlegm or feces from the bowels
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	Often there is drying up of feces in the intestine, due to the constraint of nature and when the illness is old or medicine has no effect.
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	Make sure to scrape the bark off with a spatule or your fingernail so that it does not stay wet.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	Then treat it until it is healed as it should be.
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	And if it cannot heal, start the scraping again more vigorously than before until it bleeds and is scraped raw.
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat until it is healed.
dou fremit	cooling down
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	Ants are a small fault in the appearance of the body, and they go very deep inside.
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And sometimes the cold finds them, one feels them trembling like death, they are found all over the body and most of all in the hands.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	The treatment is to take a quill from a goose feather or the strong wing of a vulture and place this quill on the trembling spot until the purple circle around it disappears.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand around the entire quill until you cover all around the trembling spot and put it deep inside, uprooting the tremor from its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	And if you wish, make one from a cane of brass or iron according to this form, and let it be hollow below and solid above:
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser.	Do not pierce [it], to keep it attached to the finger, and press it.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	And if you see that, cauterize the swelling, just as it is described in the chapter on cautery.
de la forme dou clistere	Of the form of the clyster
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet;	Sometimes we use silver, quicksilver, or melted and hammered bronze for a clyster.
et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	And sometimes we use these instruments in small and large sizes according to what they are designed for.
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	Those which are fitted for the treatment of children and those who are weak and suffer pain are small.
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	The shape of the clyster large or small is broad above where the bellies are tied thus:
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez;	And if there is an issue with the intestines being tied up, as you see, and the intestine has been pierced...
et ait a l’un des costez II pertus, et en l’autre I;	and it has two holes on one side, and one on the other.
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus, et ait entre chescun pertus I doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus I fil fort de fil crut tort en X ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	and let the belly or place where you put the medicines be made of a beast's bladder or parchment, and pierce it all around with small holes, and leave an inch between each hole, then push into these holes a strong thread of twisted flax in the shape of an X or tie them together, and assemble the belly like a goat;
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize;	and when the medicine is inside, tie it to the instrument in front with a strong thread, then administer as an enema;
et c’est li forme dou cercle:	and this is its form like a circle:
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	And let the medicine not be too hot or too cold, and anoint the head of the enema with oil or egg white, or something similar, then gently insert it;
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses II mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit, et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet;	Then the minister should squeeze the patient's two hands together until it is completely visible, then withdraw the clyster, and lift the patient's legs to the wall, and if the medic wants him/her to go out, hold them as much as possible.
et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	And if he/she sleeps one night on it, this is greater help.
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if you enema him with a stomach illness of obstruction, and the medicine wants to exit prematurely, then restart it until he is healed.
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por I enfant;	And if the hemorrhoids or abscesses are in the anus, let the clyster be as gentle as for a child.
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	And this is the shape of the gentle clyster with which leather should be withdrawn:
des plaies	Of wounds
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies;	We have already spoken about treating wounds in this chapter.
or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	For we shall tell you the treatments of hands and medicines, according to their fulfillment.
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and where the wounds are located, as well as what caused them.
