puis l’estraint, et s’il i a os desevreit, si fent sus, et l’oste, et cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit sanee.	Then hold it firmly in place, and if there is a severed bone, do the same on top of it, remove it, and treat the wound until it is healed.
de la brisure de l’os de la hainche	Of the broken hip bone
Poc avient que li os de la hainche soit brisiez, et s’il avient, si n’avient fuer c’un poc d’amenuisement au chief;	Sometimes the hip bone is broken, which results in only a slight decrease in function at the joint.
et fent dou lonc, et decline au pardedens, et vient au malaide dolor au leu, et pointure, et enfle ceu que brise.	And make it long, and bend toward the back, and pain comes to the patient at the site, with pricking, swelling where broken.
Et li restoration si est que tu estendes ta main sus, tant que tu soies sus la briseure;	And hold your hand above it, so that you are over the break;
et saiches quelz est li brisure et li figure de li;	and check which is the fracture and its form;
et se li brisure est au chief soulement, si met igal cele brisure, tant qu’ele soit a figure natureil.	and if the break is only at the head, equalize this fracture so that it has its natural form.
Et se li brisure est dou lonc, ou elle decline au dedens, si fai gesir le malaide sus son ventre, tant que li restauration de cele brisure te soit aparillie.	And if the break is along its length, or it declines inwards, make the patient lie on their stomach so that you can see to restore this break.
Et quant tu l’avras mise igal, si met sus l’emplaustre, puis met sus une estele de fust ou de keur, et estraint la briseure, si qu’ele ne se mueve;	And when you have made it even, place an ointment on top, then put a stick of wood or heartwood above it and secure the break so that it does not move.
et emple le leu desoz les costes, tant que li lieure soit igalz.	And pad the place below the sides until the level is even.
Et comande au malaide k’il dorme sus son costeit sain, ou sus son dos.	Instruct the patient to sleep on their healthy side or their back.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si n’i tochier, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez, et met sus ceu que nos avons devant dit;	And if hot abscesses develop, do not touch them until the hot abscesses are pacified, and apply what we have previously mentioned.
et puis revien a la restauration, et l’estraint si com il covient, s’il n’i a nul mavais accident;	then return to the restoration and hold it as required if there is no adverse event;
et c’est li maniere.	and this is the method.
de la brisure de l’ajutoire	Of shoulder dislocation
Li adjutoires est ceu qui est entre lou coute et lou chief de l’espaule, et s’il est brisiez, si le doit on restorer selonc l’une des II manieres:	The shoulder joints are located between the armpit and the head of the shoulder, and if they are broken, they must be restored using one of two methods:
dont l’une est que tu pren I fust plain de moiene groissor, selonc ceste forme:	one of which is to take a single piece of wood with an average thickness, in this shape:
Et lie as II chiés II liens, et les pent en haut, et siece li malaide sus I siege;	Attach two ties to the two ends of it, lifting them upwards, and place the patient on a seat;
puis li giete som bras brisiet sus le fust, tant qu’il viegne a l’aissele, et ait em mi une corbeure de fust, puis pent sus aucune pesant chose ou li ministres l’estende aval;	Then throw their broken arm onto the stick until it reaches the elbow, and place in the middle a wooden bend, then lean on something heavy where the ministers stretch them down;
puis mette li mires la briseure igal a ses mains ensamble, tant que li briseure retorne si com il covient.	Then place the splint so it breaks equally at their hands together, until the break returns as it should.
Et li autre maniere si est que on sovine le malaide sus son hatereil, et li lie la main a son col, puis comande a II ministres que li uns teigne ceu qui est sus la briseure a ses mains, et li autres teigne desoz a tout I liien, et estende chescuns a sa partie.	The second method involves hoisting the patient onto their back and tying their hand to their neck; next command two assistants such that one holds what is above the fracture in both hands while the other supports below at every joint, stretching each part as far as they are able.
Et se tu vues que li estraction soit plus fors, si estraint I liien desoz la briseure, et sus la briseure, et estende chescuns des ministres a sa part.	And if you see that the extraction is more powerful, then restrain the ligament below the fracture, and above the fracture, and stretch each of the ministers to their respective parts.
Et se li briseure est prochiene au chief de l’espaule, si covient que tu mettes I liien moien desoz l’assele, et I autre vers lou coute, desoz la briseure;	And if the break is near the head of the shoulder, you must place one strap under the armpit and another towards the cut, underneath the splint.
et ausi se li briseure est devers lou coute, si i covient mettre I liien legierement, sens labor, tant que li briseure soit igalz sus lou leu, et sus lou coute;	And if the break is towards the cut, you must place one strap lightly and gently so that the splint is aligned on the arm and over the shoulder.
puis met igal la brisure, si com il covient, et l’estraint, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	Then set the fracture evenly, as it is required, and hold it steady, unless incisions from abscesses occur.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si ne l’estraindre mie jusc’a VII jors, et met sus lainne moillie en aisil et en oile roset, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez;	And if incisions from abscesses do occur, do not hold it tight for seven days, and apply moist woolen cloth with rose oil until the incisions have healed.
puis l’estraint, et li maniere de l’estraindre si est que tu mettes l’emplaustre sus la briseure, puis assemble le bras sus l’ajutoire, et met ta main sus l’espaule ou sus lou sein;	Then hold it tight again, and the way to do so is that you apply a poultice on the fracture, then bring the arm onto the shoulder, and place your hand over the shoulder or armpit.
et met le drapeil, et estraint sus l’ajutoire, et sus lou bras, si que li bras soit en leu d’esteles, s’aucune chose ne le te deffent, ou se li os n’est muez.	And place the cloth, and hold it tightly over the shoulder and arm, so that the arm is in its natural position, unless something prevents it or if the bone has moved.
Et se tu doutes que li os ne se mueve, si use d’esteles, et met sus la brisure une estele plus large et plus fort des autres, et ait entre chescune estele I doi d’espaice, et soit chescune estele si grans qu’elle passe la briseure III dois de chescune part;	And if you doubt that the bone is not moving, use splints, and place on the fracture a splint wider and stronger than the others, with two fingers of space between each one, and let each splint be so large that it passes three fingers beyond each side of the break.
puis estrain sus les esteles, ensi com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre sus la briseure, plus fort et moins en aloignant.	Then pull up on the splints, just as I said at the beginning of this chapter regarding fractures, with more force and less separation.
Et se tu vois l’assise des esteles, et l’estrignement, si com nos avons dit, en l’oure que tu restoures le membre brisiet, et tu doutes l’aposteme chaut, si le laisse a liier jusc’a septime jor, si com nos avons dit;	And if you see the placement of the splints and the constriction, as we have said when restoring a broken limb, and doubt the hot abscess, leave it bound until the seventh day, just as we've stated.
puis regarde chescuns III jors lou lien, que prurite ne enfleure n’i viegne au leu, ou li norrissemens ne puist venir au membre por ceu k’il est trop estrois.	Then check it every three days to ensure that no itching or swelling occurs where the splint is bound, nor any numbness in the limb due to excessive tightness.
Si l’adrece, si com nos avons dit.	If addressed as we have said.
Et se nulz telz accidens n’i vient, si ne lou desliier fuer que aprés III jors ou plus, et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ait ses mains sus son stomac;	And if no such accidents occur, you should not release the dislocation before three days or more have passed. The patient must sleep on their back with their hands resting on their stomach.
et met desoz l’ajutoire I cussin plain de laine igalment, et regarde chescune houre dou jor ou de la nut, que li figure dou membre brisiet ne se mueve, ou ne soit amollis li liiens;	Place a cushion of equal wool under the affected shoulder. Check every hour during the day or night to ensure that the broken limb's position does not change and its joints do not loosen.
si l’adrece par la vertu de medicine, et li done la viande que nos avons devant mis, en teil maniere que li viande soit au premier subtilz;	If the injury heals through medical treatment, give them the food we mentioned before in such a way that their diet is very light at first.
et quant il comance a reprendre, si soit grosse.	And when they start to recover, make their diet heavier.
Et est costume que li ajutoire et li jambe doient estre repris en XL jors dou tout;	It is customary for the shoulder and leg injuries to take forty days to heal completely.
et adonques lou doit on desliier et aministrer bain et medicines d’oignemens por le leu adrecier.	And then it must be loosened and treated with baths and ointment medicines to realign its place.
Et se li estricture est laide et emboee, si demore a desliier L jors ou II mois.	And if the dislocation is severe and difficult to move, it may take one day or two months to relieve it.
de la brisure du bras	Of arm fracture:
Li bras est compos de II os, qui sont apelez li dui «foscile», de coi li uns est petis, et est cil qui enseut le pouchet;	The arm is composed of two bones, which are called the "duo foscile", one of which is small and follows the wrist.
et li autres est grans, et est cil qui est desoz, devers lou petit doi;	And the other is large, which is below towards the little finger.
par aventure brise li grans foscile soulement, ou li petis, et par aventure andui ensamble.	Perhaps only the large bone breaks or maybe just the small one, but perhaps it's both together.
Quant li petis fosciles est brisiez, li restaurations est legiere, et li sanations;	When the small bone is broken, its restoration is light and its healing swift.
et quant li grans est brisiez, si est li sanation male, et plus griés que quant il sont brisiez andui ensamble.	And when the large bone is broken, its healing is difficult and more serious than if they were both broken together.
Se c’est li petis foscile qui est brisiez soulement, si le covient poc estendre legierement, et mettre igal.	If it is only the small bone that is broken, one should extend it gently and set it evenly.
Et se c’est li grans foscile, si le covient estraindre plus fort;	And if it is a large wound, you must compress it more firmly;
et l’estende sus I cussin, et teigne le pouchet de la main plus haut des autres, et li petis dois plus bas des autres dois, et soit li malaides croisiez sus lui meisme, et I cussin devant lui plus haut, que li malaides ne soffre nule labor;	place them on a cushion, and hold the wrist of the hand higher than the others, with the little fingers lower than the other fingers, and let the patient be crossed over themselves, and the cushion in front of them, elevated so that the patient may not suffer any exertion;
puis estende li ministres som bras a la partie desoz a sa main, ou a I liien, et uns autres ministres a I autre au desus.	Then have your assistants extend their arms to the part below the patient's hand or wrist, while another assistant is above them on the other side.
Et puis le mette li mires igal, selonc sa millor forme.	Then place the mirror in front of them evenly so they see their best form.
Et se en la brisure a pieces, si met chescune en son leu, et s’il en i a nule desevree ke poigne lou keur, et tu ne la pues restorer en son leu, si fent sus et l’oste, si com nos avons dit devant.	And if the bone is broken into pieces, place each one back in its place and grasp the heart of any piece that cannot be restored to its original position; then cut it away as we have said before.
Et se avec la briseure a plaie, je en ai parleit au chapistre singuler;	And if with the fracture causing injury, I have spoken of it in the singular chapter;
si pren la cure.	then take care of the treatment.
Et se en l’encomencement dou restorement sorvient apostemes chaus, si glue I drapeil de cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire blainche, que ne soit mie ne trop durs ne trop molz;	And if in the beginning of the restoration hot abscesses appear, so prepare the bandage with a cerate made from rose oil and white wax, let it be neither too hard nor too soft;
et lie I drapeil par sus subtilment, tant que li apostemes chaus soit apaisiez.	and bind the bandage on gently, so that the hot abscesses may be calmed.
Et puis oste lou cerote, et i met l’emplaustre de la poudre dou molin avec abun d’uef, pues met les esteles, et soit li estele de la briseure adés plus fors, et un poc plus large que les autres;	Then remove the cerate, and apply an emplastrum made from mill powder with much egg white, then place the splints, making sure that the splint for the fracture is closer and a little wider than the others;
et saiches que il doit avoir VI esteles ou bras em plusors dispositions:	and know that there must be six splints on an arm in various arrangements:
soit que li briseure soit en l’un des os, soit en II;	whether the fracture is in one of the bones or in two;
et estraint plus sus la briseure que autre part, et toz jors moins en aloignant, si com j’ai dit au comencement dou chapistre;	and hold it tightly above the fracture, less so elsewhere, and always more in the direction of the break, as I said at the beginning of this chapter.
et soient li drapelz que sont sus la briseure molz et moistes, et ne soient mie dur ne aspres;	and let the cloths that are placed on the fracture be soft and moist, not hard or rough.
et soit li filz, dont il est estrains, de lin, ne trop gros ne trop menus, si com nos avons dit.	and let the thread with which it is held be made of linen, not too thick nor too fine, as we have said.
Et rewarde lou membre et lou liien aprés aucuns jors.	Reward the limb and ligament after a few days.
Et se aucuns mavais accidens vient au membre, si com prurite ki vient au membre, si covient que tu aroses lou membre d’aigue chaude, tant que cil prurites soit apaisiez;	And if any adverse event occurs in the limb, such as an itch that arises there, you must spray the limb with warm water until the itching is relieved.
et laisse le membre ne mie estroit reposer.	and let the limb rest without restriction.
Et puis rencomence l’estrignement, et se li liiens est amolis et li os desevrez, et semblant chose, si l’adresce.	Then restart the tightening process, and if the ligament is softened and the bones are separated or similar, address it.
Et se pren warde se li norrissemens ne puet venir au membre, por ceu qu’il est trop estrois, si covient que tu l’amollisses I poc, et laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant que li norrissemens i corre, et puis l’estraint.	And if you observe that nourishment cannot reach the limb due to its tightness, it is necessary that you soften it a little, and leave it thus for a few days until circulation flows again; then tighten it.
Et se nules de ces choses que nos avons dit ne vient au malaide, si ne lou desliier jusc’a XX jors.	And if none of these things we have said come to pass for the patient, do not release them until 20 days have passed.
ou enqui entor, puis li pent les mains a son col, et soit ses cols igalz, et se warde de movement et de degitement, et dorme sus son dos;	Where you inquire around him, then paint his hands on his neck, and let his necks be even, and beware of movement and twisting, and sleep on his back;
et saiches que ceste briseure est restoree en XXX jors ou en XXXV, et par aventure en XX jors, selonc les compositions et les complexions des vertus.	and know that this fracture is healed in thirty days or thirty-five, and perhaps even twenty, depending on the combinations and complexities of qualities.
de la brisure de la main	On the fracture of the hand
Saiches que au dos de la main et as nous des dois avient poc de briseures, et n’i vient mais que ploieure maintes fois.	Know that on the back of the hand and at the knuckles there are few fractures, but rather it is more often a dislocation.
Et quant li plante de la main est brisie ou ploie, si covient que li malaides siece croisiet, et siet droitement devant lui igalement;	And when the heel of the hand is fractured or bent, it is necessary for the patient to sit cross-legged, and sit upright directly in front of him evenly.
puis met sa main sus la toie estendue, et estende li ministres les os brisiez, et les mete igalz li mires, tant qu’il soient bien joint;	then place his hand on the stretched cloth, and have the assistants stretch out the fractured bones, and make them even with each other, so that they are well-aligned.
et met l’emplastre et les estoupes, se apostemes n’i vient, puis i met une estele selonc la quantiteit dou leu;	and apply the plaster and bandages, unless an abscess forms, then place a splint according to the extent of injury.
et soit envoloupee en I drapeil de lin.	And it shall be enveloped in one linen cloth.
Et se li briseure est au pardedens entor lou ventre de la plante, si fai une spere de drapelz, et comande au malaide qu’il l’estrigne a sa plante brisie;	And if the fracture is around the front of the sole [of the foot], make a sphere of cloth, and instruct the patient to strap it tight against their broken sole.
et puis l’estrain d’un lonc drapeil, et soit li estele de keur souef ausi grans com li plante de la main, et l’estraint, si com il covient.	Then strap it with a long cloth, and let the heart-wood peg be as large as the sole of the hand, then tighten it accordingly.
Et se li brisure est au defuer, si covient que tu mettes une estele sus, et une autre desoz en la plante, si que li mains soit overte et droite, puis le lie tot entor la main, et estanche lou liien entre les dois.	And if the fracture is on the outside, you must put a pad above and another below the broken bone, so that the hand is open and straight; then bind it all around the hand, and secure the binding between the fingers.
Et se li briseure vient a aucun des nous des dois, se c’est li pouchés, si le met igal, si com il covient;	And if the fracture occurs in one of the fingers, set it equal [straight], as is required.
et l’estraint avec la plante, et se tu vues si met une estele droite petite por lever la briseure, et ne se mueve;	And strap it with the sole [of the foot], and if you wish to insert a small straight peg to lift the fracture, and do not move it.
et se li brisure est as autres dois, si com en l’indice ou l’un des autres, si le met igal, et lou lie avec lou doi sain qui est aprés;	and if the fracture is in other places, such as in the index finger or any of the others, make it equal and bind it with the healthy finger that comes next.
ou tu les lie toz en I tenant, que mues vaut, ou tu met sus une estele, si com ou pouchet;	or you bind them all together at the base, as it moves better, or place a stick above it, just like for an arrow.
et pren warde en la restauration et en la disposition d’aposteme chaut, et secor ceu qui i vient, si com j’ai dit.	and take care in the restoration and treatment of a hot abscess, and alleviate what comes from it, as I have said.
de la cuixe brisie	of the broken thigh
Li os de la cuixe est maintes fois brisiez, et bien le voit on quant elle torne devant et derrier;	The thigh bone is often fractured, and it is clearly seen when the leg turns forward or backward.
et li restauration si est c’on lie I liien desus la briseure, et I autre desoz.	and its restoration is done by binding the two sides above and below the fracture.
Et li malaides gise sus sa faice, puis estende chescuns ministres son lien a sa part igalment;	The patient lies on their face, then each attendant stretches their rope to its equal part.
et c’est quant li brisure est emmi l’os.	and this is when the fracture is within the bone.
Et se li brisure est prochiene a la racine de la cuixe, si soit li uns des liiens devers lou poignil, et li autres liiens desoz la briseure.	If the fracture is close to the root of the thigh bone, one binding should be towards the armpit, and the other bindings below the fracture.
Et ausi s’elle est prochiene au genoil, et adonques soit li liens delez lou genoil, et soit li extension aval;	Also, if it is near the knee, then let the rope be placed below the knee, and the stretching be done downwards.
puis mette li mires l’os igal a ses II mains, tant qu’il soit selonc sa figure natureil, et puis met l’emplaustre, et lou lie, se apostemes chaz n’i vient.	Then the surgeon should place the bone evenly with both hands, aligning it to its natural shape, and then apply a plaster cast, binding it up if an abscess forms.
Et s’il i a aposteme chaut, si le laisse apaisier puis revien a ton ovraige et a ta cure;	If there is a warm abscess present, leave it to heal before returning to your work and treatment.
li lieure est faite en teil maniere.	The binding is done in this way:
Il covient que tu envoloupes sus la briseure I bendeil dur doublé en II ou III, et en demoure li superfluitez, puis torne la jambe tant que li talons veigne a la racine de la naige, et boute I fil lonc entre la cuixe et la jambe, delez lou genoil desoz, et veignent li chief dou fil au desus;	It is necessary that you wrap over the fracture with I hard bandage doubled in II or III, and let the excess remain, then turn the leg so that the heel reaches the base of the thigh, and thread I long piece of string between the thigh and the leg, around the knee below, and bring the end of the string above;
puis torne sus la jambe et sus la cuixe le bendeil, puis met sus la briseure esteles, et met une estele sus l’os de la jambe;	Then turn the bandage over the leg and up the thigh, then place splints on the fracture, and put a splint on the bone of the leg;
puis emple le leu vuit entre la jambe et la cuixe de drapelz souef por mettre igal l’estrignement, puis comence a liier forment III tors ou IIII sus la briseure;	Then fill the empty space between the leg and thigh with soft cloths to evenly distribute the pressure, then begin to bind tightly in the form of III twists or IIII over the fracture;
et quant plus vas en sus de la briseure, et moins l’estraint;	And as you go further above the fracture, bind it less tightly;
puis enten as II chiés dou fil que tu as bouteit entre la jambe et la cuixe, et en lie III esteles que sont desus, puis revai au desoz au chief dou fil, tant que tu veignes delez le piet;	Then attend to the two knots of thread that you have passed between the leg and thigh, and tie three stitches above them, then return below to the end of the thread until you reach near the foot.
et l’estraint, si qu’il ne se mueve de son leu, puis le laisse ensi, puis k’il n’i vient ne aposteme ne enfleure n’autre semblant.	Hold it tight so that it does not move from its place, then leave it like this until neither an abscess nor swelling or any other similar issue appears.
Et s’il i avient, si le deslie, et adresce ceu que i vient, si com nos avons dit maintes fois;	And if it does appear, then untie it and address the issue that has arisen as we have said many times before;
et se il i a pieces de l’os que poigne, si le covient ewer, s’om puet;	And if there are splinters of bone stuck in the wound then it must be irrigated with water if one is able to do so;
et s’on ne puet, si covient fendre le leu, et traire fuer;	And if this cannot be done then you must open the wound further to extract them with forceps;
et le cure si com nos avons dit, tant k’il soit sanez.	And treat him as we have said, until he is healed.
Et aucune fois est brisie li cuixe ensi c’on i met esteles, si com en l’ajutoire et ou bras;	And sometimes the thigh is broken so that pins are inserted, as in the shoulder and arm;
toutevoie, en la restauration ensi faite ne cloche mie li malaides.	However, when such restoration is performed, the patient does not suffer.
Et saiches que li cuixe est restoree en L jors, ou poc moins ou poc plus, selonc les diversitez des complexions.	And know that the thigh is restored in twenty days, or perhaps a little less or more, depending on the diversity of constitutions.
de la ruelle dou genoil	From the groove of the knee.
Saiches que en la ruelle dou genoil avient poc brisure, mais elle ploie maintes fois.	Know that in the knee alley there is little breakage, but it bends many times.
Et s’elle brise, si n’est mais c’une fendure, ou I pertus, et avient a tout plaie, et sens plaie, et ce sent om bien.	And if it breaks, it is but a crack or hole, and this happens with any wound, both wounded and unwounded, and one feels good about it.
Et li restauration si est c’on mette igal ceu qui est rons a ses dois, tant qu’il soit assemblez mues c’on puet;	And the restoration is such that one places what is rounded in its place with both hands until they are joined as well as can be done.
puis met l’emplaustre, et i met une estele reonde, se tu en as mestier, et l’estraint si com il covient, puis rewarde toutes les dispositions que nos avons dit ens autres briseures, si com aposteme chaut et autre semblant;	Then apply the plaster and insert a round pin if needed, securing it properly. Then follow all the procedures we have outlined for other fractures, such as hot abscesses and similar conditions.
si met a chescun accident ceu k’il li covient, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If you apply to each injury what is appropriate for it, until it heals.
de la brisure de la jambe	On the breaking of the leg
Saiches que en la jambe ait II os, de coi li uns est apelez par droit non «mustelz», et li autres est apelez «foscile»;	Know that in the leg there are two bones, of which one is rightly called "shin," and the other is called "tibia.
et avient tout auteil briseure com il vient au bras, et por ceu est li restauracion si com celle dou bras igalment, et li ovraiges est tout i. Et se li dui os sont brisiet ensamble, si torne li jambe de toutes pars.	And they have similar fractures as those that occur in the arm, and for this reason, the restoration is the same as that of the arm, and the treatments are all there too. If both bones are broken together, then the leg turns from all sides.
Et se li os subtilz est brisiez, si torne devant.	And if the delicate bone is broken, return to the previous step.
Et se li gros os est brisiez, si sent on grant dolor, et le voit on bien;	And if the larger bone is broken, one feels great pain, and it shows well.
et torne desoz.	And it turns downwards.
Adonques amenistre extension, et le met igal, et lie les esteles igalement;	Therefore, provide extension, make them equal, and tie the splints equally.
mais toutevoie, il covient se li brisure est laide, et il i a plusors pieces, que li extension soit menor et plus legiere;	But nonetheless, if the fracture is ugly and there are many fragments, the stretching should be reduced and made lighter.
et l’alige selonc ta vertu.	And ease it according to your skill.
Et quant tu as tout acomplit ton ovraige, si pren II faixes de fust chevees que porpreignent la jambe d’une part et d’autre, et soient dou lonc de la jambe des le genoil jusque desoz;	And when you have completed your work, take two strips of wood and wrap them around the leg on either side, making sure they are as long as the leg from the knee down.
puis envoloupe en II leus I bendeil desus et desoz, et le lie em mileu ausi, et a ceste lieure ne pora li jambe decliner a destre ne a senestre, et ensi est bien;	Then wrap two linen bandages around them and tie one in the middle, so that the leg cannot bend to the right or left. In this way it is well-supported.
et aucun i aministrent I bers dou lonc de la jambe, et s’est de fust, et i met on la jambe por warder de movement, et proprement fait on ceu en la brisure ou il a plaie;	And have them put a splint along the length of the leg, made of wood or other material, to protect against any movement. It should be applied directly above where there is an open wound due to fracture.
et remue chescun jor la jambe, por veoir s’il i a aposteme chaut n’autre accident;	and move each leg daily to check for abscess or other complications;
si le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	if he treats it until it is healed.
de la brisure des os dou piet	Of broken bones of the foot
A la cheville ne vient point de brisure, mais as os dou piet vient aucune fois brisure et as dois poc, et n’i avient fuer que quassure em plusor dispositions.	At the ankle, there is no fracture, but in the bones of the foot, there can be breaks and bruises, and sometimes only a sprain in various conditions.
Et s’il avient as os dou piet brisure, et tu vois ces os sormonter l’un l’autre, si mette si malaides som piet sus la terre, ausi com s’il voloit aler, et puis met maintenant ton piet sus lou sien, lai ou li os sont levez, puis le presse tant k’il reveignent en lor leus;	And if there is a broken bone in the foot, and you see these bones overlapping each other, let the patient put his injured foot on the ground as if he wanted to walk, then place your foot on top of theirs, where the bones are raised, then press it until they return to their original positions;
puis met l’emplaustre et estoupes sus, et met desoz lou ventre dou piet une petite tauble a II chiés plains, puis l’estraint au piet avenanment, puis que tu as envoloupez drapelz entor, et autres choses dont tu as mestier.	Then apply the plaster and pack it with dressings, place under the belly of the foot a small wooden board with two curved ends, then strap it to the foot carefully, then wrap it with bandages and other materials you may need.
Et quant III jors ou IIII seront passez, si deslie lou liien, car tu troveras les os igalz, soient brisiez, soient desaluez.	And when three or four days have passed, untie the binding, for you will find the bones equalized, whether broken or dislocated.
Et s’il i a aucuns des dois brisiez, si les restoure, si com nos avons dit as dois de la main;	And if there are any broken fingers, restore them, just as we have said for the fingers of the hand;
puis met au doi brisiet une estele selonc la longesce dou doi, et soit un poc plus large, puis met desoz le piet celle tauble que j’ai dit, et l’estrain avenanment;	Then place a splint on the broken finger in alignment with its length, and let it be slightly wider. Place underneath the foot that board I mentioned, and strain it appropriately;
et s’il en i a II ou III, ou plus, brisiez, si met sus chescun doi une estele selonc sa quantiteit, envoloupee en I drapeil de lin, et estraint la tauble desoz lou piet;	And if there are two or three, or more, broken fingers, place a splint on each finger according to its size, wrapped in a linen cloth. Straiten the board underneath their foot;
et soit estans sus lou chief de la tauble defuer lou ventre dou piet, si qu’il le teigne bien.	And let it be stretched over the head of the board outside their stomach so that it holds them well.
Et covient que tu n’oblier mie les autres choses que j’ai dit as autres briseures, des que nos avons dit;	And make sure you do not forget the other things I mentioned for treating breaks, just as we have said before;
et secor chescun accident si com il covient.	And heal every injury as it is required.
de la brisure de l’os dou poignil	Of the fracture of the wrist bone
Quant li os de la nature la femme est brisiez, si la fai seoir enlargie, puis l’encline a la partie dou dos, et soit tenue par derrier;	When the bones of a woman's back are broken, make her sit spread out, then lean her towards the back part and support her from behind;
puis emplisse li baile la nature de la malaide de couton, et en i mette ausi gros com I sto;	Then fill the patient's hollow back with cotton, and put in as much as it holds;
puis deboute la femme, et lieve lou dos poc et poc, et adonques saut li coton, tant qu’il vient a l’entree de la nature, et revient li os avec lou sto;	Then stand the woman up, lift her back bit by bit, and as the cotton rises, until it reaches the opening of her back passage, and the bones return to their place;
et quant elle vuet pissier, si oste lou coton, et quant elle a pissiet, se li remette, et ensi faice VII jors ou entor:	And when she needs to urinate, remove the cotton, and once she is done, put it back in, and do this for seven days or so;
si sera restoree li brisure, et se tu vues, pren une vessie de berbis, et lie au pertus une cainne, et boute toute la vessie en la nature;	si sera restoree li brisure, and if you see it, take a sheep's bladder, tie a cane to the opening, and insert all of the bladder into the body.
puis soffle en la cainne forment, tant que li vessie soit enflee dedens:	then blow hard into the cane, so that the bladder becomes completely inflated inside.
la nature si revenra li brisure;	the body will realign the broken bones.
puis soit emplie de coton, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit sanez.	then fill it with cotton and leave it like that for a few days until the wound heals.
Et quant li os dou poignil de l’ome est brisiez, ou de la femme, si le restoure ensi com nos avons dit en l’os de la hainche;	And when the wrist bone of a man or woman is broken, restore it in the same way as we have described for the hip bone.
et ne sont mie occultees ces briseures prochienes a celui qui i met son estude et son us, et entent mon livre.	these fractures near the wrist are not hidden from those who study them diligently and read my book.
Car li brisure li signifie em plusors dispositions la droite voie de la restauration:	For the breaking [of bones] indicates to many its correct method of restoration:
enten le donques.	Understand it then.
En la verge, quant elle est brisie, pren une gorge d’oie et i boute la verge;	In the penis, when it is broken, take a goose's windpipe and insert it into the penis;
puis envoloupe drapelz entor, et le laisse III jors ou enqui entor, et il sera sanez hastanment.	Then wrap it in cloth around, and leave it for three days so that it may heal swiftly.
de brisure avec plaie	Of breaks that have wounds.
Il covient a celui qui a brisure avec plaie, meismement s’elle est grans, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire ou semblant, qu’il soit sainiez maintenant, si que les sainies que nos avons dit le tesmoignent.	It is necessary for one who has a break with wounds, especially if it's large like the bone of the thigh or shoulder, to be healed swiftly, as the healings we have discussed attest to.
Et se li plaie saine, si la restainche de vitriole, se tu n’as autre chose, puis rencomence a restorer la briseure en cele meisme houre, ou celui jor, se apostemes chaus n’i vient.	And if the wound heals, apply vitriol to staunch it, if you have nothing else, then begin again to restore the fracture that same hour or day, unless a hot abscess comes about.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si laisse la restauration jusc’a nuevime jor, tant que li apostemes soit apaisiez, et n’i touchier ne au tier jor ne au quart, car tu i feroies venir malvais accident.	If a hot abscess does occur, leave the restoration for nine days until the abscess is alleviated, and do not touch it on the third or fourth day, as you would bring about an ill outcome.
Et se li os brisiez est aparans sus lou keur descovert, si covient que tu lou mettes a point legierement a tes mains, a extension petite.	And if the broken bone is visible on an uncovered heart, you must set it gently with your hands in slight extension.
Et se li extensions ne t’est apareillie por mettre igal a tes mains, si le ramoine a cest estrument qui est de fer, qui a VII dois ou VIII de lonc, et li largesce est selonc la quantiteit de la plaie;	And if the extension is not equipped to align with your hands, then reset it with this iron instrument which has seven or eight tines and its width according to the size of the wound;
et por ceu est mestier au mire qu’il empreigne III ou IIII, selonc ceu qu’il en ait mestier en chescune cure de briseure;	and for this it is necessary that the surgeon apply pressure three or four times according to what is needed in each treatment of a broken bone.
et soit rons et un poc gros, k’il ne ploie mie a la compression sus lou membre a ton ovraige, et soit agus devant, et gros des le mileu en avant, ensi:	and round and slightly thick so that it does not bend under pressure on the limb you are working on, and pointed at the front, and thick from the middle onwards, like this;
Et est apelez «palainche», por coi il covient que li chiés corbes soit mis sus lou chief de l’os apparent;	It is called 'palainche', which means the curved head should be placed on top of the visible bone;
et le boute a une fois, tant k’il reviegne, et soit igalz l’un encontre l’autre.	and push it in one go until it returns to its place, ensuring they are aligned with each other.
Et se li brisure est subtilz, et li estrumens ne puet bien prendre l’os, si covient que tu copes lou chief de l’os, tant que li estrumens en ait possance.	And if the fracture is subtle, and the instrument cannot grasp the bone properly, then you must cut away the head of the bone until the instrument has a firm grip.
Et se tu ne pues ramener l’os, si com nos avons dit, si lou cope d’un estrument covenable a ceu, ou incisoire ou soieure, a ton pooir;	And if you cannot reposition the bone as we have said, then use an appropriate tool such as an incision knife or a saw to your ability;
puis reis ceu qui est demorez en l’os d’aspreteit et de menues escorces.	then remove what remains in the bone of roughness and small splinters.
Et quant li os est ramenez, et li malaides sent grant dolor aprés, saiches qu’il n’est mie en son leu natureil.	And when the bone is reset, and the patient feels great pain afterward, know that it is not yet in its natural place.
Si fai tant qu’il soit en son leu, puis moille I drapeil en vin stiptique noir, et proprement se c’est en esteit;	Si make sure it is back in its place, then wet a cloth with black styptic wine, and properly so if it is on the face.
et ne mettre mie sus la plaie cerote ne autre chose ou il ait oile, qu’il n’i faice venir porriture et corruption;	and do not put any ointment or other oily substance on the wound as it will cause sores and decay;
puis aministre esteles quant tu as restoreit l’os, et laisse la plaie descoverte, et cope la coverture tout entor, selonc la quantiteit de la plaie, et te done bien en garde que li plaie ne soit estrainte avec la brisure;	then apply splints once you have reset the bone, and leave the wound uncovered, wrapping the covering all around according to the size of the wound, taking great care that the wound is not constricted with the break.
et maintes fois ont ce fait li fol mire, et ont fait venir sus le malaide ou mort ou corrodent aucune fois;	and many times have these foolish doctors done this, causing death or corrosion in some cases.
et soit li estrignemens plus molz et plus souef des autres brisures.	and the constriction should be looser and softer than with other breaks.
Et se li plaie est male ou grans, et tu doutes que mavais accidens n’i veigne, si com nos avons dit, et tu trueves dolor au leu, si n’i covient mie mettre sus esteles;	And if the wound is severe or large, and you fear bad consequences may arise, as we have mentioned, and you find pain in that place, it should not be treated with stars.
mais envoloupe entor, en leu d’esteles, drapelz durs, et les lie.	But instead of using stars, wrap around it sturdy linen cloths, and tie them in place.
Et quant tu vois aprés I jor ou II enjanrer bowe a la plaie, si oste ceu que tu as mis sus a tout vin, et i met oignement sanant plaies, si com oignement tetrafarmaçon et semblans.	And when you see swelling after one or two days at the wound, remove what you have placed on it entirely, and apply healing ointment such as Tetraconion and similar ones.
Et covient que tu deslies lou membre II fois le jor, lou matin et au vespre, tant qu’il soit soudez et sanez.	You must loosen the limb twice a day, in the morning and at night, until it is fused and healed.
Et covient que li membres soit aparilliez en teil maniere que li bowe corre aval legierement.	And ensure that the limb is bandaged in such a way that the swelling runs down slightly.
Et se maint jor trespassent, et il ne puet souder mais rent adés bowe, saiches k’il i a petites pieces d’os, por coi il covient que tu quieres la plaie avec tente, et oste toutes ces pieces desevrees que font venir celle dolor.	And if after many days it still does not heal but swells again, know that there are small bone fragments present, which is why you must probe the wound with a needle, and remove all these dislocated pieces causing pain.
Et se fistule vient au leu, ou autre maniere de corruption, si covient que tu le cures, selonc ceu qu’il dist en son chapistre ci devant.	And if a fistula forms there, or any other kind of corruption occurs, then you must treat it according to what he says in his chapter previously mentioned.
Et quant li os est brisiez, et apert sus lou membre, si com li os de la cuixe ou de l’ajutoire, et autres semblans des grans membres, si ne le traire mie, car maintes fois en vient li mors, mais le laisse tant qu’il porrisse;	And when the bone is broken and protruding from the limb, like the thighbone or humerus, and other such large bones, do not pull it out, for death often results, but leave it until it rots.
par aventure cherra par lui aprés XX jors ou XXX, puis cure la plaie, se tu pues;	Perhaps after twenty or thirty days it may fall off by itself, then treat the wound if you are able to do so.
et se tu ne pues, si la laisse.	And if you cannot, leave it be.
des brus qui vienent sor la sodure	wounds that arise over the suture
Nous vienent maintes fois aprés la santeit de la briseure, meismement quant c’est pres de la jointure, et laide chose est a veoir li figure dou membre;	We often come after the health of the fracture, especially when it is close to the joint, and it is an unpleasant sight to see the shape of the limb.
et par aventure ne puet faire li membres ses ovraiges naturelz.	and perhaps the limb cannot perform its natural functions.
Pren warde donques se li nous est fres:	Take care then if it is fresh for us:
si li aministre medicines stiptiques, si com aloes, encens, et mirre, et sarcocolle, acaice, et semblans autres, ensi que tu preignes aucune de ces choses, ou toutes ensamble, et les confit avec vin stiptique ou avec abun d’uef ou avec aisil;	if the administrator of medicines gives you astringents, such as aloe, incense, and myrrh, or substances like sarco collum, galbanum, and similar others, then ensure you take any of these things, or all together, and mix them with astringent wine or egg white or isinglass;
et les met sus le nout en estoupes, et l’estraint bien, et ne la desliier en mains jors;	and apply them to the wound with pads, pressing it firmly, and do not remove it by hand for a day;
et puis la desloie, et rencomence une autre, tant que li nodations soit ostee;	Then dislocate it again, and begin another one, until the knots are removed.
ou tu estrain sus une piece de plonc bien faite;	where you strain it over a well-formed plank of wood;
car li proprietez dou plonc si est qu’il oste toutes les enfleures desus les membres;	Because the properties of wood are such that it removes all swelling from the limbs;
et se li nodation est ja convertie en durteit ausi com piere, et il est besoing de l’oster, si la cope desus, et fent la superfluiteit apparent;	And if the knot has already turned hard like a stone, and it must be removed, then cut away the surface layer, and expose the excess.
ou tu la reis a aucun raseur, tant qu’ele soit ostee, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee.	where you return it to a rasp until it is removed, and treat it until it is healed.
dou membre qui est foibles aprés la garison	From the member which is weak after recovery.
Quant li brisure de l’os est restoree, et demoure aprés li membres foibles et subtilz, si avient por mout de causes:	When the broken bone is healed, but the limb remains weak and delicate, this occurs for many reasons:
de coi l’une est por ceu qu’il fut liiez trop estroit, et ne fut mie liiez si com il covenoit;	for which one is due to it being tied too tightly, and was not bound as it should have been;
ou por ceu qu’il i ot trop de liiens, et ne pooit venir li norrissemens au membre;	or because there were too many bindings, and nourishment could not reach the limb;
ou por multitude d’arosement;	or due to excessive bleeding;
ou por trop grans movements, ne mie en son houre;	or because of too much movement, not at the right time;
ou por ceu qu’il a poc de sanc en son cors, si est foibles.	or because they have little blood in their body, thus being weak.
Et li cure si est que tu faices mengier le malaide, et faire le cors tendre, tant que li sans soit multipliiez en lui;	And the treatment is that you should make the patient eat, and soften their body until blood is multiplied within them;
et li aministre bain, et li done joie et liesce;	and administer baths to them, giving joy and leisure;
puis met poix sus le membre, si que li poix atraie a li grant norrissement, et l’arose sovent d’aigue tede, tant que li norrissement corre au membre;	Then place lead on the limb, so that the lead draws out the great suppuration, and often irrigate it with warm water until the suppuration flows into the limb;
et reviegne a sa figure natureil.	and returns to its natural shape.
dou membre tort aprés la santeit	Of a twisted limb after injury
Quant li membres est tors aprés la restauration, et li os brisiez apert, et li forme dou membre est laide, toutevoie ne pert mie son ovraige natureil:	When the limb is twisted after restoration, and the bone is visibly broken, and its form is ugly, it still does not lose its natural function:
si ne croire mie les folz qui dient c’on doit brisier lou membre tout de noveil, et maint fol mire ont ce fait en nostre terre;	do not believe the fools who say one must break the limb anew, and many foolish doctors have done this in our land;
et cist ovraiges est blamez, et en vient grans malz, et par aventure li mors;	and these procedures are to be blamed for bringing great harm, even death;
toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k’il soient arosez d’aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;	toutevoie, se li nodations et li torture sont fres, si covient k'il soient arosez d'aigue chaude, ou herbes mollifians soient cuites, si com foilles de vismalve, et racines, et mellilote, et semblans choses;
et li fai I emplaustre mollificatif, si com dyaquilon bien fait, et tu pren le muscillaige de vismalve, et la confit avec graisse de geline ou oile de sisament, et fai emplaustre sus;	and to this wound make a softening plaster, like well-made dyaquilon ointment, and take the mucus of the mallow plant, and mix it with goose fat or sesame oil, and spread the mixture as an external application.
ou tu pren figues graisses, et les broie avec fien de colon, et semblans medicines que amenuisent le soudement.	or you take fat figs, grind them with coltsfoot leaves, and similar medicines that lessen the swelling.
Et aucune fois est ostee li nodacion por froter continuelment et longement a mains moistes.	And sometimes the nodule is removed by continually and extensively rubbing with moist hands.
Et soit amenistrez movement au membre chescune houre.	And provide gentle movement to the limb every hour.
Et se li tortuositez est enveillie et endurcie, ausi com piere, et besoins est de l’oster au fer, si la covient coper jusc’a l’os, a l’incisoire subtil legierement;	And if the tendon is hardened and knotted like stone, and it must be removed with an iron instrument, then one should cut as far down as the bone using a small delicate incision.
et mettre cusenson et estude en la cure.	and apply sutures and take care in its treatment.
Ci encomence li livres des dislocations	Here begins the book of dislocations.
Dislocations est issue d’aucune jointe de son leu, por coi il ne se puet muevre, et est li membres mal figurez, et sent li malaides grant dolor et grant lesion.	Dislocation occurs when a joint moves out of its place, which prevents it from moving, and the limb is misaligned, causing the patient great pain and injury.
Quant dislocation vient a aucun, si le covient maintenant ramener sens targier.	When dislocation occurs in someone, one must promptly reset it without delay.
Car s’on tarde, si enfle li leus, et par aventure si le remet on a poines au leu;	For if one delays, the wound swells, and sometimes it may be painfully reset into place;
por ceu ne covient mie c’on le mueve a l’oure k’il est enflez:	For this reason, it must not be moved when it is swollen.
maintes fois fait venir spame et autres dolors;	Often brings back swelling and other pains;
toutevoie, quant ce avenra, si fai sainier lou malaide, puis le laisse, tant que li apostemes chas soit apaisiez;	However, when this happens, have the patient bleed, then leave them alone until the abscess is healed;
puis arose le membre d’aigue chaude et d’oile, puis le ramoinne legierement, et cure chescun membre si com li cure venra en son leu.	Then immerse the limb in warm water and oil, then gently move it, and treat each member so that it returns to its place.
Et j’ai ordenez les chapistres des dislocations des lou chief jusc’a piez.	And I have ordered the chapters on dislocations from head to toe.
des mandibules	of jaws
Poc avient que les mandibules soient desaluees andous, et li dislocations d’ambedous est selonc II manieres:	Sometimes both jaws become dislocated and the double dislocation occurs in two ways:
ou elles sont un poc ostees de lor leus, et mollifies un poc;	in which they are slightly out of place and softened somewhat;
ou elles sont desaluees entierement, et pendent vers lou pis, et cort li salive de la bouche qu’il ne la puet tenir, ne ne puet clore sa bouche, et envoloupe sa langue avec la parole.	Where they are completely dislocated and hang downward, and saliva dribbles from the mouth which he cannot hold, nor can close his mouth, and his tongue becomes tangled in speech.
Quant li dislocations est petite, si revient par li em plusors disposicions.	When a dislocation is minor, it can often return through various adjustments.
Et s’elle est entiere et acomplie, si covient que tu la ramoinne hastanment, et ne targier mie;	And if it is complete and fully dislocated, then you must reduce it quickly, without delay.
et en tel maniere que li ministres teigne le chief dou malaide, et boute li mires som pochet de l’une de ses mains en la racine de la dislocation de la mandibule dedens la bouche, se li dislocations est de II pars;	and in such a manner that the assistant holds the patient's head, and pushes their finger from one of his hands into the root of the dislocated jaw within the mouth, if the dislocation is in two parts; 
et li autre doi des mains soient defuer, por mettre igal;	and the other finger from both hands should be outside, to keep it even.
et comande au malaide qu’il les amollisse, ses mandibules, et les mueve de toutes pars.	and instruct the patient to relax his jaws, and move them in all directions.
Et li mires la mete igal, tant qu’elle reveigne en son leu.	The practitioner then places it evenly until it returns to its proper place.
Et se li ramener est griés, meismement se ce sont les II mandibules ensamble, si les arose d’aigue chaude et d’oile, tant que les ramoinnes legierement;	And if resetting it is difficult, especially if it involves the two mandibles together, soak them in warm water and oil until they can be reset gently;
ne ne targier mie dou ramener, si com nos avons dit.	Do not delay in resetting it, as we have said.
Et quant elles sont ramenees igalment, et li bouche dou malaide clot bien sens mollifiier, si met sus drapelz moilliez en cerote fait d’oile roset et de cire, puis le lie legierement de molz liiens;	And when they are evenly reset and the patient's mouth is closed without swelling, apply wet dressings made of soft cloth in a ointment of rose oil and wax, then bind it lightly with soft bandages.
et dorme li malaides sus son dos, et ses chiés soit estans entre II cussins, si qu’il ne lou mueve ne a destre ne a senestre, ne ne s’efforce mie de maixier, mais preigne legiere viande, tant que les dolors soient ostees, et soient noees les mandibules;	Let the patient sleep on their back, with their shoulders resting between two pillows so that they cannot move them to the right or left, and let them not exert themselves by chewing, but take light food until the pain is gone, and the mandibles are healed.
et puis menjuce ce qu’il vuet legierement, et ne se travaille mie d’ovrir la bouche au mengier et au boivre, tant que li mandibule soit bien noee et sanee.	And then have him chew what he wishes lightly, and do not exert himself to open his mouth for eating or drinking until the mandible is well-numbed and healed.
Et se les II mandibules ne pueent estre remises a point a une houre, et ne sont mie converties a lor leus, si en vient fievres et sode acostumees, et par aventure solution de ventre, et par aventure vomist cole pure.	And if the two jaws cannot be reset to their original position within an hour and do not return to their proper place, fever and constant pain will result; possibly leading to diarrhea, or perhaps vomiting clear bile.
Et quant tu verras ceu, adonc saiches que c’est perdicions;	And when you see this, know that it is destruction;
et maintes fois muert cil cui il avient, en VIIII jors.	and many times the one who experiences it dies within nine days.
de la forcelle	From the fork
Li forcele ne puet desaluer dou costeit dedens la continuation de li et dou pis, et est desaluee aucune fois au defuer, et bien le sent on.	The fork cannot be dislocated from the inside of its shaft or below, and is sometimes dislocated outwards, which one can easily tell.
Et li restauration si est que li malaides gise sovin sor son dos, et estende ses bras;	And its restoration is such that the patient often lies on their back and extends their arms;
et puis presse le leu forment a ta palme, et elle revenra;	and then press the place firmly with your palm, and it will return.
puis met sus l’emplaustre et lou bendeil, et l’estraint;	then apply the plaster and bind it with bandages, holding it firmly.
et li chiez qui est devers lou coute ne puet desaluer;	and the head which is towards the knife cannot dislocate;
se poc non, et se il desalue aucune fois, si le ramoinne a son leu, si com nos avons dit;	if not, and if it dislocates at any time, then reset it to its place, as we have said;
puis met sus l’emplaustre et le bendeil, et l’estraint, et coumande au malaide qu’il se repose tant qu’il soit sanez;	then apply the plaster and bandage, hold it tight, and instruct the patient to rest until they are healed;
et ensi meisme est ramenez li chiés de l’espale, quant il est desevrez de son leu.	and likewise is the head of the shoulder reset when it is dislodged from its place.
de la dislocation de l’espaule	Of shoulder dislocation
Saiches que li espaule n’est desaluee fuer que selonc III manieres:	Know that the shoulder is dislocated only according to three ways:
de coi l’une est qu’ele desalue a la partie de l’assele au desoz;	one is that it dislocates at the back part underneath;
et li seconde est a la partie dou pis;	and the second (dislocation) is to the area of the back.
et par aventure desalue a la partie desus, et ceu avient poc;	and sometimes dislocated above this part, which rarely happens;
et ne desalue mie derrier por l’espaule, et ne desalue mie dedens por les ners;	and it does not dislocate behind the shoulder, nor inside towards the nerves;
et plusors fois desalue desoz vers l’assele, meismement a ces qui ont poc de char, car a ces saut ele fuer hastanment;	and often dislocates downwards towards the armpit, especially in those with little flesh, for to them it jumps painfully.
a ces qui ont assez char, saut ele a poines, et rentre a poines.	for those who have sufficient flesh, it jumps slightly and returns slightly.
Et par aventure avient a aucuns homes percussion ou casseure, et enfle li espaule d’un aposteme chaut, et cuide qu’elle est desaluee par ceu.	And occasionally happens to some men a blow or fracture, and the shoulder swells from a hot abscess, and they think it is dislocated because of this.
Il covient donques que tu l’esprueves, tant que tu en soies certains;	Therefore, you must test it until you are certain;
et adonques encomence la cure.	and then begin the treatment.
Et est conue li dislocations quant il est aval vers l’assele, et met difference entre l’espaule malade et la saine, et tu troveras entre lor diversiteit manifeste;	And thus is recognized dislocation when it occurs downward toward the armpit, and creates a noticeable difference between the affected shoulder and the healthy one, and you will find an obvious disparity between them.
et troveras au chief de l’espaule une fosse, et desoz l’assele au tochier le chief de l’espaule, ausi com se ce soit uns oes;	and you will find at the top of the shoulder a depression, and underneath the armpit on the other side, the head of the shoulder, as if it were an eye socket.
et ne puet li malaides ramener sa main a son neis, ne movoir de nulz movemens;	and the patient cannot bring their hand back to their nose or move any part of it.
et ausi, s’elle est desaluee en haut, si n’est mie occultee, car tu le trueves manifestement au tochier;	and also, if it is dislocated upwards, it is not hidden because you can clearly see it from the side.
et ceste maniere de dislocation n’est mie fors a ramener, quant elle est novele, ou se li enfes est malaides.	and this type of dislocation is not difficult to reset when it is recent or the patient is young.
Et li maniere est que li ministres lieve la main dou malaide en haut, puis met tes peuchas desoz l’assele, et lieve la jointure a force en haut au leu;	And the manner is that the attendants lift the patient's hand upwards, then place your palms underneath the armpit, and raise the joint forcefully upwards to its proper place;
et li ministres lieve la main, et l’estende en haut, pues le mette desoz;	and the attendants lift the hand, extend it upwards, then place it underneath;
si venra hastanment.	there will be dislocation.
Et s’elle ne vient si com nos avons dit em mains jors aprés, si covient ke li malaides soit baigniez en aigue chaude;	And if it does not come out as we have said with bare hands afterward, then the patient must be bathed in warm water;
et li amenistre arosement mollifiant et assouajant, si com decoction de altee et de fenugrec et de mellilote en aigue, et soit amenistree;	and the attendants apply softening and soothing ointments, such as a decoction of althea, fenugreek, and melilot in water, to be applied;
puis soit sovinez li malaides sus son dos, et mette on desoz l’assele un sto de lainne igal, ne trop mol ne trop dur, puis mette li mires son talon sus le sto, et lieve le chief de l’espaule vertuousement, et traie la main dou malaide;	then the patient is placed on their back, and a padded linen cushion, neither too soft nor too hard, is placed underneath the armpit. The heel of the patient's hand rests on top of the pillow, while we lift up the head of the shoulder gently, pulling the patient's arm;
et uns autres ministres teigne lou chief dou malaide, si qu’il ne se mueve aval;	and another minister holds the patient's head, so it does not move downwards.
celle espaule revient tout maintenant, et se tu vues si le ramoinne selonc ceste maniere:	this shoulder returns immediately, and if you observe as it is reset in this manner:
et est que tu faices estre present I home qui soit plus grans que li malaides;	and have another man present who is stronger than the patient;
et soit drois devers lou costeit, et boute s’espaule desoz l’assele dou malaide, et lieve l’assele en haut, si que li malaides pende en l’ar;	and he should stand upright by the patient's side, and push their shoulder underneath the patient's armpit, then lift the armpit upwards so that the patient hangs in mid-air.
et uns autres ministres traie la main dou malaide aval devers lou ventre.	another minister pulls the patient's hand downwards towards their belly.
Et se li malaides est trop legiers, si pent avec lui aucune chose pesant, et li dislocation revient maintenant.	And if the patient is too light, weigh them down with something heavy, and the dislocation will return now.
Et le ramoinne on ausi en autre maniere:	and it is also reset in another manner:
et est c’on fiche I lonc tison en terre, dont li chiés soit ausi reons com I pistal, et ne soit ne trop gros ne trop graile;	and one drives a long peg into the ground, so that the head is as high as the knee, and it should not be too thick nor too thin
puis soit mis desoz lou malaide, mais k’il ait drapelz souef sus, et li malaides soit estans dou lonc dou fust;	then it should be placed underneath the patient, but let them have soft blankets on top, and the patient should extend their body along the length of the pole;
puis soit estendue sa main aval d’autre part forment, et li jointure revenra en son leu hastanment;	then stretch out their arm from the other side, thus the joint will return to its place gradually;
et s’elle ne vuet revenir por toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si fai ceste cure:	and if it refuses to go back into place for all the things we have said, then do this treatment:
pren I tison de II bras de grant et IIII dois de large, qui ait le chief reont por mues entrer em parfont desoz l’assele, selonc ceste forme:	take a pole two arms-lengths long and four fingers wide with the head flattened so you can insert it perfectly underneath the shoulder blade according to this form:
puis lie sus le chief dou fust drapelz souez, que li fust ne blece lou malaide, puis le met desoz l’assele dou malaide;	Then place above the head of the patient a soft cloth, so that it does not wound the patient, then put it beneath the sick person's ass.
et estende som bras sus le fust dou lonc, et lie l’ajutoire sus le fust, et lou bras au chief de la main, puis met le bras sus I eschillon d’une eschiele dou large, et soit estendue li mains aval, et soit laissiez li cors pendans d’autre part:	And extend their arms over the long side of the wooden frame, and tie the injured arm to the frame, and their hand to their head. Then place the other arm on a board that is wider than them and let it hang freely down from the board, leaving the body free to dangle on the other side:
li jointure reva ens maintenant.	The joint has now recovered.
Et quant elle est ens, en quel maniere que ce soit, si covient que tu mettes desoz l’assele une spere de laine igal, puis met l’emplaustre aparilliet de poudre dou molin, avec encens et aubun d’uef, sus toute l’espaule et entor, puis l’estrain desoz l’assele avenanment, et torne le liien sus l’emplaustre, et embraice la main a son col, et soit li mains demorans ensi.	And when it is in place, however it may be, you must put under the bench an equal woolen pad, then apply a plaster prepared with flour powder, incense and egg white, over the entire shoulder and around it; then strap it underneath the bench appropriately, and turn the bandage back onto the plaster, embrace the hand to their neck, and let the hands stay thus.
Et covient qu’il menjuce poc, tant que li membres soit confortez, car il sanera plus tost;	And they should eat little for the time being until the limb is comfortable again because it will heal faster this way;
et puis menjuce plus aprés V jors ou VII, et le mueve;	Then they should eat more after five or seven days, and begin to move about.
et s’il est fermeis et il n’est mollifiez, si est sanez.	And if it is closed and not softened, then it is healed.
Et se li jointure est fuer de leu por moistor que i est venue, ou por autre cause, si covient que tu i aministres cauteres a III pertus, si com il est mis devant ou chapistre des cauteres.	And if the joint is forced out of place due to moisture that has entered it or for another reason, then you must apply cauterization to three openings, as mentioned before in the chapter on cautery.
Et se tu fais tout ceu, et il deslie aprés VII jors, et li jointure ne se tient, et ne puet lever som bras amont, adonc saiches que li nerf au chief de l’espaule sont copeit ou estendut ou amollis;	And if you do all that and it still dislocates after seven days, and the joint does not hold, and he cannot lift his arm up, then know that the nerve at the head of the shoulder is either cut, stretched or softened.
et saiches que li jointure n’iert jamais fichie en son leu.	and know that the joint will never be fixed in its place.
Li dislocation qui est devers lou pis, et les mameles, ou derrier, si est faite par impulsion, et estendement de mains, et i aministre on autre lieure;	The dislocation that is towards the armpit, breasts, or behind, is caused by a push and stretching of hands, and another place is treated.
et cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and treat until it is healed.
Et se aprés la sanation vient grietez au membre, et tardemens em movement, si use li malaides bain maintes fois, tant que celle grietez soit alegie, et reviegne a sa premiere nature.	And if after the healing process, the limb develops cracks and moves slowly, the patient should bathe frequently until these cracks are alleviated and return to their original state.
de la dislocation dou coute	Of shoulder dislocation:
Saiches que li jointure dou coute est desaluee a poinnes, et a poinnes revient;	Know that the dislocation of the neck is difficult to treat, and it often returns.
et s’est desaluee de toutes pars, et meismement devant et derrier, et li dislocations n’est mie reponue, car on la voit bien et sent bien;	and if it is dislocated from all sides, especially in front and behind, and the dislocation has not been reduced because it can be clearly seen and felt.
et desalue selonc chescune figure.	and dislocated according to each shape.
Et quant tu joins le coute malaide avec lou sain, si le pues veoir apertement.	And when you join the sick man's wound with the healthy one, you can see it clearly.
Car li jointure est chevee, et ne puet ploier lou bras, ne touchier son espaule a tout.	For the joint is dislocated, and he cannot bend his arm or reach his shoulder at all.
Et covient que tu le ramoinnes ainsois que apostemes chaus i viegne, car se apostemes chaus i venoit, si seroit grief li ramener;	And you must reset it even if an abscess forms there, because if an abscess does form, it would be difficult to reduce.
et par aventure ne puet estre ramenez dou tout en tout, meismement quant ele est au derrier;	and by chance, it cannot always be reset completely, especially when it is at the back.
si vaut pis que les autres dislocations, et est de plus grant dolor, et par aventure i vient li mors.	it is worse than other dislocations, causing greater pain, and in some cases, death may occur.
Et li restauration si est, quant elle est telz c’on la puet ramener, que tu li estendes sa main a tes II mains;	And when it is restored, once you have managed to reset it, extend their arm with your two hands;
et ses bras soit espandus, et les mains dou mire selonc le coute entor, desor et desoz, et boute la jointure a ses peuchas ensamble, ou a la racine de sa palme, tant qu’ele reviegne a son leu.	And his arms should be spread out, with the hands placed mirror-like according to the cut around, above and below, and press the knuckles together at his armpits or at the root of his palm until it returns to its place.
Et se li dislocations est au devant, si revient quant il double sa main a sa main, et fier de la racine de la palme lou coute qui est desaluez.	And if the dislocation is at the front, it occurs when one doubles over their hand to their hand, and it strains the root of the palm where it is dislocated.
Et s’il ne vuet revenir au leu, si aministre fort extension;	And if it does not want to return to its place, apply strong extension.
et est que dui ministre estendent le bras, et le teignent dui ministre, si qu’il ne se mueve a l’estension;	And since two people administering the extension hold the arm, and two people bend it so that it does not move during the extension.
puis torne le bras de chescune part, puis que tu as envoloupeit un drapeil double lonc et large;	Then turn the arm from each side and wrap it with a double-layered long and wide cloth.
et quant li mires a jointe la jointure a sa main, si l’oigne d’aucun oile por amolir la jointure, puis boute la jointure forment, tant qu’ele reviegne;	And when the surgeon joins the knuckles of the hand, grease them with some oil to soften the joints, then press the knuckle firmly until it returns.
et quant elle est au leu, si met sus emplaustre sec avec aubun d’uef, et l’estrain forment, et pent le bras au col dou malaide, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le deslie.	and when it is in place, apply a dry poultice with raw egg white on top, bind it tightly, and extend the arm to the patient's neck, leaving it there for several days before removing it.
Et se li jointure est ferme en son leu, si deslie lou liien, et le laisse;	and if the joint is firmly in place, release the bindings, and let it be.
et se tu vois que li jointure n’estrigne bien, si rencomence l’emplaustre et lou lien, et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, tant qu’il soit fermement mis;	and if you see that the joint does not hold well, then repeat the poultice and binding, leaving it so for several days until it is firmly set.
puis le deslie.	then release it.
Et se il sent grieteit aprés le ramenement de la jointe, et elle se muet, si le baigne et frote bellement, et presse tant qu’il soit assouagiez;	And if they feel soreness after the joint is reset and it moves again, then bathe and gently massage it, pressing until it is soothed.
ou tu met sus la jointure une naige de mouton grasse, puis la laisse I jor et une nuit, puis l’oste, et lou fai entrer ou bain;	where you place on the joint a layer of fatty sheep's wool, then leave it there for one day and night, remove it, and have them take a bath.
et quant il sue, se li frote la jointure tempreement, puis remet la naige sus, et puis entre ou bain;	and when they sweat, rub the joint gently, then replace the wool, and go back into the bath.
et ensi fai II fois ou III, tant qu’il soit sanez;	and do this twice or three times until it is healed.
et se tu vues, si met sus fien de vaiche moiste chaufeit avec burre, et l’estrain sus;	and if you see pus, apply moist warm cow dung mixed with butter on top of it.
si revenra a sa disposition.	it will return to its proper position.
li dislocation de la main	The dislocation of the hand
Li jointure de la main desalue, et li revenue est legiere, plus que les autres jointures.	The dislocation of the hand is light and easy to reset compared to other joints.
Toutevoie, il la covient ramener au leu hastanment, en l’oure meisme qu’ele est desaluee, ainsois que li leus soit enflez, ou qu’il i viegne aposteme chaut.	Nevertheless, it must be returned to its place immediately when dislocated, unless the area is swollen or an abscess forms there.
Et li ramenemens si est que tu mettes la main malaide sus une tauble, et estende li ministres la main, et li mires la mette igal, ensi que il mette sa paume sus l’aparance de la jointure, et la boute tant qu’elle reviegne.	And the process of resetting it is that you place the patient's hand on a table, and your assistant extends their hand, aligning it with the patient's; then they place their palm over the affected joint, pushing until it returns to its place.
Toutevoie, il covient que vos regardez s’il est bien a leu;	Nevertheless, you must ensure that it is correctly aligned.
adonc mette li malaides lou dos de sa main sus une tauble a l’estension et au ramenement.	Then have the patient place the back of their hand on a table during extension and reduction.
Et se li dislocations est au dos de la main, si mette li malaides son dos de sa main sus la tauble, et li mires mette sa main sus cele apparance de la jointure.	And if the dislocation is on the back of the hand, have the patient place the back of their hand on the table and let the assistants put their hand over the apparent joint.
S’elle revient maintenant, c’est bien.	If it returns to its place now, that is good.
Se ce non, si l’estrain d’emplaustres apaisans apostemes chaus, et lou laisse ensi sens rencomencier.	If this does not work, strain out the emollient plasters for hot abscesses, and leave it like this without starting again.
Et s’il ne le puet soffrir, et tu ne la pues mettre au leu aprés aucuns jors, si demore li jointure torte;	And if he cannot bear it, and you are unable to put it back into place after some days, the joint remains dislocated.
et ne nuist niant au malaide fuer que tant que li mains est amoillie, et ne puet estraindre aucune chose a tout:	and it does not harm the patient to leave his hand softened for as long as he cannot grasp anything at all:
adonc saiches que li nerf sont copez, ou li artere;	then know that either the nerve is severed or the artery.
si n’i a autre engien fuer que d’estraindre par cautere delez le cas, et par aventure n’i vaut autre chose.	if there is no other means but to grasp by cauterization nearby, perhaps nothing else will work.
Et quant li mains est au leu, si met sus l’emplaustre que nos avons dit, puis l’estrain et le laisse V jors, puis le deslie et laisse ensi.	And when the hand is in place, apply the plaster we mentioned earlier, then strain it and leave for five days, then release the strain and leave as is.
Et s’il ne la puet bien movoir, et il i a aucune grieteit, si la moille d’aigue chaude, et le frote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if they cannot move it properly, and there is any tear or injury, then apply a compress of warm water, and rub until it is healed.
de la dislocation des dois de la main	On the dislocation of the fingers of the hand
Aucune fois sont desaluez li doi de la main a chescune part, aucune fois au dos de la palme ou au ventre;	Sometimes the fingers of the hand become dislocated on both sides, sometimes on the back of the palm or the belly.
adonques estent le doi, et boute la dislocation a tes pouchés tant qu’il reviegne, puis sostien lou chief dou doi, et le pent vers la partie ou il est desjoins;	Then stretch the finger, and push the dislocation with your fingers until it returns, then support the head of the finger, and bend it towards the direction in which it is disjoined.
et le laisse II jors, et puis le met igal celui jor;	Leave it for two days, and then set it equal that day.
et de nut le lie, si com nos avons dit, et lou deslie de jor, et lou fai movoir, et le relie la nut;	And bind it at night as we have said, release it during the day, make it move, and rebind it at night.
et fai ce sovent, tant qu’il soit estroit, et tout ausi fai, se il est desaluez au ventre de la main, et fai si com tu as fait ci devant, tant qu’il soit sanez;	Do this frequently until it is narrow, and do the same if it is dislocated at the palm of the hand, act in the same way that you have done before until it is healed.
et tout ausi fai, quant il est desaluez d’autre part.	And do likewise when it is dislocated in any other place.
dou desaluement de l’eschinee dou dos	Of dislocation of the spine from the back
Quant l’eschinee dou dos ou dou col est desaluee, ou il en i a plusors desaluees, si n’i a point de cure, car li mors haste le malaide.	When the spine from the back or neck is dislocated, or there are multiple dislocations, there is no cure, as death quickly takes the patient.
Et li signes si est que li egestions saut fuer sens volunteit, ne ne la puet tenir, et maintes fois sont mollifiez aucun membre, ou les II cuixes ou li dui bras ou I.	And the signs are that vomiting occurs without volition, and it cannot be controlled; often some members are weakened: both thighs or both arms or one of them.
Et maintes fois se muet li eschinee a IIII pars;	And often the spine twists into four parts;
celle qui se muet au derrier si est apelee «gilbositez»:	That which is twisted behind is called "gilbositez":
li cure si est que tu rewarde se li gilbositez est venue d’enfance:	The treatment is that if the "gilbositez" comes from childhood, you should reverse it.
si n’i ait point de cure ne de sanation dou tot.	If there is no cure nor full recovery.
Et celle que vient de cheoir ou de percussions ou de semblans choses, dirent li ancien manieres de cures par grans paroles, ou il n’a mie en toutes grant profit;	And that which comes from falling or blows or similar things, the ancient methods of treatment say there is not much benefit in all of it.
mais je l’ai abregiet selonc mon entention, et ai formez estrumens en diverses manieres.	But I have abbreviated it according to my intention, and formed instruments in diverse ways.
Je dis que en la gilbositeit que vient au pis devant, nen a engien ne santeit;	I say that in the hunchback condition that arises on one side, no physician is healthy.
et ausi cele que vient droitement en II costez, et ne puet on curer fuers que celi proprement qui vient au dos, si com je dis;	And also the condition that arises evenly in two sides, and it cannot be cured except for that which properly comes to the back, as I say.
et est que li malaides soit estendus sus sa faice en I leu igal, et ait de l’estrain desoz lui, qu’il ne se blece;	And it is that the patient should be extended on their face in an equal place, and have a strain under them so they do not hurt themselves.
puis fiche I tison au chief en terre forment, et I autre as piez, et lie un liien pardesoz les asseles dou malaide, et I autre as hainches, et as genous, et as chevilles;	Then fix one iron rod in the ground firmly, and another at the feet, and tie a rope across the shoulders of the patient, and another to their hips, knees, and ankles.
et dui ministre saichent les liiens, li uns au chief et li autres as piez, parmi les II tisons;	and each assistant knows their task, one to hold the head and the other the feet, with two hot irons in between.
et soient bien fermez, li tison si com nos avons dit, et li mires mette ses paumes sus l’espinee forment, tant qu’ele reviegne.	and [make sure] they are firmly fixed, the hot irons as we have said, and the physician places his palms on the spine gently, until it returns to its place.
Et s’elle ne revient par ceste cure, si pren une tauble de III bras de lonc, et chevé desoz la paroit, et li malaides soit en costé, et boute le chief de la tauble desoz la paroit, puis met le mileu de la tauble sus l’espinee;	And if it does not return to its place with this treatment, take a board three feet long, and drive it underneath the wall, and let the patient be on their side, pressing the head of the board underneath the wall, then place the middle of the board over the spine.
et mette li mires ses piez sus l’autre chief de la tauble, et presse bien, tant qu’il reviegne au leu;	and let the physician place his feet on the other end of the board, pressing firmly until it returns to its place.
