et se tu vues, si le fai au tornet qui torne a la main.	And if you see this, make him turn to face the hand.
Et est que tu fiches II tisons au chief dou malaide d’un bras de grant, et devers les piez II autres, et ait entre chescun tison, desoure et desoz, une paume d’espaice de lonc;	And thrust two skewers into the head of the patient with one arm raised high and place two other skewers near the feet, leaving a span between each skewer above and below.
et ait en chescun tison I pertus, ou li tornet corre, et soient li tison fermement en terre, si qu’il ne se muevent;	And make one hole in each skewer where the tourniquet runs through, ensuring the skewers are firmly planted into the ground so they do not move.
et entre chescuns II tisons ait I tison tornant, sor coi li liien tornent, et ait en II tornans II petis tisons d’une paume de lonc, por torner le tornet;	And place another skewer between the two skewers turning on an axle, with two small skewers of a span in length to turn the tourniquet.
et puis lie lou lien qui est parmi les asseles au tornet devers le chief, et l’autre liien devers les piez a l’autre tornet, et chescuns des ministres torne son tornet a tout le liien, et li maistres mette l’espinee igal si com nos avons dit.	Then bind the loop which is among the axles to the tourniquet near the head and the other loop toward the feet at the other tourniquet, so each assistant turns their own axle alongside the master, who evenly applies pressure as we have said.
Et quant elle est igalz, si met sus emplaustre desiccatif avec abun d’uef, et puis les estoupes, et puis l’estele d’une tablete de III dois de lonc, que porpreigne lou leu de la gilbositeit et la partie de l’espondile sainne, puis le lie d’un liien, si com nos avons dit, et use li malaides de norrissement subtil, tant qu’il soit sanez;	And when it is even, apply a drying poultice with an abundance of eggs, then the swabs, and then a rod made from a three-day-old tablet, that reaches to the place of curvature and the healthy part of the spine, then bind it with a bandage as we have said, and let the patient use gentle nourishment until they are healed.
et s’aucune chose vient en la fin de la santez, si covient aministrer medicines amollissans et asouajans, avec l’estele que nos avons dit ci devant;	and if anything comes up in the end of the healing process, you must administer softening and soothing medicines, with the rod that we mentioned before.
et aucune fois i aministre on une piece de plonc, et aucune fois vient li apparance en la derriere spondile dou dos, et cuide on que ce soit dislocations;	and sometimes it is administered in one part of the spine, and sometimes there appears a hunch in the lower back region of the spine, which is thought to be dislocation.
et c’est li os qui apert, por coi on n’i doit mie avoir presumption:	and this is the bone which appears, therefore one must not presume to act.
par aventure feroit venir la mort.	would perhaps bring about death.
des dislocations de la hainche	Hip Dislocations
Saiches que as jointures de la hainche et as jointures de l’espaule ne vient fuers que dislocacions soulement, ne n’i vient mie si com as autres jointures;	Know that only dislocations cause pain in the hip joints and shoulder joints, not like with other joints;
et li jointure de la hainche est desaluee selonc IIII parties:	and the hip joint is dislocated according to four parts:
dedens et defuer ,et devant et derrier;	internally and externally, and in front and behind;
et plus dedens c’aillors, et poc desalue devant et derrier.	and more internally then, and sometimes dislocated both in front and behind.
Et li conoissance de sa dislocations dedens si est que quant on joint la jambe malaide avec la sainne, si est plus longe, et apert plus li malaides genous que li sains, et ne puet li malaides doubler son genoil au feu;	And the knowledge of its internal dislocation is such that when one joins the affected leg with the healthy one, it is longer, and the diseased knee appears more prominent than the healthy one, and the patient cannot bend their diseased knee to the floor.
et est li leus qui est delez enflez d’aposteme chaut, por ceu que li chiés de la cuixe vient lai.	And it is the place which is near swollen from a hot abscess, because the head of the thigh comes there.
Et li signe de celui cui il vient au defuer, si est que cist accident sont contraire a ces devant.	And the sign of him to whom it comes naturally is as follows: these accidents are contrary to those mentioned before.
Et li signes de celui cui avient au devant, si est qu’il estent bien sa jambe selonc l’acomplissement;	And the signs for someone who has this beforehand is that they stretch their leg well according to its length;
toutevoie, ne double mie le genoil sens dolor, et s’on le vuet faire aler, si ne puet avant, et retient son urine, et enfle li angre, et quant il vait, si passe sus le talon.	However, they cannot bend the knee without pain, and if one wants them to walk, they cannot beforehand, and they retain their urine, and the anus swells, and when they defecate, it passes over the heel.
Et li signes de celui cui il avient derrier, si est qu’il ne puet espandre son genoil, ne doubler, et est celle jambe plus torte de l’autre, et li angre est mollifié, et est li chiés de la cuixe au leu desoz les costes.	And the signs of one who has dislocated behind them are such that they cannot straighten their knee or bend it, and that leg is more twisted than the other, with a softened groin, and the head of the femur is in place below the ribs.
Li ramenemens de ceste semblance de dislocation si est que tu rewarde se li dislocations est anciainne, et elle demore selonc sa disposition, si n’i a nule cure;	The treatment of this similar type of dislocation is that you should reset it if the dislocation is old and remains according to its position, as there is no other treatment for it.
et n’i covient mie qu’il ait presumption.	And one must not have any presumption about it.
Et en celi dont li dislocation est fresche, et c’est des IIII manieres de dislocation, si te haste que tu tornes la jointe, et l’esten dedens et defuer, et la muef a destre et senestre;	And for the one whose dislocation is fresh, and it is of four types of dislocation, hurry to turn the joint back, stretch it both inwardly and outwardly, and move it to the right and left.
par aventure si revenra, et n’a mestier d’autre cure.	Perhaps it will return by chance, and no other treatment is needed.
Et s’il ne revient en ceste maniere, si covient que tu apareilles I ministre fort, et esten la jambe fort a II mains, ou a I liien que soit liiez sus lou genoil;	And if it does not return with this method, you must prepare a strong assistant and stretch the leg strongly with both hands or with a rope tied above the knee.
et uns autres ministres estende sa main desus en teil maniere qu’il boute ses mains desoz ses asseles, puis l’estrigne d’un souef liien sus la cuixe;	Another assistant should stretch his hand over it in such a way that he pushes his hands under the armpits and then tightens an elastic bandage around the thigh.
et uns autres tigne lou chief dou liien;	And another person holds the end of the rope.
et estendent amont et aval tuit a une fois, tant que li malaide soit levez de terre a une fois, et demoure pendans.	They extend it upstream and downstream all at once, so that the patient is lifted off the ground simultaneously, remaining suspended.
Ceste maniere d’estension si est commune as IIII semblances, et se li dislocation est revenue, si com nos avons dit, c’est bien.	This method of extension is common for four similar cases, and if the dislocation has been corrected, as we have said, it is good.
Se ceu non, si covient mettre cure a sa semblance.	If not, you must apply treatment in a similar manner.
Quant li dislocations est au pardedens, si covient que tu sovines le malaide sus son costeit sain, puis met le liien sus la racine de la cuixe, et le leu qui est desoz l’angre, puis estent le liien en haut devers l’angre, et devers la forcele;	When the dislocation is on the inside, you must lay the patient onto their healthy side, then place the bandage at the root of the thigh, and the part below the groin, stretch the bandage upwards towards the groin, and towards the loins.
puis preigne uns autres ministres ses bras, et embraice le gros leu de la cuixe malaide, et l’estende au defuer forment:	Then have other assistants take hold of his arms, embrace the thick part of the injured thigh, and extend it outward forcefully.
si revenra a son leu maintenant;	It will return to its place immediately.
et ceste maniere de dislocation est plus legiere des autres.	And this type of dislocation is lighter than the others.
Et se tu ne la pues serrer en ceste maniere que nos avons dit, si covient que tu lies les II piés dou malaide ensamble d’un fort liien souef sus les II talons, et sus les II genous, et soit li jambe malaide estendue II dois plus que li autres;	And if you cannot secure it in this manner as we have said, then you must bind the two feet of the patient together with a strong soft bandage over the heels and knees, and let the affected leg be extended twice more than the other.
puis soit pendus sus le chief d’un fust, et soit en sus de terre II bras de lonc;	Then hang it from an upright post so that it is suspended above the ground by two arms' lengths.
puis comande a I ministre qu’il embraice le chief de la cuixe, et soit uns autres ministres pendans avec le malaide, qui embraice forment la cuixe, car li jointure revient maintenant hastanment.	Then instruct one assistant to embrace the patient's thigh, and let another assistant hang with the patient, embracing the thigh firmly, for the joint will now return swiftly.
Et quant li dislocations est au defuer, si gise li malaides, si com nos avons dit en celui qui a gilbositeit, et estraigne I liien sus la jambe malaide proprement, et sus le peis ausi;	And when the dislocation is external, let the patient lie down as we have said for one with curvature of the spine, and secure the bandage firmly around the affected leg and also the foot.
puis met II tisons, I au chief et I autre as piez, puis fiche I tison entre les cuixes au malaide emmi la forme;	Then place two irons [heated in a fire], one on the head and another at the feet, then insert an iron between the thighs of the patient in the middle of the table.
et ait plantei de drapelz moistes entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide, puis estende chescuns ministre devers lui, et li mires mette igal a sa main la dislocation.	Surround it with wet cloths so that it does not burn the patient, then stretch each attendant towards him and let the surgeon align his hand to match [the alignment of] the dislocation.
S’elle revient, c’est boin.	If it returns, it's good.
Se ce non, met sus .ie. table, et le presse ensi com nos avons dit en la gilbositeit, et gise li malaides sus le sain costeit.	If not, place it on a flat surface, i.e., a table, and press it as we have described for the treatment of clubfoot, and lay the patient on their healthy side.
Et quant li dislocations est devant, si covient estendre la jambe malaide hastanment, et selonc ce que j’ai dit;	And when the dislocation is in front, it's necessary to stretch out the sick leg as far as possible [to achieve a successful reduction of the joint], and according to what I have said [previously];
et mette li mires sa paine d’estre sus l’angre malaide, puis presse a l’autre main, et l’estent aval devers lou genoil.	And let the surgeon position himself on top of the affected limb [to help reduce it], then press with one hand and stretch downwards towards the knee.
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches;	And if the dislocation is external, you should not stretch the patient downwards nor lift them up from the ground. Instead, they should be positioned as if their hip joint was also externally dislocated, just as we have mentioned regarding the position for a double hip dislocation.
et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table;	Let them lie on their face, with the ropes extended as we have mentioned previously, and one must press on the joint using a board.
et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz;	This will be sufficient when the patient stretches out their legs, ensuring they remain level.
adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve;	Adjust the thighs and apply a plaster, securing it with a tight bandage so that the hip joint does not move.
et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus;	Allow them to rest for three or four days, then remove the bandage and reapply the plaster on top of it.
et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors;	And if you see that they are even, pinch them, as before, and leave it for three days.
puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	Then untie it, and make him move gently, until the limb is strengthened.
de la dislocation dou genoil	Of the dislocation of the knee
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres:	The knee is dislocated in three ways:
c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier;	That is to say, internally and externally, and behind;
et ne desalue point devant.	And it does not dislocate in front.
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez;	And the sign is that you ask the patient to bend their leg towards their thigh, and if it does not reach their thigh, then know that they are dislocated.
et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez;	And the restoration for all of these is that you make the patient sit upright, and stretch their leg if they can, and place your back on their face, and put their foot on your feet.
puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment;	Then take his knee on your palms, and draw it between your two hands, then bend the two sides of the knee sharply.
et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement;	And have another minister stretch out his foot so that the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that he lightly shakes his leg against his thigh.
et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie;	And apply the plaster over it, and have him lift his leg against his thigh, and keep them bound tightly together for three or four days, then release it.
et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And the patient must not exert himself by walking until his limb is comfortable.
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not broken, apply strong traction as we have mentioned in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed.
de la dislocation dou talon	Of the dislocation of the heel,
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The heels are sometimes bruised, and sometimes completely dislocated, both internally and externally.
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee:	And the sign of this is that the ankle is swollen, and more so on the part where it was dislocated.
li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	The re-alignment is light, and one must gently extend it with their hands when it is only slightly moved.
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville;	And when it is completely dislocated, you must make the patient sit upright and have an assistant hold them from behind by the leg above the ankle.
puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut;	Then pull the foot towards you with your right hand, then do it twice with your left, and extend upwards while gently pushing the foot up.
et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet;	And do this twice, as we have said, by pushing and pulling the foot.
s’elle revient, c’est bien;	If it stays in place, that's good.
se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient;	But if not, start the process again as it will return.
et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	and if it cannot be returned in this way, then make the patient lay on their back on the ground, and firmly insert a pole into the earth between their thighs, tie the cloth around it so that it does not hurt the patient.
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	then have the minister hold the thigh, and another minister extend the leg to their hands or tie it with a cord around the foot so that they bind it above the ankle.
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	then each minister should extend equally, and the pole should be close between the patient's thighs to hold them when they are being extended.
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	then place the mirrors equally on the dislocation with their hands, and another minister should hold the healthy leg below, and the dislocation will return swiftly.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	And when it is ready, apply the plaster and bandages on top, applying firm pressure, tie the foot to the leg, and protect the nerves behind the ankle, ensuring the bindings are not too tight.
puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain;	Then leave it for two or three days, and if the binding loosens, apply pressure again.
puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors;	Then remove the bindings on the third or fourth day, and prevent the patient from walking for four days.
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And if they walk before this period is over, it is not guaranteed that the dislocation will not happen again.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If pus forms in the abscess, you must soothe it as we have said elsewhere until it is healed.
des dois	twice
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the shoulder is dislocated, it should be gently stretched without strain, which is a simple matter.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	And if the dislocation is in any knuckle of the foot or ankle, you must make the patient sit on a flat surface or lie straight on a table, and place your foot on top of their affected joint, then press firmly with your foot until it returns to its proper position.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie;	and when it is even, and nothing appears, place beneath the sole of the foot a two-foot plank, then strain it firmly, and leave for three days, then release it.
et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	and have them rest until they are healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	For wounds and dislocations together, you must first prepare the cautery of fire and use coals or stones to burn them red-hot; then take wax, pitch, rosin, fat, and oil, mixing all five substances. Take two small pieces of cloth, rub them with hog lard, spread the mixture on one side, and place it where you see that there is a dislocation. Let him rest for some time until the swelling goes down; then take some fine linen, soak it in water, and bind around his limb from the head to the foot of the member. Leave it bound tightly and let him sit still like this until the wound heals completely, or nearly so, if necessary.
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	When a wound accompanies the dislocation, and one wishes to restore it, often the patient dies:
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	do not be overly confident in your treatment if you are not wise in the art and have not practiced it for a long time, and if you are not compassionate, merciful, and careful, do not be bold.
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	and apply soothing, abscess-reducing poultices at the beginning, and leave the patient in God's hands if you see no hope of recovery.
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and when you see hope, then relocate the limb now, even if the abscess there gets hot;
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	and when the limb is back in place, administer soothing things for the hot abscess, and treat the wound as it should be done, with drying ointments;
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	and if with the dislocation there is a break, and small bones are separated, remove them, and do what we have said for simple illnesses;
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	and beware of entering into a state of fear, as I have said, for it is according to your Creator's will, and for the safety of your soul and body.
